cchandāṃsi vā abhibhūtayas tair evainān abhibhavaty ubhe bṛhadrathantare kārye
yatra vā indrasya harī tad indraḥ. indrasya vai harī bṛhadrathantare yad ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavataḥ pūrva evendrasya harī ārabhante
tair aśravase kārye
turaśravasaś ca vai pārāvatānāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata ete turaśravāḥ sāmanī apaśyat tābhyām asmā indraḥ śalmalināṃ yamunāyā havyaṃ nirāvahat yat tair aśravase bhavato havyam evaiṣāṃv vṛṅkte
pūrve 'bhiṣuṇuyuḥ
yā vai pūrvāḥ prasnānti tāḥ pūrvās tīrthaṃ jayanti pūrva evendram ārabhante
vihavyaṃ śasyam
jamadagneś ca vā ṛṣīṇāṃ ca somau saṃsutāv āstāṃ tata etaj gamadagnir vihavyam apaśyat tam indra upāvartata yad vihavyaṃ hotā śaṃsatīndram evaiṣāṃv vṛṅkte
yadītaro 'gniṣṭomaḥ syād ukthaḥ kāryo yady uktho 'tirātro yo vai bhūyān yajñakratuḥ sa indrasya priyo bhūyasaivaiṣāṃ yajnakratunendraṃv vṛṅkte
atho khalv āhur duṣprāpa iva vai paraḥ panthā yam evāgre yajñakratum ārabheta tasmān neyād iti
sajanīyaṃ śasyam agastyasya kayāśubhīyaṃ śasyam
asyā amuṣyā adyaśvān mithunād ahorātrābhyām evainān nirbhajati
yadi somam akrītam apahareyur anyaḥ kretavyaḥ
yadi krītaṃ yo 'nyo 'bhyāśaṃ syāt sa āhṛtyaḥ somavikrayaṇe tu kiṃ cid dadyāt
yadi somaṃ na vindeyuḥ pūtīkān abhiṣuṇuyur yadi na pūtīkān arjjunāni
gāyatrī somam āharat tasyā anu visṛjya somarakṣiḥ parṇam acchinat tasya yo 'ṃśuḥ parāpatat sa pūtīko 'bhavat tasmin devā ūtim avindann ūtīko vā eṣa yat pūtīkān abhiṣuṇvanty ūtim evāsmai vindanti
pratidhuk ca prātaḥ pūtīkāś ca śṛtaṃ ca madhyandine pūtīkāś ca dadhi cāparāhṇe pūtīkāś ca
somapītho vā etasmād apakrāmatīty āhur yasya somam apaharantīti sa oṣadhīś ca paśūṃś ca praviśati tam oṣadhibhyaś ca paśubhyaś cāvarundhe
indro vṛtram ahaṃs tasya yo nastaḥ somaḥ samadhāvat tāni babhrutūlāny arjunāni yo vapāyā utkhinnāyās tāni lohitatūlāni yāni babhrutūlāny arjunāni tāny abhiṣuṇuyād etad vai brahmaṇo rūpaṃ sākṣād eva somam abhiṣuṇoti
śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma kāryaṃ sad evainaṃ karoti
yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭubhi prohed vācaivainaṃ samardhayati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryam indriyasya vīryasya parigṛhītyai
pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥ
pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñas tam evārabhate
avabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣeta
tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syāt
yadi kalaśo dīryeta vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ brahmasāma kuryāt
avaṣaṭkṛto vā etasya somaḥ parāsicyate yasya kalaśo dīryate yad vaṣaṭkāraṇīdhanaṃ brahmasāma bhavati vaṣaṭkṛta evāsya somo bhavati
vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ samane bahūnām ity etāsu kāryam
eṣa hi bahūnāṃ samane dīryate yat kalaśaḥ
tad āhur na vā ārtyārtir anūdyārtyā vā eṣa ārtim anuvadati yaḥ kalaśo dīrṇe dadrāṇavatīṣu karotīti
śrāyantīyam eva kāryam
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricāno 'manyata sa etac chrāyantīyam apaśyat tenātmānaṃ samaśrīṇāt prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa
dugdha iva eṣa riricāno yasya kalaśo dīryate yac chrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati punar evātmānaṃ saṃśrīṇāti prajayā paśubhir indriyeṇa
yadi śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma syād vaiṣṇavīṣv anuṣṭupsu vaṣaṭkāraṇidhanaṃ kuryāt
yad vai yajñasya sravati vācaṃ pratisravati vāg anuṣṭup yajño viṣṇur vācaiva yajñasya cchidram apidadhāti
yad vai yajñasya sravaty antataḥ sravati vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ yajñasyaiva cchidraṃ vārayate
yadi prātassavanāt somo 'tiricyeta asti somo ayaṃ suta iti marutvatīṣu gāyatreṣu stuyuḥ
mādhyandinaṃ vā eṣa savanaṃ nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yaḥ prātassavanād atiricyate tasmān marutvatīṣu stuvanti marutvad dhi mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ tasmād u gāyatrīṣu gāyatraṃ hi prātassavanam
yasmāt stomād atiricyate sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāya
aindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsati
vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe pratitiṣṭhati
yadi mādhyandināt savanād atiricyeta baṇ mahāṃ asi sūryety ādityavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥ
tṛtīyasavanaṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo mādhyandināt savanād atiricyate tasmād ādityavatīṣu stuvanty ādityaṃ hi tṛtīyasavanaṃ tasmād u bṛhatīṣu bārhataṃ hi mādhyandinaṃ savanam
yasmāt stomād atiricyeta sa eva stomaḥ kāryaḥ salomatvāyaindrāvaiṣṇavaṃ hotānuśaṃsati vīryaṃ vā indro yajño viṣṇur vīrya eva yajñe pratitiṣṭhati
yadi tṛtīyasavanād atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu gaurīvitena stuyuḥ
yajño vai viṣṇuś śipiviṣṭo yajña eva viṣṇau pratitiṣṭhaty atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhāti
etad anyat kuryur ukthāni praṇayeyur ukthāni vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo 'gniṣṭomād atiricyate yady ukthyebhyo 'tiricyetātirātraḥ kāryo rātriṃ vā eṣa nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate ya ukthyebhyo 'tiricyate yadi rātrer atiricyeta viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu bṛhatā stuyur eṣu tu vā atiricyata ity āhur yo rātrer atiricyata iti
amuṃ vā eṣa lokaṃ nikāmayamāno 'bhyatiricyate yo rātrer atiricyate bṛhatā stuvanti bṛhad amuṃ lokam āptum arhati tam evāpnoti
yadi dīkṣitānāṃ pramīyate dagdhvāsthīny upanahya yo nediṣṭhī syāt taṃ dīkṣayitvā saha yajeran
etad anyat kuryur abhiṣutyānyat somam agṛhītvā grahān yāsau dakṣiṇā sraktis tad vā stuyur mārjālīye vā
api vā etasya yajñe yo dīkṣitaḥ pramīyate tam etena niravadayante
yāmena stuvanti yamalokam evainaṃ gamayanti
tisṛbhiḥ stuvanti tṛtīye hi loke pitaraḥ
parācībhiḥ stuvanti parāṅ hīto 'sau lokaḥ
sarparājñyā ṛgbhiḥ stuvanti
arbudaḥ sarpa etābhir mṛtāṃ tvacam apāhata mṛtām evaitābhis tvacam apaghnate
tā ṛco 'nubruvantas trir mārjālīyaṃ pariyanti savyān ūrūn āghnānāḥ
stutam anuśaṃsaty amuṣminn evainaṃ loke nidhnuvanti
yanti vā ete patha ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīty aindravāyavāgrān grahān gṛhṇate punaḥ panthānam apiyanti
agna āyūṃṣi pavasa iti pratipatkāryā ya eva jīvanti teṣv āyur dadhāti
saṃvatsare 'sthīni yājayeyuḥ saṃvvatsaro vai sarvasya śāntir yat purā saṃvvatsarād yājayeyur vācam aruṣkṛtāṃ krūrām ṛccheyuḥ
vṛtaḥ pavamānāḥ syuḥ saptadaśam itarat sarvam
yat trivṛtaḥ pavamānā bhavanti prāṇā vai trivṛt prāṇān evopayanti yat saptadaśam itarat sarvaṃ prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajatim evopayanti
prāṇāpānair vā ete vyṛdhyanta ity āhur ye mṛtāya kurvantīti maitrāvaruṇāgrān grahān gṛhṇate prāṇāpānau mitrāvaruṇau prāṇāpānair eva samṛdhyante
yasya kalaśa upadasyati kalaśam evāsyopadasyantaṃ prāṇo 'nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥ
tad āhuḥ payo 'vanayed iti
atho khalv āhur antarhitam iva vā etad yat payo hiraṇyam evāpo'bhyavanayed dhiraṇyam abhyunnayed iti
prāṇā vā āpo 'mṛtaṃ hiraṇyam amṛta evāsya prāṇān dadhāti sa sarvam āyur eti
yasya nārāśaṃsa upavāyati nārāśaṃsam evāsyopa+vāyantaṃ prāṇo 'nūpadasyati prāṇo hi somaḥ
yam adhvaryur antato grahaṃ gṛhṇīyāt tasyāptum avanayet
prāyaścityai vai graho gṛhyate prāyaścityevāsmai prāyaścittiṃ karoti
yadi pītāpītau somau saṃgaccheyātām antaḥ paridhyaṅgārān nirvartya juhuyāt hutasya cāhutasya cāhutasya hutasya ca / pītāpītasya somasyendrāgnī pibataṃ sutaṃ svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
prajāpataye svāhety abhakṣaṇīyasya juhuyād uttarārdhyapūrvārdhya uparavaḥ
indur indum avāgād ity avavṛṣṭasya bhakṣayet
tasya ta indrav indrapītasyendriyāvatas sarvagaṇasya sarvagaṇa upahūta upahūtasya bhakṣayāmi
hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgra ity ājyenābhyupākṛtasya juhuyād agnīdhraṃ paretya bhūtānāṃ jātaḥ patir eka āsīt sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ dyām utemāṃ tasmai ta indo haviṣā vidhema svāheti saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
yadi grāvāpi śīryate paśubhir yajamāno vyṛdhyate paśavo vai grāvāṇo dyutānasya mārutasya sāmnā stuyuḥ
mārutā vai grāvāṇaḥ svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
yadi somam abhidahed grahān adhvaryuḥ spāśayeta stotrāṇy udgātā śastrāṇi hotātha yathāpūrvaṃ yajñena careyuḥ pañca dakṣiṇā deyāḥ pāṅkto yajño yāvān yajñas tam ārabhate 'vabhṛthād udetya punar dīkṣate tatra tad dadyād yad dāsyaṃ syāt purā dvādaśyā dīkṣeta yad dvādaśīm atinayed antardhīyeta
yadi mahāvīro bhidyeta taṃ bhinnam abhimṛśed ya ṛte cid abhiśriṣaḥ purā jatrubhya ātṛdaḥ / saṃdhātā saṃdhiṃ maghavā purūvasur niṣkartā vihrutaṃ punaḥ mā bhema niṣṭyā ivendra tvad araṇā iva / vanāni na prajahitāny adrivo duroṣāso amanmahi / amanmahīd anāśavo 'nugrābhaś ca vṛtrahan / sakṛt sute mahatā śūra rādhasānu stomaṃ mademahīti mahāvīraṃ bhinnam abhimṛśet saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
asuryaṃ vā etasmād varṇaṃ kṛtvā teja indriyaṃ vīryam annādyaṃ prajāḥ paśavo 'pakrāmanti yasya yūpo virohati sa īśvaraḥ pāpīyān bhavitoḥ
tvāṣṭraṃ paśuṃ bahurūpam ālabheta tvaṣṭā vai paśūnāṃ rūpāṇāṃ vikartā tam eva tad upadhāvati sa enaṃ tejaseindriyeṇa vīryeṇānnādyena prajayā paśubhiḥ punas samardhayati saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
agninā pṛthivyauṣadhibhis tenāyaṃ lokas trivṛd vāyunāntarikṣeṇa vayobhis tenaiṣa lokās trivṛd yo 'yam antar ādityena divā nakṣatrais tenāsau lokas trivṛd etad eva trivṛta āyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
tam u pratiṣṭhetyāhus trivṛd dhy evaiṣu lokeṣu pratiṣṭhitaḥ
ardhamāsa eva pañcadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
taṃ caujo balam ity āhur ardhamāsaśo hi prajāḥ paśava ojo balaṃ puṣyanti
saṃvatsara eva saptadaśasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcadartava etad eva saptadaśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
tam u prajāpatir ity āhuḥ saṃvatsaraṃ hi prajāḥ paśavo 'nuprajāyante
āditya evaikaviṃsasyāyatanaṃ dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcavartas traya ime lokā asāv āditya ekaviṃśa etad evaikaviṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
tam u devatalpa ity āhuḥ pra devatalpam āpnoti ya evaṃv veda
trivṛd eva triṇavasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
tam u puṣṭir ity āhus trivṛd dhy evaiṣa puṣṭaḥ
devatā eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanaṃ trayastriṃśad devatāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśa etad eva trayastriṃśasyāyatanam eṣāsya bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
tam u nāka ity āhur na hi prajāpatiḥ kasmai canākam
chandāṃsy eva chandomānām āyatanam eṣaiṣāṃ bandhutā
āyatanavān bandhumān bhavati ya evaṃv veda
tān u puṣṭir ity āhuḥ paśavo hi chandomāḥ
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata so 'tāmyat tasmai vāj jyotir udagṛhṇāt so 'bravīt ko me 'yaṃ jyotir udagṛhṇād iti svaiva te vāg ity abravīt tām abravīd virājaṃ tvā cchandasāṃ jyotiṣkṛtvā yajāntā iti
tasmād yo virājaṃ stomaṃ saṃpadyate taṃ jyotiṣṭomo 'gniṣṭoma ity ācakṣate virāḍ ḍhi chandasāṃ jyotiḥ
jyotiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃv veda
anuṣṭup ca vai saptadaśaś ca samabhavatāṃ sānuṣṭup caturuttarāṇi chandāṃsy asṛjata ṣaḍuttarān stomān saptadaśas tāv etān madhyataḥ prājanayatām
trivṛc ca triṇavaś ca rāthantarau tāv ajaś cāśvaś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau rāthantaraṃ prācīnaṃ pradhūnutaḥ
pañcadaśaś caikaviṃśaś ca bārhatau tau gauś cāviś cānvasṛjyetāṃ tasmāt tau bārhataṃ prācīnaṃ bhāskurutaḥ
evaṃ vai vidvāṃsam āhur api grāmyāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ vāca ājānāti
prajāpatir akāmayata bahu syāṃ prajāyeyeti sa ātmann ṛtvyam apaśyat tata ṛtvijo 'sṛjata yad ṛtvyād asṛjata tad ṛtvijām ṛtviktvaṃ tair etaṃ dvādaśāham upāsīdat so 'rādhnot
pitā no 'rātsīd iti māsā upāsīdaṃs te dīkṣayaivārādhnuvann upasatsu trayodaśam adīkṣayan so ' nuvyam abhavat tasmād upasatsu didīkṣāṇo 'nuvyaṃ bhavaty eva ca hi trayodaśaṃ māsaṃ cakṣate naiva ca
eko dīkṣetaiko hi prajāpatir arādhnod dvādaśa dīkṣeran dvādaśa hi māsā arādhnuvaṃś caturviṃśatir dīkṣeraṃś caturviṃśatir hy ardhamāsā arādhnuvan
yadi pañcadaśo dīkṣeteme pañceme pañceme pañceme pañceme catvāro 'sāv eka iti nirdiśeyur yasmā arāddhikāmāḥ syus tam evārāddhir anveti sarva itare rādhnuvanti
yo vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiṃ vedāśnute gārhapataṃ pra gārhapatam āpnoti
saṃvatsaro vai devānāṃ gṛhapatiḥ sa eva prajāpatis tasya māsā eva saha dīkṣiṇaḥ
vindate saha dīkṣiṇo 'śnute gārhapatyaṃ pra gārhapatyaṃ āpnoti ya evaṃv veda /
yo vai chandasāṃ svarājaṃ vedāśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ āpnoti bṛhatī vāva chandasāṃ svarāḍ aśnute svārājyaṃ pra svārājyaṃ āpnoti ya evaṃv veda
tām etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ dvādaśa dīkṣā svādaśopasado dvādaśa prasutaḥ ṣaṭriṃśad etā rātrayo bhavanti ṣaṭtriṃśadakṣarā bṛhatī
jāyate vāva dīkṣayā punīta upasadbhir devalokam eva sutyayāpyeti
etāvad vāva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ yad etā rātrayo dvādaśa pūṛnamāsyo dvādaśaikaṣṭakā dvādaśāmāvāsyā yāvad eva saṃvatsara indriyaṃ vīryaṃ tad etenāptvāvarundhe dvādaśāhena
triṃśadakṣarā vā eṣā virāḍ ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtuṣv eva virājā pratitiṣṭhaty ṛtubhir virāji
dvātriṃśadakṣarā vā eṣānuṣṭub vāg anuṣṭup catuṣpādaḥ paśavo vācā paśūn dādhāra tasmād vācā siddhā vācāhūtā āyanti tasmād u nāma jānate
bhūtaṃ pūrvo 'tirātro bhaviṣyad uttaraḥ pṛthivī pūrvo 'tirātro dyaur uttaro 'gniḥ pūrvo 'tirātra āditya uttaraḥ prāṇaḥ pūrvo 'tirātra udāna uttaraḥ
cakṣuṣī atirātrau kanīnike agniṣṭomau yasmād antarā agniṣṭomāv atirātrābhyāṃ tasmād antare satyau kanīnike bhuṅktaḥ
saṃvatsarasya vā etau daṃṣṭrau yad atirātrau tayor na svaptavyaṃ saṃvatsarasya daṃṣṭrayor ātmānaṃ ned apidadhānīti
tad āhuḥ ko 'svaptum arhati yad vāva prāṇo +jāgāra tad eva jāgaritam iti
gāyatrīṃ vā etāṃ jyotiḥpakṣām āsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāham aṣṭau madhya ukthā agniṣṭomāv abhito māsā svargṃ lokam etyājarasaṃ brahmādyam annam atti dīpyamānaḥ
triṣpurastād rathantaraṃ upayanti tryāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ tanvate
jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yat triṣpurastād rathantaram upayantīti saubharam ukthānāṃ brahmasāma bhavati tenaiva tad ajāmi
pratnavatyaḥ prāyaṇīyasyāhnaḥ pratipado bhavanti teno eva tad ajāmi
trir vevopariṣṭād rathantaram upayanti trāvṛd vai vāk sarvām eva vācam avarudhya sarvam annādyaṃ dvādaśāhād uttiṣṭhanti
trayo vā ete trirātrā yad eṣa dvādaśāho gāytramukhaḥ prathamo gāyatramadhyo dvitīyo gāyatrottamas tṛtīyaḥ
yasmād gāyatramukhaḥ prathamas tasmād ūrdhvo 'gnir dīdāya yasmād gāyatramadhyo dvitīyas tasmāt tiryaṅ vāyuḥ pavate
tejasā vā ete prayanti tejo madhye dadhati tejo 'bhyudyanti jyotiṣā vā ete prayanti jyotir madhye dadhati jyotir abhyudyanti cakṣuṣā vā ete prayanti cakṣur madhye dadhati cakṣur abhyudyanti prāṇena vā ete prayanti prāṇaṃ madhye dadhati prāṇam abhyudyanti ye gāyatryā prayanti gāyatrīṃ madhye dadhati gāyatrim abhyudyanti
tantraṃ vā etad vitāyate yad eṣa dvādaśāhas tasyetair mayūkhā yad gāyatry asaṃvyāthāya
girikṣidauccāmanyaveti hovācābhipratārī kākṣaseniḥ kathaṃ dvādaśāha iti yathārān nemiḥ paryety evam enaṃ gāyatrī paryeti avisraṃsāya yathārā nābhau dhṛtā evam asyāṃ dvādaśāho dhṛtaḥ
anuṣṭubhaṃ vā etām annādyāya vyāvṛjyāsate yad etaṃ dvādaśāham
aṣṭābhir vā akṣair anuṣṭup prathamaṃ dvādaśāhasyāhar duyacchaty ekādaśabhir dvitīyaṃ dvādaśābhis tṛtīyam
akṣaraṃ tryakṣaram ucchiṣyate tad evottaraṃ trirātram anuvidadhāti
chandāṃsy evāsyās tṛtīyaṃ trirātraṃ vahanti
tāṃ vā etāṃ pratīcīṃ tiraścīṃ parācīm āsate 'nnādyāya tasmāt pratyañcaṃ tiryañcaṃ parāñcaṃ prajāḥ paśum upajīvanti
chandāṃsi vā anyo'nyasya lokam abhadhyāyan gāyatrī triṣṭubhas triṣṭub jagatyā jagatī gāyatryās tāni vyauhan yathālokaṃ tato vai tāni yaṃ-yaṃ kāmam akāmayanta tam asanvan
yatkāmo vyūḍhacchandasā dvadaśāhena yajate so 'smai kāmaḥ samṛdhyate
oko vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho yatho vai manuṣyā imaṃ lokam āviṣṭā evaṃ devatā dvādaśāham āviṣṭā devatā ha vā etena yajate ya evaṃv vidvān dvādaśāhena yajate
gṛhā vai devānāṃ dvādaśāho nāgṛhatāyā bhayyam
yo vai dvādaśāham agniṣṭomena kalpamānaṃ veda kalpate 'smai prātaḥsavanenaiva prathamas trirātraḥ kalpate mādhyandinena dvitīyas tṛtīyasavanena tṛtīyo 'gniṣṭomasāmnaiva daśamam ahaḥ kalpate
kalpate 'smai ya evaṃv veda
eti prety āśumad vītimad rukmat tejasvad yuñjānaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpaṃ trivṛtaḥ stomasya gāyatrasya chandaso rathantarasya sāmnaḥ
vṛṣavad vṛtravad rayimad viśvavad upasthitaṃ dvitīyasyāhno rūpaṃ pañcadaśasya stomasya traiṣṭubhasya chandaso bṛhataḥ sāmnaḥ
udvat trivad digvat gomaṭ ṭaṣabhavat tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ saptadaśasya stomasya jāgatasya chandaso vairūpasya sāmnaḥ
rājanvaj janavadvat sūryavad virāḍanutodavac caturthasyāhno rūpam ekaviṃśasya stomasyānuṣṭubhasya chandaso rājasya vai sāmnaḥ
citravac chiśumat paṅktiḥ śakvarī dyūnākṣarā gomad ṛṣabhavad vajryabhimat pañcamasyāhno rūpaṃ triṇavasya stomasya pāṅktena chandaso śakvarīṇāṃ sāmnaḥ
parivat prativat saptapadā dvipadā vinārāśaṃsā gomad ṛṣabhavat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ trayastriṃśasya stomasya sarveṣāṃ chandasāṃ rūpaṃ revatīnāṃ sāmnaḥ
yasmād eṣā samānā satī ṣaḍahavibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād virūpaḥ saṃvvatsaraḥ
virūpam enam anuprajāyate ya evaṃv veda
agna iti prathamasyāhno rūpam agnivibhakter agnim iti dvitīyasyāgnineti tṛtīyasyāgnir iti caturthasya
devā vai śriyam aicchaṃs tān na prathame 'hany avindan na dvitīye na tṛtīye tāñ caturthe 'hany avindan vindate śriyaṃ ya evaṃ vedāgner iti pañcamasya teno śrīḥ pratyupoditety āhuḥ
aprativādy enaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
agna iti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti
yasmād eṣā samānā saty agnivbhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartv ādityas tapati
indreti prathamasyāhno rūpam indravibhakter indram iti dvitīyasyendreṇeti tṛtīyasyendra iti caturthasyendrād iti pañcamasyendreti ṣaṣṭhasya yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti yasmād eṣā samānā satīndravibhaktir nānārūpā tasmād yathartv oṣadhayaḥ pacyante
yad ṛcā prastauti tat prathamasyāhno rūpam svaravibhakter yat purastāt stobhaṃ tad dvitīyasya yad ubhayataḥ stobhaṃ tat tṛtīyasya yad anutunnaṃ tac caturthasya yad abhyārabdhaṃ tat pañcamasya yad ihakāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam
svarāṇāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī svaravibhaktir nnānārūpā tasmād yathartu vāyuḥ pavate
padanidhanaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam nidhanavibhakter bahirṇidhanaṃ dvitīyasya niṃnidhanaṃ tṛtīyasyenidhanañ caturthasyāthakāraṇidhanaṃ pañcamasya yad ihākāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satī nidhanavibhaktir nnānārūpā tasmād ime lokāḥ saha santo nānaiva
dravadiḍaṃ prathamasyāhno rūpam iḍāvibhakter ūrdhveḍaṃ dvitīyasya pariṣṭubdheḍaṃ tṛtīyasyeḍābhir aiḍaṃ caturthasyādhyardheḍaṃ pañcamasya yad ihākāreṇābhyastaṃ tat ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpam iḍānāṃ yasmād eṣā samānā satīḍāvibhaktir nnānārūpā tasmāt samānāḥ santaḥ paśavo nānārūpāḥ
bharadvājāyanā vai sattram āsata tān apṛcchan kiṃ prathamenāhnā kuruteti praivaimeti kiṃ dvitīyenety avasam evākurmahīti kiṃ tṛtīyeneti pary evāplavāmahīti kiṃ caturtheneti sataiva sad apyadadhmeti kiṃ pañcameneti prāṇān eva vicchindanta aimeti kiṃ ṣaṣṭhenetīdam evāgacchāmeti iti
yasya padena prastauty atha svāram abhi vāva tena devāḥ paśūn apaśyan yat purastāt stobhaṃ atha svāram ud eva tenāsṛjanata yad ubhayataḥ stobham atha svāram ebhya eva tena lokebhyo devāḥ paśubhyo 'nnādyaṃ prāyacchan yad anutunnam atha svāram upaiva tenāśikṣan yasya madhye nidhanam atha svāraṃ garbhāṃs tenādadhata tāni havatāsvāreṇa prājanayan
imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ padanidhanenābhy ajayann amuṃ bahirṇidhanenāntarikṣaṃ diṅnidhanenāmṛtatvam īnidhanenāgacchan brahmavarcasam athanidhanenāvārundhatāsminn eva loka ihanidhanena pratyatiṣṭhan
imaṃ vāva devā lokaṃ dravadiḍenābhy ajayann amum ūrdhveḍenāntarikṣaṃ pariṣṭubdheḍena pratiṣṭhām iḍābhir aiḍenāvārundhata pratiṣṭhāyādhyardheḍena vyajayantāsminn eva loka iheḍena pratyatiṣṭhan
na vāk saṃvatsaram ativadatīḍaiva saṃvatsaram ativadati garbheṇa saṃvatsare paryāvṛtya prajāyete tenātivadati
tā vā etāś catasraḥ ṣaḍahaṃ parācya iḍā atiyanty eṣā nūtaiṣā viṣūcy eṣā pratīcy etad vīḍam
saṃvatsaro 'gnir vāk samvatsaro yad agnir vibhajyate vācam eva tad vibhajanti
dve dve akṣare vibhajanti dvau dvau hi māsāv ṛturatho māsānām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
ṣaḍ ahāni vibhajanti ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyā ṛtūnāṃ pratiṣṭhityā atho ṛtūnām eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate ṣaḍ u puruṣā yān agnir anuvihriyate
yad idaṃ bahudhāgnir vihriyate tad asāv ādityaḥ sarvāḥ prajāḥ pratyaṅ tasmād ete devate vibhaktim ānaśāte nāto 'nyā kā cana
stomo yujyate sattriyebhyo ' harbhyaḥ pratnavatībhiś copavatībhiś ca
yat pratnavatyo upavatībhyaḥ pūrvā yujyante brahma tat pūrvaṃ kṣatrād yujyate brahma hi pūrvaṃ kṣatram
manas tat pūrvaṃ vāco yujyate mano hi yad dhi manasābhigacchati tad vācā vadati
bṛhat tat pūrvaṃ rathantarād yujyate bṛhad dhi pūrvaṃ rathantarād vijityā tu vai rathantaraṃ pūrvaṃ yogam ānaśe
sambhāryās tṛcā bhavanti yathāśiṣṭhān vahiṣṭhān sambhared evam evaitān sambharanti gatyai
nava bhavanti navāhasya yuktyā ṛcarcaivāhar yunakti yathāprārthasya śamyā avadadhyād evam evaitan navāhasya śamyā avadadhāti gatyai
trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣu
nirāhāvanty ājyāni bhavanti yuktam eva tair āhvayati
agna āyāhi vītaya ā no mitrāvaruṇāyāhi suṣamā hi ta indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam iti rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ iti
pra somāso vipaścita iti gāyatrī bhavati pretyā abhidroṇāni babhrava ity abhikrāntyai stutā indrāya vāyava iti saṃskṛtyai pra soma deva vītaya iti pretyai pra tu draveti pretyai pra vā etenāhnā yanti
gāyatraṃ bhavati
yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
āśvaṃ bhavati
aśvo vai bhūtvā prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa prājāyata bahur abhavat prajāyate bahur bhavaty āśvena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ekākṣaraṃ nidhanam upayanti rathantarasyānativādāya
anativādy enaṃ bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
somasāma bhavati
yathā vā imā anyā oṣadhayaḥ evaṃ soma āsīt sa tapo 'tapyata sa etat somasāmāpaśyat tena rājyamādhipatyam agacchad yaśo 'bhavad rājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati yaśo bhavati somasāmnā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
yaudhājayaṃ bhavati yad eva yaudhājayasya brāhmaṇam
auśanaṃ yad auśanasya stomaḥ
abhi tvā śūra no nu ma ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
kayā naś citra ābhuvad iti kavatyas tena prājāpatyāḥ ko hi prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai
taṃ vo dasmam ṛtīṣahaṃ vasor mandānam andhaso 'bhivatsaṃ na svasareṣu dhenava ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rathantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
indraṃ gīrbhir havāmaha iti havanta evainam
tarobhir vo vidadvasum iti stomo vai taro yajño vidadvasuḥ stomena vai yajño yujyate yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum ity āha yajñam eva tad yunakti
rathantaraṃ bhavati brahma vai rathantaraṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad brahmākramya prayanti
iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate
vāmadevyaṃ bhavati paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśūnām avaruddhyai prājāpatyaṃ vai vāmadevyaṃ prajāpatāv eva pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate
naudhasaṃ bhavati brahma vai naudhasaṃ brahma prāyaṇīyam ahar brahmaṇa eva tad rahmākramante
kāleyaṃ bhavati samānaloke vai kāleyañ ca rathantarañ ceyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ paśavaḥ kāleyam asyāñ caiva paśuṣu ca pratiṣṭhāya sattram āsate
dravadiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
pra somāso madacyuta iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavṛt tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāty ayā pasvasva devayur ity eti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ pavate 'har yato harir iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bṛhad eva tad etasminn ahani yunakti tad yuktaṃ śva ārabhante pra sunvānāyāndhasa iti pravatyo bhavanti praṇinīṇyam iva hy etad ahar abhi priyāṇi pavate ca nohita ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
yajñā yajñā vo agnaya ity agner vai yajño yajña eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
saṃhitaṃ bhavati vyakṣaraṇidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai pratiṣṭhāyaiva sattram āsate
saphaṃ bhavati
saphena vai devā imān lokān samāpnuvvan yat samāpnuvaṃs tat saphasya saphatvam imān evaitena lokān samāpya sattram āsate
ākṣāraṃ bhavati
aṣṭau vā etāḥ kādughā āsaṃs tāsām ekā samaśīryata sā kṛṣir abhavad ṛdhyate 'smai kṛṣau ya evaṃ veda
tāsu devāsurā aspardhanta te devā asurān kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇānudanta nudate bhrātṛvyaṃ kāmadughābhya ākṣāreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ebhyo vai lokebhyo raso 'pākrāmat taṃ prajāpatir ākṣāreṇākṣārayad yad ākṣārayat tad ākṣārasyākṣāratvam
tasmād yaḥ purā puṇyo bhūtvā paścāt pāpīyān syād ākṣāraṃ brahma sāma kurvītātmany eved indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam ākṣārayati
januṣaikarco bhavato 'hno dhṛtyai yad vā etasyāhno 'dhṛtaṃ tad etābhyāṃ dādhāra
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati
gaurīvitir vā etac chāktyo brāhmaṇo 'tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitam abhavat
atiriktaṃ vā etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitenāhīnāñ chavastanavad bhavaty api prajāyā upakḷptam
vṛṣā vā etad vājisāma vṛṣabho retodhā adya stuvanti śvaḥ prajāyate
anuṣṭubhi chandasāṃ kriyate 'nuṣṭub bhi chandasāṃ yoniḥ svāyām eva tad yonau reto dhatte prajātyai
prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda
dvyudāsaṃ bhavaty etau vā udāsau svargasya lokasyāvasānadarśau pūrveṇa pūrvam ahaḥ saṃsthāpayanty uttareṇottaram ahar abhyativadanti
tad yathādaḥ pūrvedyuḥ spaṣṭaṃ tṛṇodakam anvavasyanto yanty evam eva tābhyāṃ svargaṃ lokam anvavasyanto yanti
gautamaṃ bhavati
sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
yad u caivānuṣtṭubhasya madhye nidhanasya brāhmaṇaṃ tad du caitasya
kāvaṃ bhavati
lokabinduḥ sāma vindate lokaṃ kāvena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
svārasu svareṇa svareṇa hi devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ pradīyate svareṇaiva tad devebhyo 'ntato 'nnādyaṃ pra yacchati
yajñāyajñīyaṃ bhavati
vāg yajñāyajñīyaṃ vāci yajñaḥ pratiṣṭhito vācy eva tad yajñam antataḥ pratiṣṭhāpayanti taṃ vāco 'dhi śva ārabhante
trivṛd eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
pratipad bhavati
samārabhate dvirātrasyāvrisraṃsāya
pavasvendo vṛṣāsuta ity anurūpyo bhavati vṛṣāvad vā eta aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
pūrvam u tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam
anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda
stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
vṛṣaṇvantas tṛcā bhavatīndriyasya vīryasyāvarudhyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati
yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
pañdadaśa eva stomo bhavati
ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhati ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ
ubhābhyāṃ vai rūpābhyāṃ bahiṣpavamānyo yujyante yatsāmā stomo bhavati tad ājyeṣu
nirāhopasthitāny ājyāni bhavanti
agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmahe mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha indram id gāthino bṛhad indro agnā namo bṛhad iti bārhatam eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ
vṛṣā pavasva dhārayeti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
punānas soma dhārayeti dhṛtyai
vṛṣā śoṇo abhikanikradad gā iti
vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa samṛddhā vṛṣaṇvad vā etad aindraṃ traiṣṭubham ahar yat dvitīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
yauktāśvaṃ bhavati
yuktāśvo va āṅgirasaḥ śiśū jātau viparyaharat tasmān mantro 'pākrāmat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad yauktāśvam apaśyat taṃ mantra upāvartata tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sama yauktāśvaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
āyāsye bhavataḥ
ayāsyo vā āṅgirasa ādityānāṃ dīkṣitānām annādyam āśnāt taṃ śug ārcchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa ete āyāsye apaśyat tābhyāṃ śucam apāhatāpa śucaṃ hata āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ebhyo vai lokebhyo vṛṣṭir apākrāmat tām ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayati vṛṣṭim āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ
annādyaṃ vāva tad ebhyo lokebhyo 'pākrāmat tad ayāsya āyāsyābhyām acyāvayat cyāvayaty annādyam āyāsyābhyāṃ tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vāsiṣṭhaṃ bhavati
vasiṣṭho vā etena vaiḍavaḥ stutvāñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
tvām id dhi havāmaha iti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
abhipravaḥ surādhasam iti yuñjate vai pūrveṇāhnā hy etena prayanti
tvām idā hyo nara ity adya caiva hyaś ca samārabhate dvirātrasyāvisraṃsāya
bṛhad bhavati varṣma vai bṛhad varṣma dvitīyam ahar varṣmaṇa eva tad varṣmākramante
śyetaṃ bhavati sāmnorvāho yajñasya santatyai
mādhucchandasaṃ bhavati sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ūrdhveḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
yas te mado vareṇya iti gāyatrī bhavati
madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
pavasva madhumattama iti pavanta iva hy etenāhnā madhumattama ity annaṃ vai madhv annādyam eva tad yajamāne dadhāti
indram accha sutā ima itīndriyasya vīryasyāvarudhyai
ayaṃ pūṣā rayir bhaga iti
anuṣṭubhaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
vṛṣāmatīnāṃ pavate vicakṣaṇa iti jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
hāviṣmataṃ bhavati
haviṣmāṃś ca vai haviṣkṛc cāṅgirasāv āstāṃ dvitīye 'hani haviṣmān arādhnon navame 'hani haviṣkṛt
ayaṃ haviṣmān ity eva jātam ahar jātaṃ somaṃ prāha devebhyaḥ sāmnaivāsmā āśiṣam āśāste sāma hi saty āśīḥ
śaṅku bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai yad vā adhṛtaṃ śaṅkunā tad dādhāra
tad u sīdantīyam iy āhur etena vai prajāpatir ūrdhva imān lokān asīdad yad asīdat tat sīdantīyasya sīdantīyatvam ūrdhva imān lokān sīdati sīdantīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
sujñānaṃ bhavati
svarvad vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ svarṇadhanaṃ bārhatam
svarṇadhanaṃ bhavati tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
pluvau vā etāv upohante svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
krauñcaṃ bhavati
vāg vai krauñcaṃ vāg dvādaśāho vācy eva tad vācā stuvate yajñasya prabhūtyai
yāmaṃ bhavati
etena vai yamo 'napajayyam amuṣya lokasyādhipatyam āśnutānapajayyam amuṣya lokasyādhipatyam aśnute yāmena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
etena vai yamī yamaṃ svargaṃ lokam agamayat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
ehy ū ṣu bravāṇi ta ity ehivatyai bhavanti tṛtīyasyāhna upahavāya santatyai
apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāya
evāhy asi vīrayur iti samānaṃ vadantīdam ittham asad iti
indraṃ viśvā avīvṛdhann ity avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam evaitayā vardhanti
sākam aśvaṃ bhavaty ukthānām abhijityā abhikrāntyai
etena hy agra ukthāny adhyajayann etenābhyakrāman
āmahīyavaṃ bhavati kḷptiś cānnādyañ ca samānaṃ vadantīṣu kriyata idam ittham asad iti
kṣatraṃ vā etad ahar abhinirvadati yat pañcadaśaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu brahmasāma bhavati brahma caiva tat kṣatrañ ca sayujī karoti brahmaiva kṣatrasya purastān nidadhati brahmaṇe kṣatrañ ca viśañ cānuge karoti
brahma vai pūrvam ahaḥ kṣatraṃ dvitīyaṃ yad gāyatrīṣu brahma sāma bhavati brahma tad yaśasārdhayati brahma hi gāyatrī
tad u samānaṃ vadantīṣu kriyate samṛddhyai
āṣṭādaṃṣṭre bhavataḥ
aiyāhā iti vā indro vṛtram ahann aiyādohoveti nyagṛhṇād vārtraghne sāmanī vīryavatī
ojo evaitābhyāṃ vīryam avarundhe
pañcadaśa eva stomo bhavaty ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ
davidyutaty āruceti tṛtīyasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
davidyutatī vai gāyatrī pariṣṭobhantī triṣṭub gavāśīr jagatī trīṇi rūpāṇi samārabhate trirātrasyāvisraṃsāya
ete asṛgram indava ity anurūpo bhavati
eta iti vai prajāpatir devān asṛjatāsṛgram iti manuṣyān indava iti pit.ṛṃs tad eva tad abhivadati
pūrvam u caiva tad repam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpaṇo 'nuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda
stotrīyānurūpau tṛco bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
rājā medhābhir īyate pavamāno manāv adhy antarikṣeṇa yātava iti
antarikṣadevatyas tṛco bhavaty antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
pañcarcau bhavati pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhy upayānti
saptadaśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
agnināgniḥ samidhyata ity āgreyam ājyaṃ bhavati
pūrve eva tad ahanī samiddhe tṛtīyam ahar abhisamindhe
mitraṃ huve pūtadakṣam iti rāthantaram maitrāvaruṇam
huva iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpam
rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati
indreṇa saṃ hi dṛkṣusa ity aindram
sam iva vā ime lokā dadṛśire 'ntarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
tā huve yayor idam iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam
huva iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yad vairūpaṃ rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ
uccā te jātam andhasa iti gāyatrī bhavati
udvad vā etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
andhasvatī bhavaty ahar vā andho 'hna ārambhaḥ
abhi somāsa āyava iti
abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥ
tisro vāca īrayati pravahnir iti tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tena tṛtīyam ahar ārabhante
triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa jāgataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
vaiṣṭambhaṃ bhavati
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā vaiṣṭambhair vyaṣṭabhnuvaṃs tad vaiṣṭambhasya vaiṣṭambhatvam
diśa iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai
paurūmadgaṃ bhavati
ahar vā etad avlīyamānaṃ tad rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tasmād devāḥ paurūmadgena rakṣāṃsy apāghnann apa pāpmānaṃ hate paurūmadgena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
devāś ca vāsurāś cāspardhanta te devā asurāṇāṃ paurūmadgena puro 'majjayan yat puro 'majjayaṃs tasmāt paurūmadgaṃ pāpmānam evaitena bhrātṛvyaṃ majjayati
gautamaṃ bhavati
yad eva gautamasya brāhmaṇam
ubhayataḥ stotraṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
antarikṣaṃ bhavati
antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyam antarikṣa eva tad antarikṣeṇa stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
āṣkāraṇidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ bhavati
as iti vai rāthantaraṃ rūpaṃ has iti bārhataṃ tṛtīyam eva tad rūpam upayanti samṛdhyai
aṅgirasāṃ saṃkrośo bhavati
etena vā aṅgirasaḥ saṃkrośamānāḥ svargaṃ lokam āpan svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
yady āva indra te śatam iti śatavatyo bhavanti
śatavad vai paśūnāṃ rūpaṃ sahasravat paśūnām evaitābhī rūpam avarūndhe
vayaṅ ghatvā sutāvanta iti satobṛhatyo varṣīyaś chanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya
taraṇir it siṣāsati vājaṃ purandhyā yujā/ āva indraṃ puruhūtaṃ na me girety āvad akṣaram uddhatam iva vai tṛtīyam ahar yad eva tāvad akṣaraṃ bhavaty ahar evaitena pratiṣṭhāpayati
pañcanidhanaṃ vairūpaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati diśāṃ dhṛtyai
pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annāghasyāvarūdhyai
diśāṃ vā etat sāma yad vairūpaṃ diśo hy evaitenābhivadati
atha yat pañcanidhanaṃ tenartūnāṃ pañca hy ṛtavaḥ
ṛtubhiś ca vā ime lokā digbhiś cāvṛtās teṣv evobhayeṣu yajamānaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati yajamānaṃ vā anupratitiṣṭhantam udgātā pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ vidvān vairūpeṇodgāyati
digvad bhavati bhrātṛvyasyāpanutyai
diśaṃ viśam iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai
has ity upariṣṭād diśāṃ nidhanam upayanti tena bārhatam
rāthantaro vā ayaṃ loko bārhato 'sāv ubhe eva tad bṛhadrathantarayo rūpeṇāparādhnoti
anaḍvāhau vā etau devayānau yajamānasya yad bṛhadrathantare tāv eva tad yunakti svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
aśvavad bhavati prajātyai
yathā maṇḍūka āṭ karoty evaṃ nidhanam upayanty ayātayāmatāyai
dvādaśa vairūpāṇi bhavanti dvādaśamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati
virūpaḥ saṃvatsaro virūpam annādyasyāvarudhyai
mahāvaiṣṭambhaṃ brahmasāma bhavaty annādyasyāvarudhyai
yadā vai puruṣo 'nnam atty athāntarato viṣṭabdhaḥ
diśa iti nidhanam upayanti diśāṃ dhṛtyai
sato bṛhatīṣu stuvanti pūrvayor ahnoḥ pratyudyamāya
rauravam acchāvākasāma bhavati
agnir vai rūro rūdro 'gniḥ
agnir vā etasya paśūn apakramayati yasya paśavo 'pakrāmanty agnir eva tasya paśūn abhikramayati yasya paśavo 'bhikrāmanti
abhy abhy evāsya paśavaḥ krāmanti ya evaṃ vidvān rauraveṇa stuvate
pariṣṭubdheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
''tisro vāca udīrata'' iti tṛtīyasyāhno rūpaṃ tena tṛtīyam ahar ārabhante
udvad vā etat trivad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
''ā sotā pariṣiñcata'' iti parivatyo bhavanti
anto vai tṛtīyam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
''sakhāya āniṣīdata'' ity uddhattam iva vai tṛtīyam ahar yad āha niṣīdatety ahar evaitena pratiṣṭhāpayati
''sutāso madhumattamā'' ity anuṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa jāgataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
''pavitraṃ te vitataṃ brahmaṇaspata'' iti
vitatam iva vā idam antarikṣam antareme antarikṣadevatyam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
pāṣṭhauhaṃ bhavati
paṣṭhavāḍ vā etenāṅgirasaś caturthasyāhno vācaṃ vadantīm upāśṛṇot sa ho vāg iti nidhanam upait tad asyābhyuditaṃ tad ahar avasat
vācaḥ sāma bhavati
vāg vai dvādaśāho vācy eva tad vācā stuvate yajñasya prabhūtyai
niṣkirīyāḥ sattram āsata te tṛtīyam ahar na prājānaṃs tān etat sāma gāyamānān vāg upāplavat tena tṛtīyam ahaḥ prājānaṃs te 'bruvann iyaṃ vāva nas tṛtīyam ahar adīdṛśad iti tṛtīyasyaivaiṣāhno dṛṣṭiḥ
śauktaṃ bhavati
śuktir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
tvāṣṭrīsāma bhavati
indraṃ vā akṣyāmayiṇaṃ bhūtāni nāsvāpayaṃs tam etena tvāṣṭrayo 'svāpayaṃs tad vāva tās tarhy akāmayanta
kāmasani sāma tvāṣṭrīsāma kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
indro vṛtrād vibhyad gāṃ prāviśat taṃ tvāṣṭrayo 'bruvaṃ janayāmeti tam etaiḥ sāmabhir ajanayaṃ jāyāmahā iti vai sattram āsate jāyanta eva
ariṣṭaṃ bhavati
devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta yaṃ devānām aghnan na sa samabhavad yam asurāṇāṃ saṃ so 'bhavat te devās tapo 'tapyanta ta etad ariṣṭam apaśyaṃs tato 'yaṃ devānām aghnat saṃ so 'bhavad yam asurāṇāṃ na sa samabhavad anenāriṣāmeti tad ariṣṭasyāriṣṭatvam ariṣṭayā evāriṣṭam antataḥ kriyate
trīḍaṃ bhavati trirātrasya dhṛtyai
dravantīm iḍām uttamām upayanti caturthasyāhnaḥ santatyai stomaḥ
pramaṃhiṣṭhāya gāyateti
yad gāyateti mahasa eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
''taṃ te mad aṅgaṇīm asīti madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
''śrudhī havaṃ tiraścyā'' iti śrutyā eva
pramaṃhiṣṭhīya bhavati
pramaṃhiṣṭhīyena vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāvartayat tam astṛṇuta bhrātṛvyavān pramaṃhiṣṭhīyenokthāni praṇayeta stṛṇute bhrātṛvyaṃ vasīyāṃ ātmanā bhavati
hārivarṇaṃ bhavati
indraś ca vai namuciś cāsuraḥ samadadhātāṃ na no naktan na divāhanan nārdreṇa na śuṣkeṇeti tasya vyuṣṭāyām anudita āditye 'pāṃ phenena śiro 'chinad etad vai na naktaṃ na divā yat vyuṣṭāyām anudita āditya etan nārdran na śuṣkaṃ yad apāṃ phenas tad enaṃ pāpīyāṃ vācaṃ vadad anvavartata vīrahan na druho druha iti tan narcā na sāmnāpahantum aśaknot
hārivarṇasyaiva nidhanenāpāhata
apaśucaṃhate hārivarṇasya nidhanena śriyaṃ ca haraś copaiti tuṣṭuvānaḥ
tairaścayaṃ bhavati
aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ yanto rakṣāṃsy anvasacanta tāny etena tiraścāṅgirasas tiryaṅ paryavaid yat tiryaṅ aparyavait tasmāt tairaścyaṃ pāpmā vāva sa tān asacata taṃ tairaścyenāpāghnatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate tairaścyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
saptadaśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
''pra ta āśvinīḥ pavamānadhenava'' iti caturthasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
āpte trirātre rūpeṇa gāyatryo dvitīyaṃ prayanti prati vai gāyatryā rūpam
jagatī pratipad bhavati jāgatam etad ahar yat tṛtīyaṃ jagatyā eva taj jagatīm abhisaṃkrāmanti
yad ato 'nyā pratipatsyāt pratikūlaṃ vānukūlaṃ vā syāt
pavamāno ajījanad ity anurūpo bhavati
janadvad vā etad ahar yac caturtham annādyaṃ janayati virājaṃ janayaty ekaviṃśaṃ stomaṃ janayati
pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam
anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda
stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
ṣaḍṛcau bhavata ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
ekaviṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati
''janasya gopā ajaniṣṭa jāgṛviḥ'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
janadvad vā etad ahar yac caturtham annādyaṃ janayati virājaṃ janayaty ekaviṃśaṃ stomaṃ janayati
''ayaṃ vāṃ mitrāvarūṇā-'' iti bārhataṃ maitrāvarūṇam
bṛhad etat parokṣaṃ yad vairājaṃ bārhatam eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati
''indro dadhīco asthabhir'' iti dādhīcas tṛco bhavati
dadhyaṅ vā āṅgiraso devānāṃ purodhānīya āsīd annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhā annādyasyāvarudhyai
''iyaṃ vāmasya manmana'' ity aindrāgnam
''indrāgnī pūrvyastutir abhrād vṛṣṭir ivājani-'' ity ānuṣṭubhī vai vṛṣṭir ānuṣṭubham etad ahar yac caturthaṃ samīcyau virājau dadhāty annādyāya stomaḥ
''payasva dakṣasādhana'' iti gāyatrī bhavati sidhyai
yat pavasveti tad bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
''tavāhaṃ soma rāraṇa sakhya indo dive dive/ purūṇi babhro nicaranti mām ava paridhīṃr atitāṃ ihi-'' iti
ati hy āyañ chakunā iva paptim ety ati hy apatat
punāno akramīd abhīti
gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
caturṇidhanam ātharvaṇaṃ bhavati catūrātrasya dhṛtyai
catuṣpadānuṣṭubhānuṣṭubham etad ahar yac caturtham
bheṣajaṃ vātharvaṇāni bheṣajam eva tat karoti
nidhanakāmaṃ bhavati
ekaṃ vā anyena niruktena nidhanena kāmaṃ sanoty athaitan nidhanakāmaṃ sarveṣāṃ kāmānām avarudhyai
āṣṭādaṃṣṭraṃ bhavati
yad evāṣṭādaṃṣṭrasya brāhmaṇam
ābhīśavaṃ bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
yad vā adhṛtam abhīśunā tad dādhāra
anutunnaṃ gāyati tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
caturṇidhanam āṅgirasaṃ bhavati catūrātrasya dhṛtyai
svaḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
sattrāsāhīyaṃ bhavati
yad vā asurāṇām asoḍham āsīt tad devāḥ sattrāsāhīyenāsahanta sattrainān asakṣmahīti tat sattrāsāhīyasya sattrāsāhīyatvam
sattrā bhrātṛvyaṃ sahate sattrāsāhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
vṛṣaṇvatyo gāyatrayo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān nayanti stomaḥ
''pibā somam indra mandatu tvā yante suṣāva haryaśvādriḥ/ sotur bāhubhyāṃ suyato nārvā-'' ity ayatam iva vai caturtham ahas tasyaiva yatyai
viśvāḥ pṛtanā abhibhṛtarannara ity atijagatī varṣīyayaś chanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yaj jayāyasaś chandasaḥ kanīyaś chanda upaiti yad eṣā caturthe 'hany atijagatī kriyate 'napabhraṃśāya
yo rājā carṣaṇīnām iti
rājye hy etarhi vāco 'gacchan rājyam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
chandobhir vai devā ādityaṃ svargaṃ lokam aharan sa nādhriyata taṃ vairājasya nidhanenādṛṃhaṃs tasmāt parāṅ cārvāṅ cādityas tapati parāṅ cārvāṅ cekāraḥ
prastāvaṃ prastutya viṣṭambhān viṣṭabhnoti mukhata eva tad annādyaṃ dhatte mukhaṃ hi sāmnaḥ prastāvaḥ
daśakṛtvo viṣṭabhnoti daśākṣarā virāṅ vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
triṃśatkṛtvo viṣṭabhnoti bhūyaso 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai
vairājaṃ sāma bhavati virāṭsu stuvanti vairājā viṣṭambhāḥ samīcīr virājo dadhāty annādyāya
anutunnaṃ gāyati retodheyāyānutunnād dhi reto dhīyate
dakṣiṇa ūrāv udgatur agniṃ manthanti dakṣiṇato hi retaḥ sicyate
upākṛte 'hiṅkṛte manthanti jātam abhihiṅkaroti
tasmāj jātaṃ putraṃ paśavo 'bhihiṅkurvanti
tasmai jātāyāmīmāṃsanta gārhapatye praharāmā3 āgnīdhrā3 āhavanīyā3 iti
āhavanīye praharanty etad āyatano vai yajamāno yadā havanīye svam eva tad āyatanaṃ jyotiṣmat karoti
jyotiṣmān brahmavarcasī bhavati ya evaṃ veda
abhijuhoti śāntyai
ājyenābhijuhoti tejo vā ājyaṃ teja eva tad ātman dhatte
''preddho agne dīdihi puro na'' iti virājābhijuhoty annaṃ virāḍ annādyasyāvarudhyai
traiśokaṃ brahmasāma bhavati
atijagatīṣu stuvanty ahna utkrāntyā ud vā etenāhnā krāmanti
diveti nidhanam upayanti pāpmano 'pahatyā apapāpmānaṃ hate traiśokena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
bhāradvājasya pṛśny achāvākasāma bhavati
annaṃ vai devāḥ pṛśnīti vadanty annādyasyāvarudhyai
iḍābhir aiḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ stomaḥ
''paripriyā divaḥ kavir'' iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai caturtham ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
tvaṃ hy aṅga daivyeti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
somaḥ punāna ūrmiṇā vyaṃvāraṃ vidhāvati/ agre vācaḥ pavamānaḥ kanikradad iti
agraṃ hy etarhi vāco 'gacchann agram evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
''puro jitīvo andhasā-'' iti virājau vairājaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
''somaḥ pavate janitā matīnām'' iti prātassavane ṣoḍaśinaṃ gṛhītaṃ taṃ tṛtīyasavane prajanayanti
triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
aurṇāyavaṃ bhavati
aṅgiraso vai sattram āsata teṣām āptaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo loka āsīt panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ na prājānaṃs teṣāṃ kalyāṇa āṅgiraso dhyāyam udavrajat sa ūrṇāyuṃ gandharvam apsarasāṃ madhye preṅkhayamāṇam upait sa iyām iti yāṃ yām abhyadiśat sainam akāmayata tam abhyavadat kālyāṇā3 ity āso vai vaḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ na prajānīthedaṃ sāma svargyaṃ lokam eṣy atha mā tu vocoham adarśam iti
sa ait kalyāṇaḥ so 'bravīd āpto vai naḥ spṛtaḥ svargo lokaḥ panthānaṃ tu devayānaṃ prajānīma idaṃ sāma svargyaṃ tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam eṣyāma iti kas te 'vocad ity aham evādarśam iti tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam āyann ahīyata kalyāṇo 'nṛtaṃ hi so 'vadat sa eṣaḥ śvitraḥ
svargyaṃ vā etat sāma svargalokaḥ puṇyaloko bhavaty aurṇāyavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
bṛhatkaṃ bhavati
sāmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ tvaṃ hīty annādyasyāvarudhyai hīti vā annaṃ pradīyate ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchati
ātīṣādīyaṃ bhavati
āyur vā ātīṣādīyam āyuṣo 'ṣarudhyai
ātamitor nidhanam upayanty āyur eva sarvam āpnuvanti
nānadaṃ bhavati
jyāyo 'bhyārambham atihāya pañcam ahaḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhna ārambhas tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai
ṣoḍaśākṣareṇa prastauti ṣoḍaśinam u caivaitenodyacchati
āndhīgavaṃ bhavati
kayor annādyam avarūndha āndhīgavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vātsapraṃ bhavati
etasmin vai vairājaṃ pratiṣṭhitaṃ pratitiṣṭhati vātsapreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vatsaprīr bhālandanaḥ śraddhāṃ nāvindata sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad vātsapram apaśyat sa śraddhām avindata śraddhā vindāmahā iti vai sattram āsate vindate śraddhām
īnidhanaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpaṃ nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
''agniṃ vo vṛdhantam'' iti
avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam eva tathā vardhayanti
''vayam u tvām apūrvya-'' ity apūrvāṃ hy etarhi prajāpates tanūm agacchann apūrvam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
''imam indra sutaṃ piba jyeṣṭham amartyaṃ madam'' iti jyaiṣṭhaṃ hy etarhi vāco 'gacchan jyaiṣṭhyam evaitayā yajamānaṃ gamayanti
saindhukṣitaṃ bhavati
sindhukṣid vai rājanyarṣir jyog aparuddhaś caran sa etat saindhukṣitam apaśyat so 'vāgacchat pratyatiṣṭhad avagacchati pratitiṣṭhati saindhukṣitena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
saubharaṃ bhavati bṛhatas tejaḥ
pannam iva vai caturtham ahas tad etena bṛhatas tejasottabhnoti saubhareṇa
vasiṣṭhasya priyaṃ bhavati
etena vai vasiṣṭha indrasya premāṇam agacchat premāṇaṃ devatānāṃ gacchati vāsiṣṭhena tuṣṭuvānaḥ stomaḥ
indraś ca bṛhac ca samabhavatāṃ tam indraṃ bṛhad ekayā tanvāty aricyata tasyā abibhedanayā mābhibhaviṣyatīti so 'bravīt ṣoḍaśī te 'yaṃ yajñakratur astv iti sa ṣoḍaśy abhavat tad asya janma
atiśriyā bhrātṛvyaṃ ricyate yo gāyatrīṣu dvipadāsu bṛhatā ṣoḍaśinā stute
''upa no haribhiḥ stutam'' ity etā vai gāyatryo dvipadā etāsu stotavyam
indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etām anuṣṭubham apaharasaṃ prāyacchat tayā nāstṛṇuta yad astṛtā vyanadat tan nānadasya nānadatvam
taṃ punar upādhāvat tasmai saptānāṃ hotrāṇāṃ haro nirmāya prāyacchat tam astṛṇuta
stṛṇute taṃ yaṃ tustūrṣate ya evaṃ veda
tasmād dharivatīṣu stuvanti harivatīḥ śaṃsanti harivatīṣu graho gṛhyate haro hy asmai nirmāya prāyacchat
ekaviṃśāyatano vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī sapta hi prātassavane hotrā vaṣaṭkurvanti sapta mādhyandine savane sapta tṛtīyasavane
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati
gaurīvitir vā etac chāktyo brahmaṇo 'tiriktam apaśyat tad gaurīvitam abhavad atiriktaṃ etad atiriktena stuvanti yad gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinaṃ śvastanavān bhavaty api prajāyā upakḷptaḥ
viśālaṃ libjayā śrūtyābhyadhād iti hovācopoditir gopāleyo 'nuṣṭubhi nānadam akar gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinam astoṣṭāñjasā śriyam upāgān na śriyā avapadyata iti
eṣa vai viśālaṃ libjayā bhūtyābhidadhāti yo 'nuṣṭubhi nānadaṃ kṛtvā gaurīvitena ṣoḍaśinā stute 'ñjasā śriyam upaiti na śriyā avapadyate
śakvarīṣu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta vajrī syām iti
vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vajraḥ śakvaryo vajreṇaivāsmai vajraṃ spṛṇoti vajrī bhavati
anuṣṭupsu ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta yaḥ kāmayeta na mā vāg ativadet
vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vāg anuṣṭub vajreṇaivāsmai vācaṃ spṛṇoti nainaṃ vāg ativadati
''asāvi soma indra ta'' ity etāsu stotavyam
virāṭsv annādyakāmaḥ ṣoḍaśinā stuvīta vajro vai ṣoḍaśī vairājam annaṃ vajreṇaivāsmā annaṃ spṛṇoty annādo bhavati
''pra vo mahe vṛdhe bharadhvam'' ity etāsu stotavyam
trayastriṃśadakṣarā vā etā virājo yad ekaviṃśatiḥ pratiṣṭhā sā yad dvādaśa prajātiḥ sā
pratiṣṭhāya prajāyate no cāntasthāyāṃ jīryate ya evaṃ veda
atha vā etā ekapadās tryakṣarā viṣṇoś chando bhurijaḥ śakvaryaḥ
etābhir vā indro vṛtram ahan kṣipraṃ vā etābhiḥ pāpmānaṃ hanti kṣipraṃ vasīyān bhavati
catustriṃśadakṣarāḥ saṃstuto bhavati trayastriṃśaddevattāḥ prajāpatiś catustriṃśo devatānāṃ prajāpatim evopayanty ariṣṭyai
hiraṇyaṃ sampradāyaṃ ṣoḍaśinā stuvate jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavati
aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa upatiṣṭhati sāmyekṣayāya bhrātṛvyalokam eva sa vidhamaṃs tiṣṭhati
ekākṣaraṃ vai devānām avamaṃ chanda āsīt saptākṣaraṃ paramaṃ navākṣaram asurāṇām avamaṃ chanda āsīt pañcadaśākṣaraṃ paramaṃ devāś ca vā asurāś cāspardhanta tān prajāpatir ānuṣṭubho bhūtvāntarātiṣṭhat taṃ devāsurā vyahvayanta sa devān upāvartata tato devā abhavan parāsurāḥ
bhavaty ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
te devā asurāṇām ekākṣareṇaiva pañcadaśākṣaram avṛñjata dvyakṣareṇa caturdaśākṣaraṃ tryakṣareṇa trayodaśākṣaraṃ caturakṣareṇa dvādaśākṣaraṃ pañcākṣareṇaikādaśākṣaraṃ ṣaḍakṣareṇa daśākṣaraṃ saptākṣareṇa navākṣaram aṣṭābhir evāṣṭāv avṛñjata
evam eva bhrātṛvyād bhūtiṃ vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda
aparuddhayajña iva vā eṣa yat ṣoḍaśī kanīyasvina iva vai tarhi devā āsan bhūyasvino 'surāḥ kanīyasvina bhūyasvinaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ vṛṅkte ya evaṃ veda
''yasmād anyo na paro 'sti jāto ya ābabhūva bhuvanāni viśvā/ prajāpatiḥ prajayā samvidānas trīṇi jyotīṃ ṣi sacate sa ṣoḍaśī-'' ity udgātā graham avekṣate
jyotiṣmān asya ṣoḍaśī bhavati ya evaṃ veda
ekaviṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati
''govit pavasva vasuvid dhiraṇyavid'' iti pañcamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
govid vā etad vasuvid dhiraṇyavidyac chakvaryaḥ
paśavaś śakvaryaḥ sarvaṃ paśubhir vindate
''tvaṃ suvīro asi somaviśvavid'' ity eṣa yāva suvīro yasya paśavas tad eva tad abhivadati
tās te kṣarantu madhumad ghṛtaṃ paya'' iti madhumad vai ghṛtaṃ payaḥ paśavaḥ kṣaranti tad eva tad abhivadati
''pavamānasya viśvavid'' ity anurūpo bhavati
viśvam eva tadvit tam abhivadati viśvaṃ hi paśubhir vindate
''pra te sargā asṛkṣata-'' iti sṛṣṭānīva hy etarhy ahāni
pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam, anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda stotrīyānurupau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
saptarcau bhavataḥ chandasāṃ dhṛtyai
caturṛco bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhy udyanti
triṇava eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai puṣṭyai trivṛd vā eṣa puṣṭaḥ
''tava śriyo varṣasy eva vidyuta'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
śrīr vai paśavaḥ śrīḥ śakvaryaḥ tad eva tad abhivadati
''agneś cikitra uṣasām ivetaya'' itītānīva hy etarhy ahānīti
''ā te yatente rathyo yathā pṛthag'' ity eva hy etarhy ahāni yatante
''purūruṇā cid dhy asty avo nūnaṃ vāṃ varuṇa-'' iti maitrāvaruṇam
yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇāti tad eva tad avayajati
''uttiṣṭhann ojasā saha-'' ity aindram
pañca vā ṛtava utthānasya rūpam ojasā sahety ojasaiva vīryeṇa sahottiṣṭhanti
''indrāgnī yuvām ima'' iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam
rathantaram etat parokṣaṃ yac chakvaryo rāthantaram eva tad rūpaṃ nirdyotayati stomaḥ
''arṣā soma dyumattama'' iti viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavanti
brahma vai gāyatrī yajño viṣṇur brahmaṇy eva tad yajñaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
''soma uṣvāṇas sotṛbhir'' iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivaitās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
''yat soma citram ukthyam'' iti gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
yaṇvaṃ bhavati paśavo vai yaṇvaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai
santataṃ gāyati yajñasya santatye
adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
śākalaṃ bhavati
etena vai śakalaḥ pañcame 'hani pratyatiṣṭhat pratitiṣṭhati śākalena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vārśaṃ bhavati
vṛśo vaijānas tryaruṇasya traidhātavasyaikṣvākasya purohita āsīt sa aikṣvāko 'dhāvayat brāhmaṇakumāraṃ rathena vyacchinat sa purohitam abravīt tava mā purodhāyām idam īdṛg upāgād iti tam etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vārśaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
mānavaṃ bhavati
etena vai manuḥ prajāpatiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati mānavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ānūpaṃ bhavati
etena vai vadhryaśva ānūpaḥ paśūnāṃ bhūmānam āśnuta paśūnāṃ bhūmānam aśnuta ānūpena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vāmraṃ bhavati
māmārṣeyeṇa praśastaṃ yaṃ vai gām aśvaṃ puruṣaṃ praśaṃsanti vāma iti taṃ praśaṃsanty ahar evaitena praśaṃsanti
adhyardheḍaṃ tathā hy etasyāhno rūpam
triṇidhanam āgneyaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
agriḥ sṛṣṭo nodadīpyata taṃ prajāpatir etena sāmnopādhamat sa udadīpyata dīptiś ca vā etat sāma brahmavarcasaṃ ca dīptiś caivaitena brahmavarcasaṃ cāvarundhe
śaiśavaṃ bhavati
śiśur vā āṅgiraso mantrakṛtāṃ mantrakṛd āsīt sa pit.ṛn putrakā ity āmantrayata, taṃ pitaro 'bruvan na dharmaṃ karoṣi yo naḥ pit.ṛn sataḥ putrakā ity āmantrayama iti, so 'bravīd ahaṃ vāva vaḥ pitāsmi yo mantrakṛd asmīti, taṃ deveṣv apṛcchanta te devā abuvann eṣa vāva pitā yo mantrakṛd iti tad vai sa udajayad ujjayati śaiśavena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
viṣṇumatyo gāyatryo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ
indraḥ prajāpatim upādhāvad vṛtraṃ hanānīti tasmā etac chandobhya indriyaṃ vīryaṃ nirmāya prāyacchad etena śaknuhīti tac chakvarīṇāṃ śakvarītvaṃ sīmānam abhinat tat simā mahnyam akarot tan mahnyā mahān ghoṣa āsīt tan mahānāmnyaḥ
diśaḥ pañcapadā dādhārartūn ṣaṭpadā chandāṃsi saptapadā puruṣaṃ dvipadā
dvyopaśāḥ saṃstutā bhavanti tasmād dvyopaśāḥ paśavaḥ
iḍe abhito 'thakāraṃ tasmāc chṛṅge tīkṣṇīyasī stūpāt
upakṣudrā gāyati tasmād upakṣudrāḥ paśavaḥ
aṃsaśliṣṭā gāyati tasmād asaṃśliṣṭāḥ paśavaḥ
nānārūpā gāyati tasmān nānārūpāḥ paśavaḥ
āpo vai kṣīrarasā āsaṃste devāḥ pāpavasīyasād abibhayur yad apa upanidhāya stuvate pāpavasīyaso vidhṛtyai
vidhṛtiḥ pāpavasīyaso bhavati ya evaṃ veda
gāyatram ayanaṃ bhavati brahmavarcasakāmasya svarṇidhanaṃ madhunāmuṣmiṃl loka upatiṣṭhate, traiṣṭubham ayanaṃ bhavaty ojaskāmasyāthakāraṇidhana mājyenāmuṣmiṃl loka upatiṣṭhate, jāgatam ayanaṃ bhavati paśukāmasyeḍānidhanaṃ payasāmuṣmiṃl loka upatiṣṭhate
añjasāryo mālyaḥ śakvarīḥ prārautsīd iti hovācālammaṃ pārijānataṃ rajanaḥ kauṇayo yady enāḥ pratiṣṭhāpaṃ śakṣyatīty etad vā etāsām añjayati pratiṣṭhitā ya ābhiḥ kṣipraṃ prastutya kṣipram udgāyati
śakvarībhiḥ stutvā purīṣeṇa stuvate
paśavo vai śakvaryo gauṣṭhaḥ purīṣaṃ goṣṭham eva tat paśubhyaḥ paryasyanti tam evainān pravartyanty avisraṃsāya
''indro madāya vāvṛdha'' ity avardhanta hy etarhi
tāsu bārhadgiram
''svādor itthā viṣuvata'' iti viṣuvān vai pañcamam ahas tāsu rāyovājīyam
indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat teṣāṃ traya udaśiṣyanta pṛthuraśmir bṛhadgirī rāyovājas te 'bruvan ko na imān putrān bhariṣyatīty aham itīndro 'bravīt tān ādhinidhāya paricāryaṃ carad vardhayaṃs tān vardhayitvābravīt kumārakā varān vṛṇīdhvam iti, kṣatraṃ mahyam ity abravīt pṛthuraśmis tasmā etena pārthuraśmena kṣatraṃ prāyacchat kṣatrakāma etena stuvīta kṣatrasyaivāsya prakāśo bhavati, brahmavarcasaṃ mahyam ity abravīt bṛhādgiris tasmā etena bārhadgireṇa prāyacchat brahmavarcasakāma etena stuvīta brahmavarcasī bhavati, paśūn mahyam ity abravīd rāyovājas tasmā etena rāyovājīyena paśūn prāyacchat paśukāma etena stuvīta paśumān bhavati
pārthuraśmaṃ rājanyāya brahmasāma kuryāt bārhadgiraṃ brāhmaṇāya rāyovājīyaṃ vaiśyāya svenaivenāṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati stomaḥ
''asāvy aṃśur madāya-'' iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
''abhi dyumnaṃ bṛhadyaśa'' ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayos saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥ
''prāṇā śiśur mahīnām'' iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ mahyo hi simāḥ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
''pavasva vājasātaya'' iti vaiṣṇavyo 'nuṣṭubho bhavanti
yajño vai viṣṇur yad atra nāpi kriyate tad viṣṇunā yajñenāpi karoti
''indur vājī pavate gonyoghā'' iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivainās tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
triṣṭubhaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
santani bhavati pañcamasyāhnas santatyai
vāg vā eṣā pratatā yad dvādaśāhas tasyā eṣa viṣuvān yat pañcamam ahas tām evaitena santanoti
cyāvanaṃ bhavati
prajātir vai cyāvanaṃ prajāyate bahur bhavati cyāvanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
ebhyo vai lokebhyo vṛṣṭir apākrāmat tāṃ prajāpatiś cyāvanenācyāvayad yad acyāvayat tac cyāvanasya cyāvanatvaṃ cyāvayati vṛṣṭiṃ cyāvanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
kroṣa bhavati
etena vā indra indrakrośe viśvāmitrajamadagnī imā gāva ity ākrośat paśunām avarudhyai krośaṃ kriyate
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
ṛṣabhaḥ śākvaro bhavati
paśavo vai śakvaryaḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apy arjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante
pārthaṃ bhavati
etena vai pṛthur vainya ubhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam āśnutobhayeṣāṃ paśunām ādhipatyam aśnute pārthena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
aṣṭeḍaḥ padastobho bhavati
indro vṛtrāya vajram udayacchat taṃ ṣoḍaśabhir bhogaiḥ paryabhujat sa etaṃ padastobham apaśyat tenāpāveṣṭayad apāveṣṭayann iva gāyet pāpmano 'pahatyai
pāpmā vāva sa tam agṛhṇāt taṃ padastobhenāpāhatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate padastobhena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
pador uttamam apaśyat tat padastobhasya padastobhatvam
dvādaśanidhano bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
dāśaspatyaṃ bhavati
yāṃ vai gāṃ praśaṃsanti dāśaspatyeti tāṃ praśaṃsanty ahar evaitena praśaṃsanti
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
''āte agna idhīmahi-'' iti
apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāyaiva
''indrāya sāma gāyata-'' iti pūrṇāḥ kakubhas tenānaśanāyuko bhavati
puruṣo vai kakup puruṣam eva tan madhyataḥ prīṇāti
''asāvi soma indra ta'' iti simānāṃ rūpaṃ svenaivaināṃs tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
sañjayaṃ bhavati
devāś ca vā asurāś ca samadadhata yatare naḥ sañjayāṃs teṣāṃ naḥ paśavo 'sān iti te devā asurān sañjayena samajayan yat samajayaṃs tasmāt sañjayaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai sañjayaṃ kriyate
saumitraṃ bhavati
dīrghajihvī vā idaṃ rakṣo yajñahā yajñiyān avalihaty acarat tām indraḥ kayācana māyayā hantuṃ nāśaṃsatātha ha sumitraḥ kutsaḥ kalyāṇa āsa tam abravīd imām acchā brūṣveti tām acchā brūta sainam abravīn nāhaitan na śuśruva priyam iva tu me hṛdayasyeti tām ajñapayat tāṃ saṃskṛte 'hatāṃ tad vāva tau tarhy akāmayetāṃ kāmasani sāma saumitraṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
sumitraḥ san krūram akar ity enaṃ vāg abhyavadat taṃ śug ārcchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etat saumitram apaśyat tena śucam apāhatāpaśucaṃ hate saumitreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
mahāvaiśvāmitraṃ bhavati
pāpmānaṃ hatvā yad amahīyanta tan mahāvaiśvāmitrasya mahāvaiśvāmitratvam
hāyā ihayā ohā oheti paśūn evaitena nyauhanta
trīḍaṃ bhavati trirātrasya dhṛtyai
dravantīm iḍām uttamām upayanti ṣaṣṭhasyāhnaḥ santatyai
triṇava eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai puṣṭyai trivṛd vā eṣa puṣṭhaḥ
''jyotir yajñasya pavate madhupriyam'' iti ṣaṣṭhasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
jyotir vai gāyatrī chandamāṃ jyotiḥ revatī sāmnāṃ jyotis trayastriṃśaḥ stomānāṃ jyotir eva tat samyak saṃdadhāsy api ha putrasya putro jyotiṣmān bhavati
''madhu priyam'' iti paśavo vai revatyo madhupriyaṃ tad eva tad abhivadati
''madintamo matsara indriyo rasa'' itīndriyaṃ vai vīryaṃ rasaḥ paśavas tad eva tad abhivadati
''amṛkṣata pravājina'' ity anurūpo bhavati
sṛṣṭānīva hy etarhy ahāni
pūrvam u caiva tad rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati yat pūrvaṃ rūpam apareṇa rūpeṇānuvadati tad anurūpasyānurūpatvam anurūpa enaṃ putro jāyate ya evaṃ veda stotrīyānurūpau tṛcau bhavataḥ prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
daśarcau bhavato daśākṣarā virāṭ vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
uttaro daśarco bhavati sodarka indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya
yatra ve devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
caturṛco bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
dhvasre vai puruṣantī tarantapurumīḍhābhyāṃ vaitadaśvibhyāṃ sahasrāṇy aditsatāṃ tāv aikṣetāṃ kathaṃ nāv idam āttam apratigṛhītaṃ syād iti tau praty etāṃ dhvasrayoḥ puruṣantyor ā sahasrāṇi dadmahe tarat sa mandī dhāvatīti tato vai tat tayor āttam apratigṛhītam abhavat
āttam asyāpratigṛhītaṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
vinārāśaṃso bhavaty ubhayasyānnādyasyāvarudhyai mānuṣasya ca daivasya ca
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
trayastriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai devatāsu vā eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ
''imaṃ stomam arhate jātavedasa'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
''prativāṃ sūra udita'' iti sūravan maitrāvaruṇam
anto vai sūro 'nta etat ṣaṣṭham ahar ahnām anta eva tad ante stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
''bhindhi viśvā apadviṣa'' ity aindraṃ sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
''yajñasya hi stha ṛtvija'' ity aindrāgnaṃ sodarkam indriyasya vīryasya rasasyānatikṣārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan stomaḥ
''indrāyendo marutvata'' iti marutvatyo gāyatryo bhavanti
marutvad dhi mādhyandinaṃ savanam
''mṛjyamānaḥ suhastya-'' iti simānāṃ rūpam
samānaṃ vai simānāṃ rūpaṃ revatīnāṃ ca simābhyo hy adhirevatyaḥ prajāyante
''etam u tyaṃ daśa kṣipa'' ity ādityā ādityā vā imāḥ prajās tāsām eva madhyataḥ pratitiṣṭhati
gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
iṣovṛdhīyaṃ bhavati
paśavo vā iṣovṛdhīyaṃ paśūnām avarudhyā iṣe vai pañcamam ahar vṛdhe ṣaṣṭham avardhanta hy etarhi yajamānam evaitena vardhayanti
krauñcaṃ bhavati
kruṅṅ eṣyam ahar avindad eṣyam iva vai ṣaṣṭham ahar evaitena vindanti
vājadāvaryo bhavanti
annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai yadā hi vā annam atha gaur athāśvo 'tha puruṣo vājī
revatyo bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai
ṣaṇṇidhanī ṣaḍrātrasya dhṛtyai
āpo vai revatyas tā yat pṛṣṭhaṃ kuryur apaśur yajamānaḥ syāt paśūn asya nirdaheyur yatra vā āpo vivartante tad oṣadhayo jāyante 'tha yatrāvatiṣṭhante nirmṛtukās tatra bhavanti tasmāt pavamāne kurvanti parācā hi pavamānena stuvate
methī vā iṣovṛdhīyaṃ rajjuḥ krauñcaṃ vatso vājadāvaryo revatyo mātaro yad etāny evaṃ sāmāni kriyanta evam eva prattāṃ dugdhe
aukṣṇorandhre bhavataḥ
ukṣṇorandhro vā etābhyāṃ kāvyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vājajid bhavati sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvaṃ vā ete vājaṃ jayanti ye ṣaṣṭham ahar āgacchanti
annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai
varuṇasāma bhavati
etena vai varuṇo rājyam ādhipatyam agacchad yaśo 'bhavad rājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati yaśo bhavati varuṇasāmnā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
aṅgirasāṃ goṣṭho bhavati
paśavo vai revatyo gauṣṭham eva tat paśubhyaḥ paryasyanti tam evainān pravartayanty avisraṃsāya
ihavad vāmadevyaṃ bhavati
etena vai vāmadevo 'nnasya purodhām agacchad annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhā annasyāvarudhyai
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarñcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
marutvatyo gāyatryo bhavanti tad u traiṣṭubhād rūpān na yanti stomaḥ
yātayāmāny anyāni chandāṃsy ayātayāmā gāyatrī tasmād gāyatrīṣu stuvanti
''surūpa kṛtnum ūtaya'' ity abhyārambheṇa ṣaṭpadāḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai
''ubhe yad indra rodasī'' iti ṣaṭpadāḥ ṣaṣṭhasyāhno rūpaṃ tena ṣaṣṭham ahar ārabhante santatyai
revatīṣu vāravantīyaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati
apāṃ vā eṣa raso yad revatyo revatīnāṃ raso yad vāravantīyaṃ sarasā eva tad revatīḥ prayuṅkte yad vāravantīyena pṛṣṭhena stuvate
revad vā etad raivatyaṃ yad vāravantīyam asya revān revātyā jāyate
revān bhavati ya evaṃ veda
keśine vā etad dālbhyāya sāmāvir abhavat tad enam abravīd agātāro mā gāyanti mā mayodgāsiṣur iti kathaṃ ta āgā bhagava ity abravīd āgeyam evāsmy āgāyann iva gāyet pratiṣṭhāyai tad alammaṃ pārijānataṃ paścādakṣaṃ śayānam etām āgāṃ gāyantam ajānāt tam abravīt puras tvā dadhā iti tam abruvan ko nv ayaṃ kasmā alam ity alaṃ nu vai mahyam iti tad alammasyālammatvam
iheheti gāyet pratiṣṭhāyai
ṛṣabho raivato bhavati
paśavo vai raivatyaḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante
śyeno bhavati
śyeno ha vai pūrvapretāni vayāṃsy āpnoti pūrvapretānīva vai pūrvāṇy ahāni teṣām āptyai śyenaḥ kriyate
śyeno vā etad ahaḥ sampārayitum arhati sa hi vayasām āśiṣṭhas tasyānapahananāya sampāraṇāyaitat kriyate 'nto hi ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāhaḥ saptamaṃ ca
brahmavādino vadanti yad bṛhad āyatanāni pṛṣṭhāny athaite dve gāyatryau dve jagatyau kva tarhi bṛhatyo bhavantīti
ye dve jagatyoḥ pade te gāyatryā upasampadyete tat sarvā bṛhatyo bhavanty āyatane pṛṣṭhāni yātayatyāyatanavān bhavati
ṣaṭpadāsu stuvanti ṣaḍrātrasya dhṛtyai
saptapadayā yajati saptamasyāhnaḥ santatyai stomaḥ
''parisvāno giriṣṭhā'' iti parivatyo gāyatryo bhavanti sarvasya paryāptyai
''sasunveyo vasūnām'' iti paśavo vai vasu paśūnām avarudhyai
''taṃ vassakhāyo madāya-'' iti vālakhilyāḥ
vālakhilyāv etau tṛcau ṣaṣṭhe cāhani saptame ca
yad etau vālakhilyau tṛcau bhavato 'hnor eva vyatiṣaṅgayāvyatisraṃsāya santatyai
''somāḥ pavanta indava'' ity anuṣṭubho nibhasado bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai
''ayā pavā pavasvainā vasūni-'' iti triṣṭubhas satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brahmāṇam
vaidanvātāni bhavanti
vidanvān vai bhārgava indrasya pratyahaṃs taṃ śug ārcchat sa tapo 'tapyata sa etāni vaidanvatāny apaśyat taiḥ śucam apāhatāpaśucaṃ hate vaidanvatais tuṣṭuvānaḥ
bharadvājasya lomata bhavati
paśavo vai loma paśūnām avarudhyai
tad u dīrgham ity āhur āyur vai dīrgham āyuṣo 'varudhyai
kārṇaśravasaṃ bhavati śṛṇvanti tuṣṭuvānam
karṇaśravā vā etad āṅigarasaḥ paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjata yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati gaur:ivitasya brāhmaṇam
madhuścyunnidhanaṃ bhavati
paramasyānnādyasyāvarudhyai paramaṃ vā etad annādya yan madhu
prajāpater vā etau stanau yad ghṛtaścyunnidhanaṃ ca madhuścyunnidhanaṃ ca yajño vai prajāpatis tam etābhyāṃ dugdhe yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate taṃ dugdhe
krauñce bhavataḥ
śnauṣṭhaṃ bhavati
śnuṣṭir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāt lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
agner vā etad vaiśvānaraṃ sāma dīdihīti nidhanam upayanti dīdā eva hy agnir vaiśvānaraḥ
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
brahmavādino vadanti prāyaṇato dvipadāḥ kāryā udayanatā3 iti
udayanata eva kāryāḥ puruṣo vai dvipadāḥ pratiṣṭhāyai
vācā vai sarvaṃ yajñaṃ tanvate tasmāt sarvāṃ vācaṃ puruṣo vadati sarvā hy asmin saṃstutā pratitiṣṭhati
gūrdo bhavati
gopāyanānāṃ vai sattram āsīnānāṃ kirātakulyāv asuramāye antaḥparidhy asūn prākiratāṃ te ''agre tvan no antama'' ity agnim upāsīdaṃs tenāsūn aspṛṇvaṃs tad vāva te tarhy akāmayanta kāmasani sāma gūrdaḥ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
gotamasya bhandra bhavati
āśiṣam evāsmā etenāśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ
etena vai gotamo jemānaṃ mahimānam agacchat tasmād ye ca parāñco gotamād ye cārvāñcas ta ubhaye gotamā ṛṣayo bruvate
udvaṃśaputrā bhavati
yad vā udvaṃśīyaṃ tad udvaṃśaputraḥ
ardheḍām atisvarati
tasmād ūdhardhārā ati carantīḍāyām antataḥ paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
kḷpta upariṣṭād ṛk sāma ca vimucyete abhy u svareṇa saptamam ahaḥ svarati santatyai
ūhuṣīva vā etarhi vāg yadā ṣaḍahaḥ santiṣṭhate na bahu vaden nānyaṃ pṛcchen nānyasmai prabrūyāt
madhu vāśayed ghṛtaṃ vā yathehuṣo bahaṃ pratyanakti tathā tat
trayastriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai devatāsu vā eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ
āpyante vā etat stomāś chandāṃsi yat ṣaḍaha āpyate
āpte ṣaḍahe chandāṃsi stomān kṛtvā prayanti
''pra kāvyam uśanevara bruvāṇa'' iti gāyatryā rūpeṇa prayanti
iyaṃ vai gāyatry asyām eva pratiṣṭhāya prayanti
triṣṭup pratipad bhavati
ojo vīryaṃ triṣṭubojasyeva vīrye parākramya prayanti
stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
harivatyo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
dvādaśarcau bhavataḥ
dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaram eva tatpūrvasmai ṣaḍahāya pratyudyacchati savīvadhatāyai
caturviṃśatir bhavanti caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaram eva tatpūrvasmai ṣaḍahāya pratyudyacchati savīvadhatāyai
dṛta aindrota iti hovācābhipratārī kākṣasenir ye mahāvṛkṣasyāgraṃ gacchanti ka te tato bhavanti prarājan pakṣiṇaḥ patanty avāpakṣāḥ padyante
ye vai vidvāṃsas te pakṣiṇo ye 'vidvāṃsas te 'pakṣās trivṛt pañcadaśāv eva stomau pakṣau kṛtvā svarga lokaṃ prayanti
caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati teja se brahmavarcasāya
''mūrdhānaṃ divo aratim pṛthivyā'' ity āgreyam ājyaṃ bhavati
mūrdhā vā eṣa divo yas tṛtīyas trirātraḥ
''vaiśvānaram ṛta ājātam agnim'' iti vaiśvānara iti vā agneḥ priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainaṃ tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati
''pra vo mitrāya gāyata-'' iti dyāvāpṛthivīyaṃ maitrāvaruṇaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī vai mitrāvaruṇayoḥ priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainau tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati
''indrāyāhi citrabhānav'' ity ārbhavam aindram ṛbhavo vā indrasya priyaṃ dhāma priyeṇaivainaṃ tad dhāmnā parokṣam upaśikṣati
''tam īḍiṣva yo arciṣā-'' ity aniruktam aindrāgnaṃ devatānām anabhidharṣāyottamārdhe 'nirāha devatānām apraṇāśāya stomaḥ
''vṛṣā pavasva dhāraya-'' iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
vṛṣaṇvatyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
''punānaḥ soma dhāraya-'' iti dhṛtyai
''pro ayāsīd indur indrasya niṣkṛtam'' iti pravatyo bhavanti praṇinīṣeṇyam iva hy etad ahaḥ
jagatyaḥ satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
santani bhavati saptamasyāhnaḥ santatyai
yathā vai vyokasau vipradravata evam ete ṣaṣṭhaṃ cāhaḥ saptamaṃ ca vipradravatas tau yathā samānīya saṃyujyād evam evaite etena sāmnā saṃyunakti
yajño vai devebhyo 'pākrāmat sa suparṇarūpaṃ kṛtvācarat taṃ devā etaiḥ sāmabhirārabhanta yajña iva vā eṣa yac chandomā yajñasyaivaiṣa ārambhaḥ
rohitakūlīyaṃ bhavaty ājijityāyai
etena vai viśvāmitro rohitābhyāṃ rohitakūla ājim ajayat
viśvāmitro bharatānāṃ manassatyāyāt so 'dantibhir nāma janatayāṃśaṃ prāsyate māṃ māṃ yūyaṃ astikāṃ jayāthemāni mahyaṃ yūyaṃ pūrayātha yadīmāv idaṃ rohitāv aśmācitaṃ kūlam udvahāta iti sa ete sāmanī apaśyat tābhyāṃ yuktvā prāsedhat sa udjayat
ājir vā eṣa pratato yad dvādaśāhas tasyaite ujjityai
kaṇvarathantaraṃ bhavati tejo vā etad rathantarasya yat kaṇvarathantaram
sarasam eva tad rathantaraṃ prayuṅkte yat kaṇvarathantareṇa saptame 'hani stuvate
jāmi dvādaśāhasyāstīti ha smāhogradevo rājanir bārhataṃ ṣaṣṭham ahar bārhataṃ saptamaṃ yat kaṇvarathantaraṃ bhavati tenājāmi
gauṅgavaṃ bhavati
agnir akāmayatānnādaḥ syām iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad gauṅgavam apaśyat tenānnādo 'bhavad yad annaṃ vitvā gardadyad agaṅgūyat tad gauṅgavasya gauṅgavatvam annādyasyāvarudhyai gauṅgavaṃ kiyate
yat sāma devatā praśaṃyati tena yajamānāḥ satyāśiṣaḥ satyāśiṣo 'sāmeti vai sattram āsate satyāśiṣa eva bhavanti
āyāsyaṃ bhavati tiraścīnanidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai
ayāsyo vā āṅgirasa ādityānāṃ dīkṣitānām annam āśnāt sa vyabhraṃśata sa etāny āyāsyāny apaśyat tair ātmānaṃ samaśrīṇād vibhraṣṭam iva vai saptamam ahar yad etat sāma bhavaty ahar eva tena saṃśrīṇāti
pravadbhargavaṃ bhavati
''vayaṃ ghatvā sutāvanta'' iti bṛhatyo varṣīyaśchanda ākramate 'napabhraṃśāya
''nakiṣ ṭaṃ karmaṇā naśad'' iti bṛhatyaḥ satyo 'bhyārambheṇa jagatyaḥ
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yaj jyāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etā abhyārambheṇa jagatyo bhavanty ahna eva pratyuttambhāya
abhinidhanaṃ kāṇvaṃ bhavita
abhinidhanena vā indro vṛtrāya vajraṃ prāharat tam astṛṇuta stṛṇute bhrātṛvyam abhinidhanena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vaikhānasā vā ṛṣaya indrasya priyā āsaṃs tān rahasyur devamalimluḍ munimaraṇe 'mārayat taṃ devā abruvan kva tarṣayo 'bhūvānn iti tān praiṣam aicchat tān nāvindat sa imān lokān ekadhāreṇāpunāt tān munimaraṇe 'vindat tān etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vaikhānasaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe stomaḥ
''yas te mado vareṇya'' iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
''eṣasya dhārayā suta'' iti kakubhaḥ satyo 'bhyārambheṇa triṣṭubhaḥ
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yat jyāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etā abhyārambheṇa triṣṭubho bhavanty ahna eva pratyuttambhāya
''sakhāya āniṣīdata-'' iti vālakhilyā vālakhilyāv etau tṛcau ṣaṣṭhe cāhani saptame ca yad etau vākhilyau tṛcau bhavato 'hnor eva vyatiṣaṅgāyāvyavasraṃsāya santatyai
''purojitī vo andhasa'' iti virāḍ annaṃ virāḍ annādyasyāvarudhyai
''pra vājy akṣār'' ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtiḥ
atho etad dhy evaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ kriyante
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś chandomā ity etac chandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt
''ye somāsaḥ parāvati-'' iti parāvatam iva vā etarhi yajño gatas tam evaitenānvicchanti
dakṣaṇidhanaṃ bhavati
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmāt sṛṣṭā abalā ivācchadayaṃs tāsv etena sāmnā dakṣāyety ojo vīryam adadhād yad etat sāma bhavaty oja eva vīryam ātman dhatte
śārkaraṃ bhavati
indraṃ sarvāṇi bhūtāny astuvan sa śarkaraṃ śiśumārarṣim upetyābravīt stuhi meti so 'paḥ praskandann abravīd etāvato 'haṃ tvāṃ stuyām iti tasmād apāṃ vegam avejayat sa hīna ivāmanyata sa etat sāmāpaśyat tenāpo 'nusamāśnuta tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma śārkaraṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
plavo bhavati
samudraṃ vā ete prasnāntīty āhur ye dvādaśāham upayantīti yo vā aplavaḥ samudraṃ prarunāti na sa tata udeti yata plavo bhavati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
ativiśvāni duritā taremeti yad evaiṣāṃ duṣṭutaṃ duśśastaṃ tad etena taranti
ekādaśākṣaraṇidhano bhavaty ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub ojīvīryaṃ triṣṭub ojasy eva vīrye pratitiṣṭhati
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brahmaṇam
kārtayaśaṃ bhavati
hīti nidhanam upayanti pāpmano 'pahatyai
apa pāpmānaṃ hate kārtayaśena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
sāhaiviṣaṃ bhavati
suhavir vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
brahmāvādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś chandomā iti puruṣaś chandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadā chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
jarābodhīyaṃ bhavaty annādyasyāvarudhyai
annaṃ vai jarābodhīyaṃ mukhaṃ gāyatrī mukha eva tad annaṃ dhatte 'nnam atti
annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
iḍāntāḥ pāvamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍāḥ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ
''ā te vatso mano yamad'' ity apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yad ukthāni yad eti salomatvāyaiva
''tvaṃ na indrābhara-'' iti pūrṇāḥ kakubhaḥ
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yaj jayāyasaḥ stomāt kanīyāṃsaṃ stomam upayanti yad etāḥ pūrṇāḥ kakubho bhavanty anapabhraṃśāya
vatsaś ca vai medhātithiś ca kāṇvāv āstāṃ taṃ vatsaṃ medhātithir ākrośad abrāhmaṇo 'si śūdrāputra iti so 'bravīd ṛtenāgniṃ vyayāva yataro nau brahmīyān iti vātsena vatso vyain maidhātithena medhātithis tasya na loma ca nauṣat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma vātsaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
sauśravasaṃ bhavati
upagur vai sauśravasaḥ kutsasyauravasya purohita āsīt sa kutsaḥ paryaśapad ya indraṃ yajātā iti sa indraḥ suśravasam upetyābravīd yajasva māśanāyāmivā iti tam ayajata sa indraḥ puroḍāśas taḥ kutsam upetyābravīd ayakṣata mā kva te pariśaptam abhūd iti kas tvā yaṣṭeti suśravā iti sa kutsa aurava upāgāḥ sauśravasasyodgāyata audumbaryā śiro 'cchinat sa śuśravā indram abravīt tvattanād vai medam īdṛg upāgād iti tam etena sāmnā samairayat tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāma sauśravasaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
vīṅkaṃ bhavati
cyavano vai dādhīco 'śvinoḥ priya āsīt so 'jīryat tam etena sāmnāpsu vyaiṅkayatāṃ taṃ punaryuvānam akurutāṃ tad vāva tau tarhy akāmayetāṃ kāmasani sāma vīṅkaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
''śiśuṃ jajñānaṃ haryataṃ mṛjanti'' ity aṣṭam asy āhnaḥ pratid bhavati
śiśur iva vā eṣa saptamenāhnā jāyate tam aṣṭamenāhnā mṛjanti
stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
harivatyo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
navarcā bhavanti
pañcarco bhavati pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅktam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
bāṇavān bhavaty anto vai bāṇo 'nta etad aṣṭamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
trayas tṛcā bhavanti prāṇāpānānāṃ santatyai
''agniṃ vo devam agnibhiḥ sajoṣā'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
agnibhir ity eva pūrvāṇy ahāni abhi samiddhāny aṣṭamam ahar abhisamindhe
''mitraṃ vayaṃ havāmaha'' iti bārhataṃ maitrāvaruṇam
ugragādham iva vā etac chandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyātiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya
''tam indraṃ vājayāmasi-'' ity aindram
aṣṭamena vai devā ahnendram avājayan navamena pāpmānam aghnann ahar evaitena vājayanti
''indre agnā namo bṛhad'' iti bārhatam aindrāgnam
ugragādham iva vā etad yac chandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rape vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya stomaḥ
''adhvaryo adribhiḥ sutam'' iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai
gāyatryaḥ satyas triṣṭubhorūpeṇa traiṣṭubhaṃ hy etad ahaḥ
''abhi somāsa āyava'' ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ bṛhad iti bṛhata ubhayoḥ saha rūpam upaity ubhau hi varṇāv etad ahaḥ
''dhartā divaḥ pavate kṛtvyo rasa'' ity adhṛta iva vā eṣas tryaho yad dharteti dhṛtyā eva
jagatyas satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubho loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
vairūpaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai vairūpaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai virūpaḥ saṃvatsaro virūpam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
āśu bhārgavaṃ bhavati
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā āśunābhyadhinvaṃs tad āśor āśutvam
mārgīyavaṃ bhavati
devaṃ vā etaṃ mṛgayur iti vadanty etena vai sa ubhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam āśnutobhayeṣāṃ paśūnām ādhipatyam aśnute mārgīyaveṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
saumitraṃ bhavati
yad eva saumitrasya brāhmaṇam
aiṭataṃ bhavati
iṭan vā etena kāvyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
sākamaśvaṃ bhavati yad eva sākamaśvasya brāhmaṇam
tad u dhurāṃ sāmety āhuḥ prāṇā vai dhuraḥ prāṇānām avarudhyai
vilambasauparṇaṃ bhavati
ātmā vā eṣa sauparṇānāṃ yad aṣṭame 'hani pakṣāv etāv abhito bhavato ye saptamanavamayor vīva vā antarātmā pakṣau lambate yadantarātmā pakṣau vilambate tasmād vilambasauparṇam
svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai sauparṇaṃ kriyate
dvitīyaṃ hy etad rūpaṃ yac chandomāḥ
paśavo vai vāmadevyaṃ paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn saṃdadhāti
gāyatrapārśvaṃ bhavati
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā gāyatrapārśvena samatanvaṃs tasmād gāyatrapārśvam
trirātro yad vyaśīryata tam etaiḥ sāmabhir abhiṣajyan gāyatrapārśvenopāyacchan santaninā samatanvan saṃkṛtinā samaskurvan pratiṣṭhitau pūrvau trirātrāv apratiṣṭhita eṣa yad etāny eva sāmāni kriyanta etasyaiva pratiṣṭhityai
pauruhanmanaṃ bhavati
puruhanmā vā etena vaikhānaso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
abhyāghātyaṃ bhavaty abhyāghātyasāmāno hi chandomāḥ
dvaigataṃ bhavati
dvigad vā etena bhārgavo dviḥ svargaṃ lokam agacchad āgatya punar agacchat dvayoḥ kāmayor avarudhyai dvaigataṃ kriyate
hārāyaṇaṃ bhavati
indras tejaskāmo haraskāmas tapo 'tapyata, sa etad dhārāyaṇam apaśyat tena tejo haro 'vārundha tejasvī harasvī bhavati hārāyaṇena tuṣtuvānaḥ
achidraṃ bhavati
yad vā etasyāhnaś chidram āsīt tad devā acchidreṇāpy auhaṃs tad acchidrasyācchidratvam
bārhadukthaṃ bhavati
bṛhaduktho vā etena vāmneyo 'nnasya purodhām agacchad annaṃ vai brahmaṇaḥ purodhām annādyasyāvarudhyai
udvad bhārgavaṃ bhavati
pravatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyann udvatodāyan
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
''ka īṃ veda sute sacā-'' iti satobṛhatyaḥ
apabhraṃśa iva vā eṣa yas saptame 'hani satobṛhatyo bhavanti nāṣṭame tasmād aṣṭame kāryā anapabhraṃśāya
tadāhuḥ śithilam iva vā etac chando yat satobṛhātīty eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā bṛhatī yā punaḥpadā yad indra prāg apāg udag iti diśāṃ vimarśaḥ pratiṣṭityai
tāsu naipātithaṃ brahmasāma
sāmārṣeyavat svargāya yujyate svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
''ubhayaṃ śṛṇavac ca na'' iti
yac ca pṛṣṭhāni yāni caitāny ahāni teṣām ubhayeṣāṃ santatyai
tāsu vaiyaśvam
vyaśvo vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyā etat pṛṣṭhānām antataḥ kriyate stomaḥ
''pavasva deva āyuṣag indraṃ gacchatu te mada'' iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
''prāṇā śiśur mahīnām'' iti prāṇavatyo bhavanti prāṇān eva tad yajamāne dadhāti
''abhī no vājasātamam'' ity abhīti rathantarasya rūpaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
''pavasva soma mahān samudra'' ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtir atho etad dhy evaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ kriyante brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś chandomā ity etac chandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt
''hinvanti sūram usraya'' iti gāyatryaḥ satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāj jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
svāśirām arko bhavati
annaṃ vā arko 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai prāṇā vai svāśiraḥ prāṇānām arudhyai
surūpaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai surūpaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai
bhāsaṃ bhavati bhāti tuṣṭuvānaḥ
padanidhanaṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
svarbhānur vā āsura ādityaṃ tamasāvidhyat sa na vyarocata tasyātrir bhāsena tamo 'pāhan sa vyarocata yad vai tad bhā abhavat tad bhāsasya bhāsatvam
tama iva vā etāny ahāni yac chandomās tebhya etena sāmnā vivāsayati
kākṣīvataṃ bhavati
kākṣīvān vā etenauśijaḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati kākṣīvatena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
āsitaṃ bhavati
asito vā etena daivalas trayāṇāṃ lokānāṃ dṛṣṭim apaśyat trayāṇāṃ kāmānām avarudhyā āsitaṃ kriyate
aiṣiraṃ bhavati
traitaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai
padanidhanaṃ rāthantaraṃ rāthantaraṃ hy etad ahaḥ
nāthavindu sāma vindate nāthaṃ nāthavindūny etāny ahāni yat chandomā nātham evaitair vindate
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
kautsaṃ bhavati
etena vai kutso 'ndhaso vipānam apaśyat sa ha sma vai surādṛtinopavasathaṃ dhārayaty ubhayasyānnādyasyāvarudhyai kautsaṃ kriyate
śuddhāśuddhīyaṃ bhavati
indro yatīn sālāvṛkebhyaḥ prāyacchat tam aślīlā vāg abhyavadat so 'śuddho 'manyata sa etac chuddhāśuddhīyam apaśyat tenāśudhyac chudhyati śuddhāśuddhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
krauñcaṃ bhavati yad eva krauñcasya brāhmaṇaṃ yat dvitīye 'hani
rayiṣṭhaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai rayiṣṭhaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai
audalaṃ bhavati
udalo vā etena vaiśvāmitraḥ prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavaty audalena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś chandomā iti puruṣachandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadāś chandomānām ayātayāmatayau
viśoviśīyaṃ bhavati
agnir akāmayata viśo viśo 'tithis syāṃ viśo viśa ātithyam aśnuvīyeti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad viśoviśīyam apaśyat tena viśo viśo 'tithir abhavat viśo viśa ātithyam aśnuta viśo viśo 'tithir bhavati viśo viśa ātithyam aśnute viśoviśīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
iḍāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍā paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ
