''preṣṭhaṃ vo atithim'' ity ātithyasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
''aindra no gadhi priya-'' itīndriyasya vīryasyāvarudhyai
''purāṃ bhindur yuvā kavir amitaujā ajāyata/ indro viśvasya karmaṇo dhartā vajrī puruṣṭuta'' iti dhṛtyā eva
auśanaṃ bhavati
uśanā vai kāvyo 'kāmayata yāvān itareṣāṃ kāvyānāṃ lokas tāvantaṃ spṛṇuyām iti sa tapo 'tapyata sa etad auśanam apaśyat tena tāvantaṃ lokam aspṛṇod yāvān itareṣāṃ kāvyānām āsīt tad vāva sa tarhy akāmayata kāmasani sāmauśanaṃ kāmam evaitenāvarundhe
sāṃvartaṃ bhavati
devānāṃ vai yajñaṃ rakṣāṃsy ajighāṃsaṃs tāny etena indraḥ saṃvartam apāvapad yat saṃvartam apāvapat tasmāt sāṃvartaṃ pāpmā vāva sa tān asacata taṃ sāṃvartenāpāghnatāpa pāpmānaṃ hate sāṃvartena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
mārutaṃ bhavati
māsā vai raśmayo maruto raśmayo maruto vai devānāṃ bhūyiṣṭhā bhūyiṣṭhā asāmeti vai sattram āsate bhūyiṣṭhā eva bhavanty ṛtumanti pūrvāṇy ahāny anṛtavaḥ chandomā yad etat sāma bhavati tenaitāny ahāny ahāny ṛtumanti bhavanti
catuścatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavaty ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīrye triṣṭup
''akrān samudraḥ parame vidharmann'' iti navamasyāhnaḥ pratipad bhavati
paramaṃ vā etad ahar vidharma vidharma vā etad anyair aharbhir ahar yan navamaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ hi variṣṭham
''matsi vāyum iṣṭaye rādhase na'' iti vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇati tad eva tad avayajati
stotrīyas tṛco bhavati prāṇāpānānām avarudhyai
daśarco bhavati daśākṣarā virāṭa vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
saprabhṛtayo bhavāntīndriyasya vīryasya rasasyānaticārāya yatra vai devā indriyaṃ vīryaṃ rasam apaśyaṃs tad anunyatudan
aṣṭarco bhavati
aṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe
ṣaḍṛcā bhavanty ṛtūnāṃ dhṛtyai
catvāraḥ ṣaḍṛcā bhavanti caturviṃśatir ardhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati
savān uttamaḥ ṣaḍṛco bhavaty ubhayasya parokṣapratyakṣasyāvarudhyai
tṛca uttamo bhavati yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyanti
aṣṭācatvāriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
''aganma mahā namasā yaviṣṭham'' ity āgneyam ājyaṃ bhavati
gacchantīva vā ete ye navamam ahar gacchanti
''yo dīdāya samiddhasve duroṇa'' iti dīdāyeva hy eṣa yo navabhir aharbhis tuṣṭuvānaḥ ''svāhutam'' iti svāhuto hy eṣa yo navabhir aharbhir āhuto ''viśvataḥ pratyañcam'' iti viśvato hy eṣa pratyaṅ
''tvaṃ varuṇa uta mitro agna'' iti vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇati tad eva tad avayajati
''mitraṃ huve pūtadakṣam'' iti rāthantaraṃ maitrāvaruṇam
ugragādham iva vā etad yac chandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya
''mahāṃ indro ya ojasā-'' ity aindram aṣṭamena vai devā ahnendram avājayann avamena pāpmānam aghnann ahar evaitena mahayanti
''tā huve yayor idam'' iti rāthantaram aindrāgnam
ugragādham iva vā etad yac chandomās tad yathāta ugragādhe vyatiṣajya gāhanta evam evaitad rūpe vyatiṣajati chandomānām asaṃvyāthāya stomaḥ
''pavamānasya jighnato hareś candrā asṛkṣata'' iti harivatyo gāyatryo bhavanti chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
''pavamānasya jighnata'' iti vai bṛhato rūpaṃ ''hareś candrā asṛkṣata-'' iti jagatyā ubhayoḥ saharūpam upaiti sāmnaś ca chandasaś ca
''parīto ṣiñcatā sutam'' iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai navamam ahas tasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
''asāvi somo aruṣo vṛṣā harir'' iti jagatyas satyas triṣṭubho rūpeṇa tasmāt triṣṭubhāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
bharadvājasyādārasṛd bhavati
divodāsaṃ vai bharadvājapurohitaṃ nanājanāḥ paryayanta sa upāsīdad ṛṣe gātuṃ me vindeti tasmā etena sāmnā gātum avindad gātuvid vā etatsāmānena dāre nāsṛnmeti tad adārasṛto 'dārasṛttvaṃ vindate gātuṃ na dāre dhāvaty adārasṛtā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
surūpaṃ bhavati yad eva surūpasya brāhmaṇam
hariśrīnidhanaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai hariśriyaḥ paśūnām avarudhyai śriyaṃ ca haraś copaiti tuṣṭuvānaḥ
saindhukṣitaṃ bhavati yad eva saindhukṣitasya brāhmaṇam
gatanidhanaṃ vābhravaṃ bhavati gatyai
vabhrur vā etena kaumbhyo 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
iḍānāṃ saṃkṣāro bhavati
paśavo vā iḍā paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti
ṛṣabhaḥ pāvamāno bhavati
paśavo vai chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tan mithunam apyarjati prajātyai na ha vā anṛṣabhāḥ paśavaḥ prajāyante
pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati
pṛṣṭhaṃ vā etad ahnāṃ yan navamaṃ pṛṣṭha eva tat pṛṣṭhena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
kaulmalabarhiṣaṃ bhavati
kulmalabarhir vā etena svargaṃ lokam apaśyat prajātiṃ bhūmānam agacchat prajāyate bahur bhavati kaulmalabarhiṣeṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
arkapuṣpaṃ bhavati
annaṃ vai devā arka iti vadanti rasam asya puṣpām iti sarasam evānnādyam avarundhe 'rkapuṣpeṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
dairghyaśravasaṃ bhavati
dīrghaśravā vai rājanya ṛṣir jyog aparuddho 'śanāyaṃś caran sa etad dairghaśravasam apaśyat tena sarvābhyo digbhyo 'nnādyam avārundha sarvābhyo adigbhyo 'nnādyam avārundhe dairghaśravasena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vaiyaśvaṃ bhavati yad eva vaiyaśvasya brāhmaṇam
abhīśavaṃ yad ābhīśavasya
devasthānaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai saṃskṛti bhavati saṃṃskṛtyai
ahar vā etad avlīyata tad devā devasthāne tiṣṭhantaḥ saṃkṛtinā samaskurvaṃs tat saṃkṛteḥ saṃkṛtitvaṃ devasthānena vai devāḥ svarge loke pratyatiṣṭhan svarge loke pratitiṣṭām ety etat
varuṇāya devatā rājyāya nātiṣṭhanta sa etad devasthānam apaśyat tato vai tās tasmai rājyāyātiṣṭhanta tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śreṣṭhyāya
kṣatrasyevāsya prakāśo bhavati pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
bhargo bhargeṇa tuṣṭuvāno bhavati yaśo yaśasā
vāsiṣṭhaṃ bhavati yad eva vāsiṣṭhasya brāhmaṇam
dīrghatamaso 'rko bhavaty annaṃ vā arko 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai
sāmarājaṃ bhavati sāmrājyam ādhipatyaṃ gacchati sāmarājñā tuṣṭuvānaḥ
tad u saṃvad ity āhuḥ saṃvatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokaṃ prāyann udvatodāyan
nidhanāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanty ahno dhṛtyai stomaḥ
''śrāyanta iva sūryam'' iti sūryavatyo bhavanti
ādityadevatyaṃ hy etad ahar anto vai sūro 'nta etan navamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
''yata indra bhayāvahe tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi/ maghavañ chagdhi tava tan na ūtaye vidviṣo vimṛdho jahi-'' iti dviṣaś caiva mṛdhaś ca navamenāhnā vihatya daśamenāhnottiṣṭhanti
śrīr vai śrāyantīyaṃ śrīr navamam ahaḥ śriyam eva tac chriyāṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
samantaṃ bhavati
samantena paśukāmaḥ stuvīta purodhākāmaḥ samantena stuvīta
āgneyī pṛthivy āgneyo brāhmaṇa aindrī dyaur aindro rājanyo 'ntarikṣeṇa dyāvāpṛthivī samante antarikṣeṇaivainaṃ samantaṃ karoti vindate paśūn pra purodhām āpnoti ya evaṃ vidvān samantena stuvate stomaḥ
''tvaṃ somāsi dhārayur'' iti gāyatrī bhavaty ahno dhṛtyai tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
''tvaṃ hy aṅga daivyā'' iti tvam iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
''pavasva deva vītaya'' iti bṛhato rūpaṃ bārhataṃ hy etad ahaḥ
''parityaṃ haryataṃ harim'' iti parivatyo bhavanty anto vai navamam ahasyaitāḥ paryāptyai
''pavasva soma mahe dakṣāya-'' ity akṣarapaṅktiḥ stomānāṃ prabhūtir atho etad dhy evaitarhi chando 'yātayāma yad akṣarapaṅktis tena chandomā ayātayāmānaḥ kriyante brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś chandomā ity etac chandaso yad etā akṣarapaṅktaya iti brūyāt
''upoṣu jātam apturam'' iti gāyatryas satyo jagatyo rūpeṇa tasmāt jagatīnāṃ loke kriyante
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brahmaṇam
āśvasūktaṃ bhavati
agniṃ vai pūrvair aharbhir ājuhoty athaitad ādityadaivatyam ahaḥ śukra āhuta ity asau vā ādityaḥ śukras tam evaitenājuhoti
śāmmadaṃ bhavati
śammad vā etenāṅgiraso 'ñjasā svargaṃ lokam apaśyat svargasya lokasyānukhyātyai svargāl lokān na cyavate tuṣṭuvānaḥ
āśiṣam evāsmā etenāśāste sāma hi satyāśīḥ
dāvasur vā etad āṅgirasaḥ paśukāmaḥ sāmāpaśyat tena sahasraṃ paśūn asṛjat yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnāṃ puṣṭyai
pratīcīneḍaṃ kāśītaṃ bhavati
parācībhir vā anyābhir iḍābhī reto dadhad athaitat pratīcīneḍaṃ kāśītaṃ prajātyai tasmāt parāñco garbhāḥ sambhavanti pratyañcaḥ prajāyante tasmād ute 'vācīnabilebhyo nāvapadyanta etena hy eva te dhṛtāḥ
hāviṣkṛtaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai kṛtānuvāda eva saḥ
sauparṇaṃ bhavati yad eva sauparṇasya brahmaṇam
vaiśvamanasaṃ bhavati
viśvamanasaṃ vā ṛṣim adhyāyam udvrajitaṃ rakṣo 'gṛhṇāt tam indro 'cāyad ṛṣiṃ vai rakṣo 'grahīd iti tam abhyavadad ṛṣe kas tvaiṣa iti, sthāṇur iti brūhīti rakṣo 'bravīt, sa sthāṇur ity abravīt tasmai vā etena praharety asmā iṣīkāṃ vajraṃ prayacchann abravīt tenāsya sīmānam abhinat saiṣendreṇateṣīkā pāpmā vāva sa tam agṛhṇāt taṃ vaiśvamanasenāpāhatāpapāpmānaṃ hate vaiśvamanasena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati yad eva gaurīvitasya brāhmaṇam
nihavo bhavaty annādyasyāvarudhyai
hīti vā annaṃ pradīyata īty āgrir annam atti
ṛṣayo vā indraṃ pratyakṣa nāpaśyan sa vasiṣṭho 'kāmayata katham indraṃ pratyakṣaṃ paśyeyam iti sa etan nihavam apaśyat tato vai sa indraṃ pratyakṣam apaśyat, sa enam abravīd brāhmaṇaṃ te vakṣyāmi yathā tvatpurohitā bharatāḥ prajaniṣyante 'tha mānyebhya ṛṣibhyo mā pravoca iti tasmā etān stomabhāgān abravīt tato vai vasiṣṭhapurohitā bharatāḥ prājāyanta sendraṃ vā etat sāma yad etat sāma bhavati sendratvāya
yad vāhiṣṭhīyaṃ bhavati
brahmayaśasaṃ vā etāni sāmāny ṛcā śrotrīyāṇi brahmāyaśasī bhavati yad vāhiṣṭhīyena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
āsitaṃ bhavati yad evāsitasya brāhmaṇam
sādhraṃ bhavati siddhyai
ākūpāraṃ bhavati
akūpāro vā etena kaśyapo jemānaṃ mahimānam agacchaj jemānaṃ mahimānaṃ gacchaty ākūpāreṇa tuṣṭuvānaḥ
vidharma bhavati dharmasya vidhṛtyai
brahmavādino vadanti yat ṣaḍahe stomāś chandāṃsy āpyante kiṃ chandasaś chandomā iti puruṣacchandasa iti brūyāt puruṣo vai pāṅktaḥ puruṣo dvipadā chandomānām ayātayāmatāyai
śrudhyaṃ bhavati
paśavo vai śrudhyaṃ paśūnām avarudhyai
prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān etena sāmnā śrūdhiyā ehiyety anvahvayat ta enam upāvartanta yad etat sāma bhavati paśūnām upāvṛtyai
upainaṃ paśava āvartante ya evaṃ veda
gāyatrīṣu stuvanti pratiṣṭhāyai brahmavarcasāya yenaiva prāṇena prayanti tam abhyudyantīḍāntāḥ pavamānā bhavanti paśavo vā iḍā paśavaś chandomāḥ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti stomaḥ
āgreyīṣu pūrveṣām ahnām ukthāni praṇayanty athaitasyāhna āgneyy aindrayāṃ praṇayanty ubhayor eva rūpayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati
aidhmavāhaṃ bhavati
āgneyy aindrīṣu stuvanti brahma caiva tat kṣatraṃ ca sayujīkaroti brahmaiva kṣatrasya purastān nidadhāti brāhmaṇe kṣatraṃ ca viśaṃ cānuge karoti
traikakubhaṃ bhavati
ojasy eva tad vīrye pratitiṣṭhaty ojo vīryaṃ traikakubham
udvaṃśīyaṃ bhavati yad evodvaṃśīyasya brāhmaṇam
aṣṭācatvāriṃśaṃ eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai prajātyai
gāyatraṃ vai saptamam ahas traiṣṭubham aṣṭamaṃ jāgataṃ navamam athaitad ānuṣṭubham ahar yad daśamam
tad āhur yad ānuṣṭubhaṃ stomyāṃ pratyakṣam upeyuḥ parāṃ parāvataṃ yajamāno gacchen na pratitiṣṭhed iti yā vai caturviṃśatir gāyatryas tā aṣṭādaśānuṣṭubho 'nuṣṭubham eva tat stomyāṃ parokṣam upayanti pratiṣṭhāyai pratitiṣṭhati
prajāpatiṃ vā etenāhnā pariveviṣati tatra vyavavadyaṃ yad vai śreṣṭhe pariviṣyamāṇo vadaty annādyasya so 'vagrahas tasmān na vyavavadyam annādyasyānavagrāhāya
tad u vyavavadyaṃ yathā śreṣṭhāya baliṃ hriyamāṇaṃ panthānaṃ paryanuvedayati gatyai tathā tat
yāvaty anuṣṭup tāvatīṃ vācaṃ sampādya vibrūyus tad v anatiriktaṃ svasyo caiva yajñasyāriṣṭyai
abhi vā ete devān ārohantīty āhur ye daśabhir aharbhiḥ stuvata iti pañcānām ahnām anurūpaiḥ pratyavayanti yathābhyāruhya pratyavarohet tathā tan navarco bhavati yā evāmūḥ prayacchan yā avadadhāti tā etā udasyati
vāruṇy eṣā bhavati yad vai yajñasya duriṣṭaṃ tad varuṇo gṛhṇāti tad eva tad avayajaty ādityaiṣā bhavatīyaṃ vā aditir asyām eva pratitiṣṭhati
caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmarcasāya
''suṣamiddho na āvaha-'' ity āpriya ājyāni bhavanti
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricānāmanyata sa etāny āpriya ājyāny apaśyat tair ātmānam āprīṇāt dugdha iva vā eṣa riricāno yo daśabhir aharbhis tuṣṭuvāno yad etāny āpriya ājyāni bhavanty ātmānam evaitair āprīṇāti
''yad adya sūra udita'' iti sūravan maitrāvaruṇam
anto vai sūro 'nta etad daśamam ahnām anta eva tadantena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
''ut tvā madantu somā'' ity udvad aindram utthānasya rūpam
''indrāgnī āgataṃ sutam'' iti yenaiva rūpeṇa prayanti tad abhyudyanti stomaḥ
''uccā te jātam andhasa'' ity udvatyo gāyatryo bhavanty utthānasya rūpam
''punānas soma dhāraya-'' iti panthānam eva tat paryavayanti
''ā jāgṛvir vipra ṛtaṃ matīnām'' iti yad āpte pravatīḥ kuryur atipadyer anyad āvatyo bhavanty anatipādāya
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
āmahīyavaṃ bhavati kḷptiś cānnādyaṃ ca kḷptiṃ caivaitenānnādyaṃ cābhyuttiṣṭhanti
ājigaṃ bhavaty ājijityāyai
ājir vā eṣa pratato yat dvādaśāhas tasyaitad ujjityai
ābhīkaṃ bhavaty abhikrāntyai
āṅgirasas tapas tepānāḥ śucam aśocaṃs ta etat sāmāpaśyaṃs tān abhīke 'bhyavarṣat tena śucam aśamayanta yad abhīke 'bhyavarṣat tasmād ābhīkaṃ yām eva pūrvair aharbhiḥ śucaṃ śocanti tām etenānna śamayitvottiṣṭhanti
utsedho bhavati
utsedhena vai devāḥ paśūn udasedhan niṣedhena paryagṛhṇan
antarotsedhaniṣedhau yajñāyajñīyam
paśavo 'nnādyaṃ yajñāyajñīyaṃ paśūn eva tad annādyam utsedhaniṣedhābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāti
mādhyandine vai pavamāne devā yajñāyajñīyena yajñaṃ saṃsthāpya svargaṃ lokam ārohaṃs tad ya evaṃ veda mādhyandina evaitat pavamāne yajñāyajñīyena yajñaṃ saṃsthāpya svargaṃ lokam ārohati
atho parokṣam anuṣṭubhaṃ sampadyate 'har eṣā vai pratyakṣam anuṣṭup yad yajñāyajñīyaṃ tad yat tṛtīyasavane kuryuḥ pratyakṣam anuṣṭubham ṛccheyus tasmān mādhyandine kurvanti tena parokṣam anuṣṭubham upayanti
gaurīvitaṃ bhavati
etad vai yajñasya śvastanaṃ yad gaurīvitam etad āyatano yajamāno yan madhyandino yad gaurīvitaṃ madhyandine bhavati śvastanam eva tad yajamāna ātman dhatte stomaḥ
''kayā naś citra ābhuvad'' iti kavatyas tena prājāpatyāḥ ko hi prajāpatiḥ prajāpater āptyai
''mā cid anyad viśaṃsata-'' ity utthānam eva tad āśiṣo hy etarhi
''ud u tye madhumattamā'' ity udvatya udayanīye 'hany etad āśiṣo hy evaitarhi
''tarobhir vo vidadvasum'' iti stomo vai taro yajño vidadvasuḥ stomena vai yajño yujyate yat tarobhir vo vidadvasum ity āha yajñam eva tad yunakti
vāmadevyasyarkṣu rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati
gāyatrī vai rathantarasya yoniḥ svāyām eva tad yonau rathantaraṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
tejo vai gāyatrī chandasā tejo rathantaraṃ sāmnā tejaś caturviṃśastomānāṃ teja eva tat samyak saṃdadhāty api ha putrasya putras tejasvī bhavati
aṣṭākṣareṇa prathamāyā ṛcaḥ prastauty aṣṭāśaphāṃs tatpaśūn avarundhe
dyvakṣareṇottarayor ṛcoḥ prastauti dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu pratiṣṭhāpayati
gāyatraṃ vai rathantaraṃ gāyatracchando yad gāyatrīṣu rathantaram bhavati tena svāyāṃ janatāyām ṛdhnotīme vai lokā gāyatrī yad gāyatrīṣu rathantaraṃ bhavatīmān eva tal lokān samāpyottiṣṭhanti
maidhātithaṃ bhavati
etena vai medhātithiḥ kāṇvo vibhindukād vyūdhnīr gā udasṛjata paśūnām avarudhyai maidhātithaṃ kriyate
abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavaty ekākṣaranidhanaḥ pratiṣṭhāyai
ekākṣarā vai vāg vācy eva pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhanti
kāleyam acchāvākasāma bhavati
samānaloke vai kāleyaṃ ca rathantaraṃ ceyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ paśavaḥ kāleyam asyāṃ caiva paśuṣu ca pratiṣṭhāyottiṣṭhanti stomaḥ
''svādiṣṭhayā madiṣṭhayā-'' iti gāyatrī bhavati madavad vai rasavat tṛtīyasavanaṃ madam eva tad rasaṃ dadhāti
gāyatraṃ bhavati yad eva gāyatrasya brāhmaṇam
saṃhitaṃ bhavati dyvakṣaraṇidhanaṃ pratiṣṭhāyai pratiṣṭhāyaivottiṣṭhanti
saphaṃ bhavati
saphena vai devā imān lokān samāpnuvant samāpnuvaṃs tat saphasya saphatvam imān evaitena lokān samāpyottiṣṭhanti
rohitakūlīyaṃ bhavati yad eva rohitakūlīyasya brāhmaṇam
śyāvāśvāndhīgave bhavataḥ samīcyau virājau dadhāty annādyāya
pipīlikāmadhyāsu stuvanti
indro vṛtraṃ hatvā nāstṛṣīti manyamānaḥ parāṃ parāvatam agacchat sa etām anuṣṭubhaṃ vyauhat tāṃ madhye vyavāsarpad indragṛhe vā eṣo 'bhaye yajate abhaya uttiṣṭhati ya evaṃ vidvān etāsu stuvate
yajñāyajñīyanidhanaṃ sauhaviṣaṃ bhavati yajñāyajñīyād eva tat tṛtīyasavene na yanti
vājajid bhavati
sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvaṃ vā ete vājaṃ jayanti ye daśamam ahar āgacchanty annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai
daśākṣaraṃ nidhanam upayanti daśarātrasya dhṛtyai daśākṣarā virāḍ vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
sūryavatīṣu stuvanty anto vai sūro 'nta etad daśamam ahnām anta eva tad antena stuvate pratiṣṭhāyai
upavatyo bhavanti pratiṣṭhāyai parivatyo bhavanti sarvasya paryāptyai
caturviṃśa eva stomo bhavati tejase brahmavarcasāya
virāṭsu vāmadevyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavati śāntyai kḷptyai
sad vai vāmadevyaṃ sāmnāṃ sad virāṭ chandasāṃ sat trayastriṃśaḥ stomānāṃ satām antān saṃdhāyottiṣṭhanty api ha putrasya sattvam aśnute
brahmavādino vadanti yatas sattrād udasthātā3 sthitā3d iti yad yata iti brūyur apratiṣṭhānā aprajaso bhaviṣyantīty enān brūyād yat sthitād iti brūyuḥ sthāyukaiṣāṃ śrīr bhaviṣyati na vasīyāṃso bhaviṣyantīty enān brūyāt pūrṇād eva pūrṇam abhyudasthāmeti brūyuḥ
ete vai pūrṇāt pūrṇam abhyuttiṣṭhanti ye vāmadevyena stutvottiṣṭhanti
antarikṣaṃ vai vāmadevyam antarikṣeṇedaṃ sarvaṃ pūrṇam
eṣa vai samṛddhaḥ stomo yat trayastriṃśas trayastriṃśadakṣarāsu samṛddhāv eva pratitiṣṭhanti
sarveṣāṃ vā etāś chandasāṃ rūpaṃ yāt tripadās tena gāyatryo yad ekādaśākṣarāṇi padāni tena triṣṭubho yat dvādaśākṣaraṃ padaṃ tena jagatyo yat trayastriṃśadakṣarās tena virājas tenaiva cānuṣṭubho na hy ekasmād akṣarād virādhayanti
trayastriṃśa eva stomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyai devatāsu vā eṣa pratiṣṭhitaḥ
prajāpatir vā idam eka āsīn nāhar āsīn na rātrir āsīt so 'sminn andhe tamasi prāsarpat sa aicchat sa etam abhyapadyata tato vai tasmai vyaucchad vyuṣṭir vā eṣa āhriyate yad vai taj jyotir abhavat tat jyotiṣo jyotiṣṭvam
eṣa vāva prathamo yajñānāṃ ya etenāniṣṭvāthānyena yajate gartapatyam eva taj jīyate pra vā mīyate
yathā vā idam agner jātād agnayo vihriyanta evam etasmād adhy anye yajñā vihriyante
yo hi trivṛd anyaṃ yajñakratum āpadyate sa taṃ dīpayati yaḥ pañcadaśaḥ sa taṃ yaḥ saptadaśaḥ sa taṃ ya ekaviṃśaḥ sa tam
etat tad yad āhur eko yajña ity etad dhi sarve jyotiṣṭomā bhavanti
asthūrir vā eṣa santato yajño dvau dvau hi stomau savanaṃ vahatas trivṛt pañcadaśau prātaḥsavanaṃ pañcadaśasaptadaśau mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saptadaśaikaviṃśau tṛtīyasavanam
yā mitadakṣiṇaiva syād eṣa eva kārya iyaṃ vai jyotir iyam amitasya yantrikaiṣā vā etaṃ yantum arhati
tasya navatiśataṃ stotrīyās tāsāṃ yā aśītiśataṃ tāḥ ṣaṭtriṃśinyo virājaḥ ṣaḍ ṛtava ṛtuṣv eva virājā pratitiṣṭhati
atha yā daśaiṣā vā ātmanyā virāḍ etasyāṃ vā idaṃ puruṣaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
gauś cāśvaś cāśvataraś ca gardabhaś cājāś cāvayaś ca vrīhayaś ca yavāś ca tilāś ca māṣāś caitasyām eva virāji pratitiṣṭhati
tasya dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇāḥ
vīrahā vā eṣa devānāṃ yaḥ somam abhiṣuṇoti yāḥ śataṃ vairaṃ tad devān avadayate 'tha yā daśa daśa prāṇāḥ prāṇāṃs tābhiḥ spṛṇoti yaikādaśyātmānaṃ tayā yā dvādaśī saiva dakṣiṇā
śleṣma vā etad yajñasya yad dakṣiṇā na vā aśleṣmā ratho vahaty atha śleṣmavatā yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam abhyaśnuta evam etena dakṣiṇāvatā yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam abhyaśnute
śubho vā etā yajñasya yad dakṣiṇā yad dakṣiṇāvatā yajate śubham evāsmin dadhāti
athaiṣa gauḥ
gavā vai devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo 'nudantaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ nudate ya evaṃ veda
yad vai tad devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo govayaṃs tad gor gotvam
govayati pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ ya evaṃ veda
tasya pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ vajro vai pañcadaśo vajram eva tat purastān nidadhāti tena vijayate
paśustomo vā eṣa evam iva vai paśuḥ samāhitaḥ śiraḥ sthavīyo 'ṇīyas yo grīvā pārśvābhyāṃ varīyāṃ sakthibhyāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
yat pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati trivṛt tyājyāni saptadaśa mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ rūpeṇaivainaṃ tat samardhayati
ekā saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyate tasmāt paśoḥ paścād atiriktam
athaiṣa gauḥ
gavā vai devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo 'nudantaibhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ nudate ya evaṃ veda
yad vai tad devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo govayaṃs tad gor gotvam
govayati pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ ya evaṃ veda
tasya pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ vajro vai pañcadaśo vajram eva tat purastān nidadhāti tena vijayate
paśustomo vā eṣa evam iva vai paśuḥ samāhitaḥ śiraḥ sthavīyo 'ṇīyasyo grīvā pārśvābhyāṃ varīyāṃsakthibhyāṃ variṣṭhaḥ
yat pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati trivṛnty ājyāni saptadaśa mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ rūpeṇaivainaṃ tat samardhayati
ekā saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyate tasmāt paśoḥ paścād atiriktam
athaiṣa āyuḥ
āyuṣā vai devā asurān āyuvatāyute bhrātṛvyaṃ ya evaṃ veda
svargakāmo yajeta
ūrdhvāḥ stomā yanty anapabhraṃśāya
etenaivāmayāvinaṃ yājayed atirātraḥ kāryaḥ
sa gāyatrīṃ saṃpadyate prāṇo gāyatry āyur eṣa āyuś caivāsmin prāṇaṃ cobhe samīcī dadhāti
svargyā vā ete stomā yat jyotir bhavati jyotir evāsmai sa purastād dharaty athaiṣa gaur ekayā virājam atirikta ārambhaṇam eva tad athaiṣa āyur ekasyā virāja ūna āsāda eva so 'tho ūnātiriktau stomau mithunau prajātyai
ete vai trikadrukāḥ stomā etair vā indraḥ sarvāṃ tṛptim atṛpyat
tṛpyati prajayā paśubhir ya evaṃ veda
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmai śraiṣṭhyāya nātiṣṭhanta sa āsāṃ diśāṃ prajānāṃ ca rasaṃ pravṛhya srajaṃ kṛtvā pratyamuñcata tato 'smai prajāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta
tiṣṭhante 'smai samānāḥ śraiṣṭhyāya ya evaṃ veda
so 'kāmayatendro me prajāyāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ syād iti tām asmai srajaṃ pratyamuñcat tato vā indrāya prajāḥ śraiṣṭhyāyātiṣṭhanta tac chilpaṃ paśyantyo yat pitary apaśyan
tasmād yaḥ putrāṇāṃ dāyaṃ dhanatamam ivopaiti taṃ manyante 'yam evedaṃ bhaviṣyatīti
tato vā idam indro viśvam ajayad yad viśvam ajayat tasmād viśvajit
so 'kāmayata yan me 'nabhijitaṃ tad abhijayeyam iti sa etam abhijitam apaśyat tenānabhijitam abhyajayat
yad abhijid bhavaty anābhijitasyābhijityai
tau vā etāv indrastomau vīryavantau śilpaṃ vā etau nāma stomāv āstām
paśyate gṛhe śilpaṃ ya evaṃ veda
na vai yamau nāma stomau sto yo yamābhyāṃ yajetaitābhyāṃ yajeta samṛdhyai
punarabhyāvartaṃ stomā bhavanti punarabhyāvartaṃ hy etābhyām indro 'jitam ajayat
trīṃs trivṛdabhijitaḥ praṇayati trīn pañcadaśaḥ trīn saptadaśaḥ trīn ekaviṃśas te dvādaśa saṃpadyante dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti
caturas trivṛdviśvajitaḥ praṇayati caturaḥ pañcadaśaś caturaḥ saptadaśas te dvādaśa saṃpadyante dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti
''upa tvā jāmayo gira'' ity upavatī pratipad bhavati stomasya rūpam
prāṇair vā eṣa vyṛdhyata ity āhur yaḥ sarvaṃ dadāti sarvān stomān sarvāṇi pṛṣṭhāny upaitīti yad vāyavyā bhavati prāṇānāṃ samṛdhyai
sarasvataś ca sarasvatyāś cottare bhavataḥ
mithunaṃ vā etad yat sarasvāṃś ca sarasvatī ca mithunam evāsya yajñamukhe dadhāti prajananāya
sāvitrī caturthī bhavati
duṣkaraṃ vā eṣa karoti yaḥ sarvaṃ dadāti yat sāvitrī bhavati savitṛprasṛtaṃ me karmāsad iti savitṛprasūtam evāsya karma bhavati
brāhmaṇaspatyā pañcamī bhavati
brahma vai brahmaṇaspatir brahmaivāsya yajñamukhe dadhāti
āgnipāvamānī ṣaṣṭhī bhavati
agnir evainaṃ niṣṭapati pavamānaḥ punāti pūtam evainaṃ yajñiyaṃ pṛṣṭhāny upanayati
yanti vā ete patha ity āhur ye saṃbhāryāḥ kurvate
pāvamāna uttamas tṛco bhavati tena patho nayanti
sa tu vai pṛṣṭhaiḥ stuvītety āhur ya etāni bahiṣpavamāne yuñjyād iti
upavatī pratipad bhavaty upa vai rathantaraṃ rathantaram evāsmai tayā yunakti
sarasvatī dvitīyā bhavati svargo lokaḥ sarasvān svargo loko bṛhad bṛhad evāsmai tayā yunakti
sarasvatyās tṛtīyā bhavati vāg vai sarasvatī vāg vairūpaṃ vairūpam evāsmai tayā yunakti
sāvitrī caturthī bhavati prajāpatir vai savitā prajāpatir vairājaṃ vairājam evāsmai tayā yunakti
brāhmaṇaspatyā pañcamī bhavati brahma vai brahmaṇaspatir brahma śakvaryaḥ śakvarīr evāsmai tayā yunakti
āgnipāvamānī ṣaṣṭhī bhavati gāyatrī vai revatī gāyatracchandā agnī revatīr evāsmai tayā yunakti
na catvāri ṣaḍbhyo vibhavanti yad aniruktāni tena vibhavanti
sarvāṇi svārāṇy ājyāni taj jāmi nānādevatyaiḥ stuvanty ajāmitāyai
''suṣamiddho na āvaha-'' ity āpriya ājyāni bhavanti
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata sa dugdho riricāno 'manyata sa etāny āpriya ājyāny apaśyat tair ātmānam [thus BI; KSS ātmanam] āprīṇād dugdha iva vā eṣa riricāno yaḥ sarvaṃ dadāti yad āpriya ājyāni bhavanty ātmānam evaitair āprīṇāti
etarhi tu vai pṛṣṭhāni yathāyatanaṃ kalpanta ity āhur yad rathantaraṃ prathamaṃ bṛhad uttamaṃ madhya itarāṇīti
jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyata ity āhur yat sarvāṇi nidhanavanti saha kriyanta iti yad antarā somā yanty antarokthāni śasyante 'ntarā vaṣaṭkurvanti tenājāmi
vyatyāsam iḍāś ca nidhanāni cāhus tenājāmi
cyavante vā etad revatyaḥ svād āyatanād ity āhur yat trayastriṃśāt stomād yantīti yad gāyatryo bhavanti tenāyatanān na cyavante yā hi kā ca gāyatrī sā revatī
paraśubhir vā eṣa vyṛdhyata ity āhur yaḥ sarvaṃ dadāti tac chavīṃ paridhatte paśubhir eva samṛdhyate
rohiṇī chavī bhavaty etad vai paśunāṃ bhūyiṣṭhaṃ rūpaṃ yad rohitaṃ sākṣād evainān avarundhe
araṇye tisro vasaty āraṇyaṃ tābhir annādyam avarundhe
udumbare vasaty ūrg udumbara ūrjam evāvarundhe
khanitreṇa jīvaty avṛttim apajayati
ubhayataḥkṣṇud abhrir bhavaty ubhayata evāsmā annādyaṃ rajaty asmāc ca lokād amuṣmāc ca
niṣādeṣu tisro vasaty asyāṃ vā ete parīttā yad evāsyām annādyaṃ tad avarundhe
jane tisro vasati janyaṃ tābhir annādyam avarundhe
samānajane tisraḥ samānajanyaṃ tābhiḥ
dvādaśaitā rātrayo bhavanti dvādaśamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaram anv annādyaṃ prajāyate tad evāptvāvarundhe
saṃvatsaraṃ na yāced āmādyam iva vā etad yaḥ sadyodattaṃ pratyatti sadyo vai devānaṃ saṃvatsaraḥ
nodīyamānaṃ prati nuden nādyasyāpratinodāya
uṣṇīṣaṃ bibharti śilpatvāya
na mṛnmayena pibed āhutir vā eṣā yad brāhmaṇasya mukhaṃ na vai mṛnmayam āhutim ānaśe 'tha yad amṛnmayapo bhavati sva eva mukha āhutiṃ juhoti
pañcaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
sarvajitā vai devāḥ sarvam ajayan sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati
tasya mahāvrataṃ pṛṣṭham
arkyaṃ śasyate
caturviṃśatiḥ saṃvatsarasyārdhamāsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ pañcaviṃśo 'nnaṃ vrataṃ saṃvatsarād etenānnādyam avarundhe
annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
etena vai gaurāṅgirasaḥ sarvaṃ pāpmānam atarat sarvaṃ pāpmānaṃ taraty etena stomena tuṣṭuvānaḥ
athaiṣa jyotiḥ
parāṅ vai trirātro 'rvāṅ agniṣṭomo yas trirātre vibhraṃśate na tasmin punar asty atha yo 'gniṣṭome prāyaścittimat tad api hy etenaikaviṃśatidakṣiṇena punar yajeta yasmin hy eva yajñakratau vibhraṃśate saiva tasya prāyaścittiḥ
upasadi sahasraṃ prātaranuvākam anvāha tad asau lokaḥ sahasraṃ dakṣiṇās tad antarikṣaṃ sahasram etāny akṣarāṇi tad ayaṃ loka eṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
ṛksthā vā anyat sahasram ity āhur akṣaresthā anyad iti yat trirātre dīyate tadṛksthā/ atha yad agniṣṭome tad akṣaresthā
yat sahasrākṣarāsu brahmasāma bhavati sahasrasyaiva sā pratiṣṭutiḥ
yāvad vai sahasraṃ gāva uttarādharā ity āhus tāvad asmāt lokāt svargo loka iti tasmād āhuḥ sahasrayājī vā imān lokān prāpnoti
paśubhir vā eṣa vyṛdhyata ity āhur yaḥ sadyaḥ sahasraṃ dadātīti paṅktiṣu brahmasāma bhavati pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktāḥ paśavo yajña eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
trivṛtaṃ stomaṃ saṃpadyate virājaṃ chandaḥ
prāṇo vai trivṛd annaṃ virāṭ na vai prāṇa ṛte 'nnāt pārayati nānnam ṛte prāṇāt prāṇeṣu caivānnādye ca pratitiṣṭhati
athaiṣa sarvajyotiḥ sarvasyāptiḥ sarvasya jitiḥ sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati
paramo vā eṣa yajñaḥ paramaṃ sahasraṃ paramatāṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
tasya dviśatāḥ stotrīyā anto vai vāco dviśatamantaḥ sahasramanta eva tad antaṃ pratiṣṭāpayati
kṛtastomo vā eṣa sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati sarvaṃ hi kṛtena jayati
virājaṃ saṃpadyate 'nnaṃ virāḍ annādyam evāvarundhe
ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo 'ntata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati
athaiṣa viśvajyotir ukthyaḥ
paśavo vā ukthāni paśavo viśvaṃ jyotir viśva eva jyotau paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
aharbhir vai trirātra imān lokān āpnoti savanair eṣa uttamam uttaraṃ trirātrasyāhar varṣīya uttaram uttaram etasya savanaṃ varṣīyas tena trirātram āpnoty uttara uttara eṣāṃ lokānāṃ jyāyāṃs tenemān lokān āpnoti
asthūrir vā eṣa santato yajño dvau dvau hi stomau savanaṃ vahataḥ
trivṛtpañcadaśau prātaḥsavanaṃ saptadaśapañcaviṃśau mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ caturviṃśaikaviṃśau tṛtīyasavanam
yad vai yukte santata ādhīyate vahati tadyathā yukte santata ādadhyād evam etasmin sahasram ādhīyate
ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavataḥ
iyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ dyaur bṛhad evāsmāl lokād gāyaty evāmuṣmād ubhayor anayor lokayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati
anuṣṭubhy ātharvaṇaṃ bhavati
bheṣajaṃ vai devānām atharvāṇo bheṣajāyaivāriṣṭyai
udvaṃśīyam ukthānām antato bhavati sarveṣāṃ vā etat pṛṣṭhānāṃ rūpaṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
uktho bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni paśavaḥ sahasraṃ paśuṣv eva tat paśūn dadhāti
yo vā agniṣṭome trirātraṃ protaṃ vidyāt so 'gniṣṭome sahasraṃ dadyāt trirātrāyatanaṃ hi sahasram
''upāsmai gāyatā naraḥ'' ''upoṣu jātam apturaṃ'' ''pavasva vāco agriya'' iti pratipado bhavanty etad vai trirātram akaḥ
pavamāne rathantaraṃ karoti pavamānasyāntyaṃ vāmadevyaṃ bṛhat pṛṣṭham
iyaṃ vai rathantaram antarikṣaṃ vāmadevyaṃ dyaur bṛhad ime lokās trirātro yad etāni sāmāni sadhryañci karotīmān eva tal lokān saṃdadhāti tena trirātram āpnoti
kakubhaṃ prācīm udūhati
puro hy etayā satyā apaśuvīryaṃ karoti
tasyām iḍānāṃ saṃkṣāraḥ puruṣo vai kakup paśava iḍānāṃ saṃkṣāra ātmany eva tat paśūn pratiṣṭhāpayati
''pratnaṃ pīyūṣaṃ pūrvyaṃ yad uktham'' iti satobṛhatyo bhavanti
satobṛhatyā vai devā imān lokān vyāpnuvann imān evaitābhir lokān vyāpnoti
tā vā etā gāyatryo yat tripadās tena gāyatryas tā vā etā jagatyo yad dvādaśākṣarāṇi padāni tena jagatyas tā vā etā bṛhatyo yat ṣaṭtriṃśadakṣarās tena bṛhatyaḥ sarveṣāṃ vā etāś chandasāṃ rūpaṃ sarvāṇi rūpāṇi paśūnām avarundhe
etad vai pratyakṣaṃ mahāvrataṃ tasya gāyatraṃ śiro bṛhadrathantare pakṣau vāmadevyam ātmā yajñāyajñīyaṃ pucchaṃ dakṣiṇā evārkyam eṣa vāva pratyakṣaṃ mahāvratena stuvate ya etena yajate
tasya bṛhat pṛṣṭhaṃ paṅktiṣu brahmasāma tad āhuś chando vyādhīyate yad bṛhat pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati paṅktiṣu brahmasāmeti
śrāyantīyam eva kāryaṃ na chando vyādhīyate
eṣo sahasrasya pratiṣṭutiḥ
sahasram anyam abhitiṣṭhatīty āhuḥ sahasram anyo 'nvātiṣṭhatīti
kakubhaṃ prācīm udūhaty atha yad eṣā dvipadā kakubho loke kriyate sahasrasyaiva so 'nvāsthāyaḥ
anuṣṭubhaṃ saṃpadyate vāg anuṣṭub vāk trirātras tena trirātram āpnoti
ādityāś cāṅgirasaś cādīkṣanta te svarge loke 'spardhanta te 'ṅgirasa ādityebhyaḥ śvaḥ sutyāṃ prābruvaṃs ta ādityā etam apaśyaṃs taṃ sadyaḥ parikrīyāyāsyam udgātāraṃ vṛtvā tena stutvā svargaṃ lokam āyann ahīyantāṅgirasaḥ
bhrātṛvyavān yajeta
bhavaty ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tasmā amum ādityam aśvaṃ śvetaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇām ānayaṃs te pratigṛhya vyabhraṃśata sa etāny āyāsyāny apaśyat tair ātmānaṃ samaśrīṇāt
tad āyāsyāni bhavanti bheṣajāyaiva śāntyai
svargakāmo yajeta
bṛhatīṃ saṃpadyate bṛhatyā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargam evaitena lokam āpnoti
paśukāmo yajeta
paśavo vai bṛhatī paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
etasyaivaikaviṃśam agniṣṭomasāma kṛtvāmayāvinaṃ yājayet
prāṇo vai trivṛt prāṇa ādityaḥ prāṇair eṣa vyṛdhyate ya āmayāvī prāṇair evainaṃ samardhayati [thus BI; KSS seems to read samarṅghayati]
virājaṃ saṃpadyate 'pa vā etasmād annādyaṃ krāmati ya āmayāvy annaṃ virāḍ annadyam evāsmin dadhāti
ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo bhavaty apratiṣṭhito vā eṣa ya āmayāvī pratiṣṭhaikaviṃśaḥ praty eva tiṣṭhati
etenaivānnādyakāmo vā pratiṣṭhākāmo vā yajetānnaṃ virāṭ pratiṣṭhaikaviṃśo 'tty annaṃ pratitiṣṭhati
urvarā vedir bhavaty etad vā asyā vīryavattamaṃ vīryeṇaiva yajñaṃ samardhayati
khala uttaravedir atra hi sa rasaḥ samavaiti sarasam eva yajñaṃ karoti
khalevālī yūpo bhavaty etayā hi taṃ rasam utkṛṣanti
trivatsaḥ sāṇḍaḥ somakrayaṇaḥ sendratvāya
sarvā diśo 'śvarathāḥ somapravākā vidhāvanti
sarvābhya evāsmai digbhyo 'nnādyam avarundhe
yojane caturvāhiṇā prācyāṃ diśi prāhaivam iva vā adhvāno vimitā yaivādhvano mātrātāṃ dhāvayanti traipade praṣṭhivāhinodīcyāṃ gavyūtau dvyogena praticyāṃ krośe sthūriṇā dakṣiṇaitad vai diśāṃ rūpaṃ yadaiva diśāṃ rūpaṃ tena yajñaṃ samardhayanti
sakṣīradṛtayo rathā bhavanti tato yan navanītam udiyāt tadājye 'pi kāryaṃ sadyastvāya
athaiṣo 'ṅgirasām anukrīḥ
etena vā aṅgirasa ādityān āpnuvan yo hīna ānujāvara iva syāt sa etena yajetāpnoti pūrveṣāṃ prahām āpnuvan hy etenāṅgirasa ādityān
tasya caturviṃśau pavamānau
caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī gāyatryā vai devā imān lokān vyāpnuvann imān evaitena lokān vyāpnoti
tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe prāṇo gāyatrī prajananaṃ prāṇād eva gāyatryāḥ prajāyate
ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś [thus BI; KSS cāryujaś] ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate
virājaṃ saṃpadyate 'nnaṃ virāḍ annādyam evāvarundhe
ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo 'ntata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati
athaiṣa viśvajic chilpaḥ
śilpaṃ vā eṣa stomānāṃ paśyati gṛhe śilpaṃ ya evaṃ veda
tasyāṣṭādaśau pavamānau
cakrīvān vā eṣa yajñaḥ kāmāya yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etenābhyaśnute yatra hi cakrīvatā kāmayate tad abhyaśnute
svargakāmo yajeta
svargo lokaḥ pṛṣṭhāni svargam evaitena lokam āpnoti
tejo brahmavarcasaṃ pṛṣṭhāni yad ekadhā pṛṣṭhāni bhavanty ekadhaivāsmiṃs tejo brahmavarcasaṃ dadhāti
annaṃ paśavaḥ pṛṣṭhāni yad ekadhā pṛṣṭhāni bhavanty ekadhaivāsminn annādyaṃ paśūn dadhāti
tad āhur nānālokāni pṛṣṭhāni yad ekasmin yajñakratau samavarudhyanta īśvaro yajamāno 'pratiṣṭhātor iti
ekaviṃśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo madhya eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhaty ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo 'ntata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati
dvāv etāv ekaviṃśau bhavato dvipād yajamāno yajamānam eva yajñe paśuṣu ca pratiṣṭhāpayati
athaiṣa ekatrikaḥ prajāpater udbhit
etena vai prajāpatir eṣāṃ lokānām udabhinat
kṛtastomo vā eṣa udbhinnaṃ hy eva kṛtasya
yad ekayā stuvanty eko vai prajāpatiḥ prajāpatim evāpnoty atha yat tisṛbhis traya ime lokā eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
tā u catasras saṃpadyante catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
gāyatrīṃ saṃpadyate tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe
prāṇo gāyatrī prajananaṃ prāṇād eva gāyatryāḥ prajāyate
''ayā rucā hariṇyā punāna'' ity ārbhavaḥ pavamānaḥ
sarveṣāṃ vā eṣā chandasāṃ rūpaṃ sarveṣv eva chandaḥsv ārbhavaṃ pavamānaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
tasyāṃ gāyatrapārśvaṃ na gāyatrād eti na sāmno na nidhanāt
devā vai svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs teṣāṃ daivā ahīyanta vrātyāṃ pravasantas ta āgacchan yato devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tena taṃ stomaṃ na chando 'vindan yena tān āpsyaṃs te devā maruto 'bruvann etebhyas taṃ stomaṃ tac chandaḥ prayacchata yenāsmān āpnavān iti tebhya etaṃ ṣoḍaśaṃ stomaṃ prāyacchan parokṣam anuṣṭubhaṃ tato vai te tān āpnuvan
hīnā vā ete hīyante ye vrātyāṃ pravasanti na hi brahmacaryaṃ caranti na kṛṣiṃ vaṇijyāṃ ṣoḍaśo vā etat stomaḥ samāptum arhati
marutstomo vā eṣa yāni kṣudrāṇi chandāṃsi tāni marutām
kakubhaṃ prācīm udūhaty atha yad eṣā dvipadā kakubho loke kriyate rūpeṇaivenāṃs tat samardhayati
''adhāhīndra girvaṇa'' iti viṣamaṃ chando viṣama iva vai vrātaḥ sarvān evaitān samān karoti
tāsu dyautānam
dyutāno mārutas teṣāṃ gṛhapatir āsīt ta etena stomenāyajanta te sarva ārdhnuvan yad etat sāma bhavaty ṛdhyā eva
yan niruktaṃ nidhanam upeyur gṛhapatir evardhnuyād apetara ārdhnītātha yad aniruktam upayanti sarvān evaitān ṛddhau bhūtau pratiṣṭhāpayati
garagiro vā ete ye brahmādyaṃ janyam annam adanty aduruktavākyaṃ duruktam āhur adaṇḍyaṃ daṇḍena ghnantaś caranty adīkṣitā dīkṣitavācaṃ vadanti ṣoḍaśo vā eteṣāṃ stomaḥ pāpmānaṃ nirhantum arhati yad ete catvāraḥ ṣoḍaśā bhavanti tena pāpmano 'dhi nirmucyante
''devo vo draviṇodā'' ity agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ devatāsv evainān pratiṣṭhāpayati
atho khalv āhuḥ ''adarśi gātuvittama'' ity eva satobṛhatīṣu kāryaṃ viṣama iva vai vrātaḥ sarvān evainān satobṛhataḥ karoti
tad āhuḥ śithilam iva vā etat chandaś carācaraṃ yat satobṛhatī ''devo vo draviṇodā '' ity eva kāryam
eṣā vai pratiṣṭhitā bṛhatī yā punaḥpadā tad yat padaṃ punar ārabhate tasmāt putro mātaram adhyeti
uṣṇīṣaṃ ca pratodaś ca jyāhṇoḍaś ca vipathaś ca phalakāstīrṇaḥ kṛṣṇaśaṃ vāsaḥ kṛṣṇavalakṣe ajine rajato niṣkas tad gṛhapateḥ
valūkāntāni dāmatūṣāṇītareṣāṃ dve dve dāmanī dve dve upānahau dviṣaṃhitāny ajināni
etad vai vrātyadhanaṃ yasmā etad dadati tasminn eva mṛjānā yānti
trayastriṃśatā trayastriṃśatā gṛhapatim abhisamāyanti trayastriṃśad dhi devā ārdhnuvan ṛdhyā eva
athaiṣa ṣaṭṣoḍaśī ye nṛśaṃsā ninditāḥ santo vrātyāṃ pravaseyus ta etena yajeran
abhipūrveṇa vā ete pāpmanā gṛhītā ye nṛśaṃsā ninditāḥ santo vrātyāṃ pravasanti yat ṣaṭṣoḍaśāni stotrāṇi bhavanti tena pāpmāno 'dhi nirmucyante
yad ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhāyā ekaviṃśo madhyata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati
uktho bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni paśavo nṛśaṃsam agryaṃ pariṇayanti paśubhir evainān agryaṃ pariṇayati
athaiṣa dviṣoḍaśo ye kaniṣṭhāḥ santo vrātyāṃ pravaseyus ta etena yajeran
hīnā vā ete ahīyante ye kaniṣṭhāḥ santo vrātyāṃ pravasanti yat trivṛtaḥ pavamānā bhavanti mukhaṃ vai trivṛt stomānāṃ mukhata evainān yajñasya pariṇayati
yad vai ṣoḍaśe stotre bhavatas tena pāpmano 'dhi nirmucyante
ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo 'ntata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati
athaiṣa śamanīcāmeḍhrāṇāṃ stomo ye jyeṣṭhāḥ santo vrātyāṃ pravaseyus ta etena yajeran
agrād agraṃ rohanty ūrdhvāḥ stomā yanty anapabhraṃśāya
etena vai śamanīcāmeḍhrā ayajanta teṣāṃ kuṣītakaḥ sāmaśravaso gṛhapatir āsīt tān luśākapiḥ khārgalir anuvyāharad avākīrṣata kanīyāṃsau stomāv upāgur iti tasmāt kauṣītakānāṃ na kaś canātīva jihīte yajñāva kīrṇā hi
indro vai triśirasaṃ tvāṣṭram ahaṃs tam aślīlā vāg abhyavadat so 'gnim upādhāvat sa etad agnistotram apaśyat tad ātmany adhividhāya tenainam ayājayat tenāsyāślīlāṃ vācam apāhan
apāślīlāṃ vācaṃ hate ya evaṃ veda
yo 'pūta iva syād agniṣṭutā yajetāgninaivāsya pāpmānam apahatya trivṛtā tejo brahmavarcasaṃ dadhāti
tad āhur yat trivṛd bhavaty ekasmād evāṅgāt pāpmānam apahanti mukhād eveti
jyotiṣṭoma eva kāryaḥ
yat trivṛd bhavati yad evāsya mukhato 'pūtaṃ tat tenāpahanti yat pañcadaśo yad evāsyorasto bāhvor apūtaṃ tat tenāpahanti yat saptadaśo yad evāsya madhyato 'pūtaṃ tat tenāpahanti yad ekaviṃśo yad evāsya pador aṣṭhīvator apūtaṃ tat tenāpahanti
vaiśvānaraṃ vā eṣa praviśatīty āhur yo 'gniṣṭutā yajata iti vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kāryaṃ tasya yad apūtaṃ tad agniḥ kṣāpayaty athetaraḥ śuciḥ pūta udeti
trivṛd agniṣṭud agniṣṭomas tasya vāyavyāsv agniṣṭomasāma
brahmavarcasakāmo yajeta
tejo vai trivṛd brahmavarcasaṃ yad vāyavyāsv agniṣṭomasāma bhavaty upaivainaṃ tad dhamati
yathā hiraṇyaṃ niṣṭaped evam enam agniṣṭun niṣṭapati
etasyaiva revatīṣu vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma kṛtvā paśukāmo yajeta
jaratkakṣo vā eṣa yo 'paśur yathā vai jaratkakṣe paśavo na ramanta evam etasmin paśavo na ramante yo 'paśur yadā vai jaratkakṣam agnir dahaty athainam abhivarṣaty athāsminn oṣadhayo jāyante 'tha vai tasmin paśavo ramante
ramante 'smin paśavo ya evaṃ veda
yad evāsyāpaśavyaṃ tad agniṣṭun nirdahati yad agniṣṭun nirdahati tad adbhī revatībhiḥ śamayati
jyotiṣṭomenāgniṣṭutā yajñavibhraṣṭo yajeta
yasmin vā yajñakratau vibhraṃśeta
agnir vā etasya havyam atti yo yajñe vibhraṃśate na devatā havyaṃ gamayaty agnim evaikadhardhnoti
yad vai saṃśīryate 'thānyan niṣkurvanti tena tad yāti yadā vāva tan niṣkurvanty atha tad yāti yeṣv eva stomeṣu vibhraṃśate yasmin yajñakratau tair eva yajeta yeṣv eva stomeṣu vibhraṃśate yasmin yajñakratau teṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
saptadaśenāgniṣṭutānnādyakāmo yajeta
annaṃ vai saptadaśo 'gnir annādyasya pradātāgnir evāsmā annādyaṃ prayacchati
annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sarvaḥ saptadaśo bhavati prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti
trivṛd agniṣṭomas tasyāniruktaṃ prātaḥsavanam
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā asmāt sṛṣṭā apākrāman sa etad aniruktaṃ prātaḥsavanam apaśyat tenāsāṃ madhyaṃ vyavait tā enam upāvartanta pary enam āviśan
grāmakāmo yajeta yad etad aniktaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ bhavati madhyam evāsāṃ vyavaity upainam āvartante pary enaṃ viśanti
sa eṣa prajāpater apūrvo nāsmāt pūrvo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ
tasya prātaḥsavane sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣv ekādaśadakṣiṇā vyādiśaty aśvadvādaśā madhyandine tā ubhayīr apākaroty ekādaśa tṛtīyasavane tā vaśāyām apākaroti
trayastriṃśad etā dakṣiṇā bhavanti trayastriṃśad devatā devatā evāpnoty aśvaś catustriṃśo dakṣiṇānāṃ prajāpatiś catustriṃśo devatānāṃ prajāpatim evāpnoti
sa eṣa bṛhaspatisavo bṛhaspatir akāmayata devānāṃ purodhāṃ gaccheyam iti sa etenāyajata sa devānāṃ purodhām agacchat
gacchati purodhāṃ ya evaṃ veda
sa eṣa sthapatisavo yaṃ sthāpatyāyābhiṣiñceran sa etena yajeta
gacchati sthāpatyaṃ ya evaṃ veda
kṛṣṇājine 'dhy abhiṣicyata etad vai pratyakṣaṃ brahmavarcasaṃ brahmavarcasa evādhy abhiṣicyate
ājyenābhiṣicyate teja ājyaṃ teja ātman dhatte
trivṛd agniṣṭomaḥ sa sarvasvāro yaḥ kāmayetānāmayatāmuṃ lokam iyām iti sa etena yajeta
prāṇo vai trivṛt prāṇaḥ svaraḥ prāṇān evāsya bahir ṇirādadhāti tājak pramīyate
trivṛd vai stomānāṃ kṣepiṣṭho yat trivṛd bhavaty āśīyaḥ saṃgacchātā ity ananto vai svaro 'nanto 'sau loko 'nantam evainaṃ svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayati
abhivatyaḥ pravatyo bhavanty asmād evainaṃ lokāt svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayanti
ārbhavapavamāne stūyamāna audumbaryā dakṣiṇā prāvṛto nipadyate tad eva saṃgacchate
sa eṣa śunaskarṇastoma etena vai śunaskarṇo bāṣkiho 'yajata tasmāc chunaskarṇastoma ity ākhyāyate
trivṛd agniṣṭomo vaiśvadevasya lokaḥ
āgneyī pratipad vaiśvadevaḥ paśur bārhaspatyānubandhyā
na yūpaṃ minvanti nottaravediṃ nivapanti
paridhau paśuṃ niyuñjanti
pañcāśad dakṣiṇā
ahataṃ vasāno 'vabhṛthād udeti caturo māso na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti
tataś caturṣu māseṣu varuṇapraghāsānāṃ loke dvidivaḥ
vāruṇī pratipan mārutaḥ paśuḥ
kavatī pratipad vāruṇaḥ paśuḥ
maitrāvaruṇy anūbandhyā minvanti yūpaṃ ny uttaravediṃ vapanti yūpe paśū niyuñjanti
śataṃ dakṣiṇā ahataṃ vasāno 'vabhṛthād udeti caturo māso na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti
tataś caturṣu māseṣu sākamedhānāṃ loke trirātraḥ
anīkavatī pratipad āgneyaḥ paśur mārutī pratipad aindrāgnaḥ paśur vaiśvakarmaṇī pratipad ekādaśinī paśavaḥ sauryānūbandhyā minvanti yūpaṃ ny uttaravediṃ vapanti yūpe paśūn niyuñjanti pañcāśacchataṃ dakṣiṇā
ahataṃ vasāno 'vabhṛthād udeti caturo māso na māṃsam aśnāti na striyam upaiti
tataś caturṣu māseṣu śunāsīryasya loke jyotiṣṭomo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
upavatī pratipad vāyavyaḥ paśur āśviny anūbandhyā minvanti yūpaṃ ny uttaravediṃ vapanti yūpe paśuṃ niyuñjanti dvādaśaṃ śataṃ dakṣiṇā
agniḥ saṃvatsaraḥ sūryaḥ parivatsaraś candramā idāvatsaro vāyur anuvatsaro 'gniṃ saṃvatsaraṃ vaiśvadevenāpnoti sūryaṃ parivatsaraṃ varuṇapraghāsaiś candramasam idāvatsaraṃ sākamedhair vāyum anuvatsaraṃ śunāsīryeṇa
haviryajñair vai devā imaṃ lokam abhyajayann antarikṣaṃ paśumadbhiḥ somair amum imān eva lokān āpnoty eṣu lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
yadāgnihotraṃ juhoty atha daśa gṛhamedhina āpnoty ekayā rātryā, yadā daśa saṃvatsarān agnihotraṃ juhoty atha darśapūrṇamāsayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśa saṃvatsarān darśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ yajate 'thāgniṣṭomayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśabhir agniṣṭomair yajate 'tha sahasrayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśabhiḥ sahasrair yajate 'thāyutayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśabhir ayutair yajate 'tha prayutayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśabhiḥ prayutair yajate 'tha niyutayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśabhir niyutair yajate 'thārbudayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśabhir arbudair yajate 'tha nyarbudayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśabhir nyarbudair yajate 'tha nikharvakayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśabhir nikharvakair yajate 'tha badvayājinam āpnoti, yadā daśabhir badvair yajate 'thākṣitayājinam āpnoti yadā daśabhir akṣitair yajate 'tha gaur bhavati, yadā gaur bhavaty athāgnir bhavati yadāgnir bhavaty atha saṃvatsarasya gṛhapatim āpnoti
yadā saṃvatsarasya gṛhapatir bhavaty atha vaiśvadevasya mātrām āpnoty ato vā itare parastarāṃ parastarām eva sarve
etān eva lokān āpnoty etān lokān jayati ya evaṃ veda
saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
devāś ca vā asurāś ca prajāpater dvayāḥ putrā āsaṃs te 'surā bhūyāṃso balīyāṃsa āsan kanīyāṃso devās te devāḥ prajāpatim upādhāvan sa etam upahavyam apaśyat
sa aikṣata yan niruktam āhariṣyāmy asurā me yajñaṃ haniṣyantīti so 'niruktam āharat
sa uttame stotre ''devo vo draviṇodā'' iti devān abhiparyāvartata
tato devā abhavan parāsurāḥ
bhavaty ātmanā parāsya bhrātṛvyo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
atho khalv āhuḥ ''yajñāyajñā vo agnaya'' ity eva kāryam
agnir vai sarvā devatās tena na devatānāṃ kāṃ canāntar eti
indro yatīn sālāvṛkeyebhyaḥ prāyacchat tam aślīlā vāg abhyavadat sa prajāpatim upādhāvat tasmā etam upahavyaṃ prāyacchat taṃ viśve devā upāhvayanta tasmād upahavyaḥ
abhiśasyamānaṃ yājayet
devatā vā etaṃ parivrajanti yam anṛtam abhiśaṃsanti devatā evāsyānnam ādayanti
tasya pūtasya svaditasya manuṣyā annam adanti
grāmakāmo yajeta
mārutī bhavati marutau vai devānāṃ viśo viśam evāsmā anuniyunakty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati
paśukāmo yajeta pauṣī bhavati
paśavo vai pūṣā paśūn evāvarundhe
vaiśvadevī bhavati viśve hy enaṃ devā upāhvayanta
bṛhatsāmā bhavati
prajāpatir hy enam indrāya prāyacchat
aśvaḥ śyavo dakṣiṇā
sa hy aniruktaḥ
sa brahmaṇe deyaḥ
brahmā vā ṛtvijām aniruktaḥ svenaivainaṃ tad rūpeṇa samardhayati
yāvad dha vai kumāre sadyo jāta eno nāsmiṃs tāvac ca naino bhavati ya evaṃ veda
saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
tasya dvādaśa dīkṣopasadaḥ
svargakāmo yajeta
dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraḥ svargo lokaḥ svargam evaitena lokam āpnoti
ghṛtavrato bhavati
devavrataṃ vai ghṛtaṃ devavratenaiva devatā apyeti
uttareṇottareṇa kāṇḍenopaity uttara uttara eṣāṃ lokānāṃ jyāyān svargasya samaṣṭyai
bṛhatsāma bhavati bṛhatā vai devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan svargam evetena lokam āpnoti
ṛtam uktvā prasarpanty ṛtenaivainaṃ svargaṃ lokaṃ gamayanti
somacamaso dakṣiṇā devatayaiva devatā apyeti
audumbaro bhavaty ūrg udumbara ūrjam evāvarundhe
sagotrāya brahmaṇe deyaḥ somapīthasyāvidohāya
sarvaḥ saptadaśo bhavati
dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavaḥ sa vai saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraḥ svargo lokaḥ svargam evaitena lokam āpnoti
saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
tasya dīkṣaṇīyāyām iṣṭau dvādaśamānaṃ hiraṇyaṃ dadāti caturviṃśatimānaṃ prāyaṇīyāyāṃ dve caturviṃśatimāne ātithyāyāṃ catvāri caturviṃśatimānāni prātaḥ prathamāyām upasady aṣṭau caturviṃśatimānāny aparāhṇe prathamāyām upasadi ṣoḍaśacaturviṃśatimānāni prātar madhyamāyām upasadi dvātriṃśataṃ caturviṃśatimānāny aparāhṇe madhyamāyām upasadi catuḥṣaṣṭiṃ caturviṃśatimānāni prātar uttamāyām upasady aṣṭāviṃśatiśataṃ caturviṃśatimānāny aparāhṇa uttamāyām upasadi dve aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamāne agnīṣomīyasya paśor vapāyāṃ catvāry aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni prātaḥ paśor vapāyām aṣṭāv aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni prātaḥsavane sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu ṣoḍaśāṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni mādhyandine savane 'naḍucchataṃ ca rukmo hotuḥ srag udgātur dvātriṃśatam aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni tṛtīyasavane sanneṣu nārāśaṃseṣu catuḥṣaṣṭim aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāny udayanīyāyām iṣṭāv aṣṭāviṃśatiśatam aṣṭāviṃśatiśatamānāni vaśāyā vapāyām
eṣa vā anaḍuho lokam āpnoti ya evaṃ veda
eṣa vai jyotiṣmantaṃ puṇyaṃ lokaṃ jayati ya evaṃ vidvān etena yajate
saptadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ
tasya prātaḥsavanīyān somān pratiduhā śrīṇāti śṛtena madhyandine dadhnā tṛtīyasavane
paśukāmo yajeta
yat sarvāṇi savanāny āśīrvanti bhavanty anusavanam evainaṃ paśubhiḥ sarmardhayati prajā tv asya mīliteva bhavati śukriye hi savane payasā śrīṇāti
vaiśyaṃ yājayet
etad vai vaiśyasya samṛddhaṃ yat paśavaḥ paśubhir evainaṃ samardhayati
tasya kaṇvarathantaraṃ pṛṣṭham
sadoviśīyaṃ brahmasāma
paśavo vai kaṇvarathantaraṃ paśavaḥ sadoviśīyam ābhipūrvān evāsmin paśūn dadhāti
sarvaḥ saptadaśo bhavati
dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavaḥ sa vai saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nuprajāyante tān evāptvāvarundhe
saptadaśa ukthyaḥ
indro vṛtram ahan sa viṣvaṅvīryeṇa vyārcchat tasmai devāḥ prāyaścittim aicchaṃs taṃ na kiṃ canādhinot taṃ tīvrasoma evādhinot
somātipavitaṃ yājayet
chidra iva vā eṣa yaṃ somo 'tipavate yat tīvrasomena yajate pihityā evācchidratāyai
rājānam aparuddhaṃ yājayet
viḍ vā etam atipavate yo rājāparudhyate yat tīvrasomena yajate pihityā evācchidratāyai
grāmakāmo yajeta
grāmo vā etam atipavate yo 'laṃ grāmāya san grāmaṃ na vindate yat tīvrasomena yajate pihityā evācchidratāyai
prajākāmo yajeta prajā vā etam atipavate yo 'laṃ prajāyāḥ san prajāṃ na vindate yat tīvrasomena yajate pihityā evācchidratāyai
paśukāmo yajeta paśavo vā etam atipavante yo 'laṃ paśubhyaḥ san paśūn na vindate yat tīvrasomena yajate pihityā [thus BI; 'pihityā KSS] evācchidratāyai
āmayāvinaṃ yājayet prāṇā vā etam atipavante ya āmayāvī yat tīvrasomena yajate pihityā evācchidratāyai
śatam āśiraṃ duhanti tīvrayanty evainam
tat tā u eva dakṣiṇāḥ
abhy abhisomān unnayanti tīvra enaṃ dhinavad ity ubhāv adhvaryū sarve camasādhvaryavo 'cchāvākāya pratigṛṇanti tīvrayanty evainam
tad abhakṣayanta ṛtvijaś camasān avajighranti tīvrayanty evainaṃ tat tān acchāvākasya stotre bhakṣayanti tīvrayanty evainam
tad yat savanāni vyavabhakṣayeyur apakrāmukā yajamānāc chrīḥ syāt sakṛtsakṛt savanānām antato bhakṣayanti savanānām asaṃbhedāya
rathantaraṃ sāma bhavati
iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyāṃ vā eṣa na pratitiṣṭhati yo na pratitiṣṭhaty asyām evainaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavaty etad evāsmiñ chrīṇāti
vāg anuṣṭup vāco raso yajñāyajñīyaṃ vācy evāsya rasaṃ dadhāti
viśoviśīyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavaty etad evāsmin sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
udvaṃśīyam ukthānām antato bhavati sarveṣāṃ vā etat pṛṣṭhānāṃ rūpaṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
ukthyo bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
saptadaśa ukthyaḥ ṣoḍaśimān saptadaśī
yāvān vai prajāpatir ūrdhvas tāvāṃs tiryaṅ
yāvanta ime lokā ūrdhvās tāvantas tiryañcaḥ
vājapeyayājī vāva prajāpatim āpnoti
yat saptadaśa stotrāṇi tenordhvam apnoti yat sarvaḥ saptadaśas tena tiryañcam
tasya nānāvīryāṇi savanāni
aniruktaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ vājavan mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ citravat tṛtīyasavanam
yad aniruktaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ bhavaty anirukto vai prajāpatiḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti yad vājavan mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ annaṃ vai vājo 'nnādyasyāvarudhyai yac citravat tṛtīyasavanaṃ svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
viyonir vājapeya ity āhuḥ prājāpatyaḥ san niruktasāmeti yad aniruktaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ tena sayoniḥ
rathantaraṃ sāma bhavaty āśīya ujjhityai
iyaṃ vai rathantaram asyām evādhy abhiṣicyate
tasmād vājapeyayājy apratyavarohī
asyāṃ hi so 'dhy abhiṣicyate
abhīvarto brahmasāma bhavati brahmaṇo vā eṣa ṛṣabha ṛṣabhatām evainaṃ gamayati
yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭubhi bhavati vāg anuṣṭup vāco raso yajñāyajñīyaṃ vācy evāsya rasaṃ dadhāti
vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavatīndriyasya vīryasya parigṛhītyai
udvaṃśīyam ukthānām antato bhavati sarveṣāṃ vā etat pṛṣṭhānāṃ rūpaṃ sarveṣv eva rūpeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
gaurīvitaṃ ṣoḍaśisāma bhavati
atiriktaṃ gaurīvitam atiriktaḥ ṣoḍaśy atirikta evātiriktaṃ dadhāti
tad āhur jāmi vā etad yajñe kriyate yad udvaṃśīyād gaurīvitena stuvate svārāt svāreṇeti
na jāmy asti savanaṃ saṃtiṣṭhate
ukthaṃ śasyate vaṣaṭkāro 'ntarā tenājāmi
apacchid iva vā etad yajñakāṇḍaṃ yat ṣoḍaśī tenājāmi
yajñāraṇye saṃtiṣṭhata ity āhur aty ukthāny ety ati ṣoḍaśinaṃ na rātriṃ prāpnotīti
viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu bṛhad uttamaṃ bhavati
eṣā vai prajāpateḥ paśuṣṭhā tanūr yac chipiviṣṭaḥ prāṇo vai bṛhat prāṇa eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
bṛhatā stuvanti bṛhad amuṃ lokam āptum arhati tam evāpnoti
prajāpatir akāmayata vājam āpnuyāṃ svargaṃ lokam iti sa etaṃ vājapeyam apaśyad vājapeyo vā eṣa vājam evaitena svargaṃ lokam āpnoti
śukravatyo jyotiṣmatyaḥ prātaḥsavane bhavanti tejo brahmavarcasaṃ tābhir avarundhe
vājavatyo mādhyandine bhavanti svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
annavatyo gaṇavatyaḥ paśumatyas tṛtīyasavane bhavanti bhūmānaṃ tābhir avarunadhe
sarvaḥ saptadaśo bhavati prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti
hiraṇyasraja ṛtvijo bhavanti mahasa eva tad rūpaṃ kriyate
eṣa me 'muṣmin loke prakāśo 'sad iti
jyotir vai hiraṇyaṃ jyotir evāsmin dadhāti
ājiṃ dhāvanti yajamānam ujjāpayanti svargam evainaṃ tal lokam ujjāpayanti
nākaṃ rohati svargam eva tal lokaṃ rohati
sarajase rohati manuṣyalokād evainam antar dadhāti
vājināṃ sāma brahmā rathacakre 'bhigāyati vājo vai svargo lokaḥ svargam evainaṃ tal lokam ujjāpayati
viṣṇoḥ śipiviṣṭavatīṣu bṛhaduttamaṃ bhavati svargam eva tal lokaṃ rūḍhvā bradhnasya viṣṭapam abhyatikrāmati
agniṣṭomaṃ prathamam āharati yajñamukhaṃ vā agniṣṭomo yajñamukham evārabhya savamākramate
athaiṣo 'bhiṣecanīyaḥ
tasya dvātriṃśāḥ pavamānā dvātriṃśadakṣarā 'nuṣṭub vāg anuṣṭub yāvatī vāk tayaiva sūyate
saṃśara iva vā eṣa chandasāṃ yad viṣamā stomā ayathāpūrvam iti
yat samāḥ pavamānās tenāsaṃśaras tena yathāpūrvam
ātmanā vā agniṣṭomenardhnoty ātmanā puṇyo bhavaty atha yad ukthāni paśavo vā ukthāni viḍ ukthāni yad ukthāni bhavanty anusantatyā eva
''vāyo śukro ayāmita'' iti vāyavyā pratipad bhavati vāg vai vāyur vācam evāsya yajñamukhe yunakti tayābhiṣicyate sarvasyā eva vācaḥ sūyate sarvā enaṃ vāco rājeti vadanti
saṃbhāryā bhavanti pṛṣṭhāny eva tābhir yunakti yan nānādevatyās tena yunakti vīryaṃ vai pṛṣṭhāni vīrya evādhy abhiṣicyate
yanti vā ete yajñamukhād ity āhur ye saṃbhāryāḥ kurvata iti
yat ''pavasya vāco agriya'' iti tena yajñamukhān na yanti
''davidyutatyā rucā-'' iti chandasāṃ rūpaṃ chandāṃsy evāsya yajñamukhe yunakti tair abhiṣicyate
''etam u tyaṃ daśa kṣipa'' ity ādityā ādityā vā imāḥ prajās tāsām eva madhyataḥ sūyate
''pavasvendo vṛṣā suta'' vṛṣaṇvatyo bhavanti triṣṭubho rūpaṃ vīryaṃ vai triṣṭup vīrya evādhy abhiṣicyate
''utte śuṣmāsa īrata'' ity udvatyo bhavanty udvad vā anuṣṭubho rūpam ānuṣṭubho rājanyas tasmād udvatyo bhavanti
''pavamānasya te kava'' iti prāṇānāṃ kḷptyai
''adha kṣapā pariṣkṛta'' ity anuṣṭup prathamānuṣṭub uttamā vāg vā anuṣṭub vācaiva prayanti vācam abhyudyanti
chinnam iva vā etad yad ekarcā yad etāvānuṣṭubhau tṛcāv abhito bhavato bahavaḥ puraetāro bhavanti bahavaḥ paścāpinaḥ
sauryānuṣṭub uttamā bhavati svargasya lokasya samaṣṭyai
varuṇasya vai suṣuvāṇasya bhargo 'pākrāmat sa tredhāpatad bhṛgus tṛtīyam abhavac chrāyantīyaṃ tṛtīyam apas tṛtīyaṃ prāviśat
yad bhārgavo hotā bhavati tenaiva tad indriyaṃ vīryam āptvāvarundhe yat śrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati tenaiva tad indriyaṃ vīryam āptvārundhe yat puṣkarasrajaṃ pratimuñcate tenaiva tad indriyaṃ vīryam āptvāvarundhe
daśamī bhavati
daśa camasā daśa camasādhvaryavo daśa daśa camasam abhiyanty ā daśamāt puruṣād anvākhyāya prasarpanti daśa samṛddho hy eṣa yajña enaṃ vāva te tad yajñam anvaicchan ya etena yajata etad evendriyaṃ vīryam āttvāsmin dadhāti
sarvaḥ saptadaśo bhavati dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavaḥ sa vai saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsarād evendriyaṃ vīryam āptvāvarundhe
indro vṛtram ahaṃs tasyeyaṃ citrāṇy upaid rūpāṇy asau nakṣatrāṇām avakāśena puṇḍarīkaṃ jāyate yat puṣkarasrajaṃ pratimuñcate vṛtrasyaiva tad rūpaṃ kṣatraṃ pratimuñcate
dvādaśa puṣkarā bhavanti dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsare 'ntar bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca bhūtena caivainaṃ bhavyena ca samardhayati
srag udgātus saurya udgātā na vai tasmai vyaucchad atho vy evāsmai vāsayati
rukmo hotur āgneyo hotātho amum evāsmā ādityam unnayati
prākāśāv adhvaryor yāv iva hy adhvaryū atho cakṣuṣī evāsmin dadhāti
aśvaḥ prastotuḥ prājāpatyo 'śvaḥ prājāpatyaḥ prastotātho preva hy aśvaḥ prothati preva prastotā stauti
dhenuḥ pratihartuḥ paya evāsmin dadhāti
vaśā maitrāvaruṇasya vaśaṃ mā nayād iti
ṛṣabho brāhmaṇācchaṃsino vīryaṃ vā ṛṣabho vīryam evāsmin dadhāti
vāsaḥ potuḥ pavitratvāya
varāsī neṣṭur anulambeva hy eṣā hotrā
sthūri yavācitam acchāvākasya sthūrir iva hy eṣā hotrātho nirvaruṇatvāyaiva yavā na vai tarhi yad asyāṃ dakṣiṇā abhy abhavann atho asya ta eva tenābhīṣṭāḥ prītā bhavanti
anaḍvān agnīdho yuktyai
ajaḥ subrahmaṇyāyai
vatsatary unnetuḥ sāṇḍas trivatso grāvastuto mithunatvāya
dvādaśa paṣṭhauhyo garbhiṇyo brahmaṇo dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhaty atha yad garbhiṇyo vāg vai dhenur mantro garbho vācy evāsya mantraṃ dadhāty āmantraṇīyo bhavaty atha yad dhenubhavyā dvādaśa payāṃsi tāny evāsmin dadhāti tasmād āhuḥ payasvī rājā puṇya iti
yo vai savād eti nainaṃ sava upanamaty atha yaḥ sāmabhya eti pāpīyān suṣuvāṇo bhavati
saṃbhāryā bhavanti pṛṣṭhāny eva tābhir yunakti
etāni vāva sāmāni yat pṛṣṭhāni
yat saṃbhāryā bhavanti tad eva sāmabhyo naiti
yāni devarājñāṃ sāmāni tair amuṣmin loka ṛdhnoti yāni manuṣyarājñāṃ tair asminn ubhayor anayor lokayor ṛdhnoti devaloke ca manuṣyaloke ca
sāmatriṣṭubhy adhy abhiṣicyate vīryaṃ vai sāma triṣṭup vīrya evādhy abhiṣicyate
ekādaśa rājasāmāni bhavanty ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭub ojo vīryaṃ triṣṭub ojasy eva vīrye 'dhy abhiṣicyate
yat trivṛtam abhiṣecanīye kuryur brahma kṣatrāyāpidadhyur yat trivṛtam uddharanti brahma tat kṣatrād uddharanti tasmād bharatāṃ pratidaṇḍā brahmaṇā na hi te trivṛtam abhiṣecanīye kurvanti
ekaviṃśo 'bhiṣecanīyasyottamaḥ saptadaśo daśapeya ekaviṃśaḥ keśavapanīyasya prathamaḥ kṣatraṃ vā ekaviṃśo viṭ saptadaśaḥ kṣatreṇaivāsmai viśam ubhayataḥ parigṛhṇāty anapakrāmukāsmād viṭ bhavati
yad vai rājasūyenābhiṣicyate tat svargaṃ lokam ārohati sa yad imaṃ lokaṃ nopāvarohed ati janaṃ vā gacched ud vā mādyed yad eṣo 'rvācīnastomaḥ keśavapanīyo bhavaty asya lokasyānuddhānāya yathā śākhāyāḥ śākhām ālambham upāvarohed evam etenemaṃ lokam upāvarohati pratiṣṭhāyai
indro vṛtram ahan sa viṣyaṅvīryeṇa vyabhraṃśata sa etac chrāyantīyam apaśyat tenātmānaṃ samaśrīṇād indriyeṇa vā eṣa vīryeṇa vyṛdhyate yo rājasūyenābhiṣicyate vṛtraṃ hi hanti yac chrāyantīyaṃ brahmasāma bhavati punar evātmānaṃ saṃśrīṇāti
yajñāyajñīyam anuṣṭubhi bhavati vācā vā eṣa vyṛdhyate yo rājasūyenābhiṣicyate vṛtraṃ hi hanti vāg anuṣṭub vāco raso yajñāyajñīyaṃ vācy evāsya rasaṃ dadhāti
vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavatīndriyeṇa vā eṣa vīryeṇa vyṛdhyate yo rājasūyenābhiṣicyate vṛtraṃ hi hanti yad vāravantīyam agniṣṭomasāma bhavatīndriyasya vīryasya parigṛhītyai
aśrayan vāva śrāyantīyenāvārayanta vāravantīyenendriyasya vā eṣā vīryasya parigṛhītiḥ
apratiṣṭhito vā eṣa yo rājasūyenābhiṣicyate yadā vā etena dvirātreṇa yajate 'thaiva pratiṣṭhā
yāvanti saṃvatsarasyāhorātrāṇi tāvatya etāḥ stotrīyāḥ saṃvatsara eva pratitiṣṭhati
agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar atirātra uttaraṃ nānaivāhorātrayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati
amāvāsyāyāṃ pūrvam ahar udriṣṭa [em. Caland: uddṛṣṭa] uttaraṃ nānaivārdhamāsayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati paurṇamāsyāṃ pūrvam ahar vyaṣṭakāyām uttaraṃ nānaiva māsoḥ pratitiṣṭhati tad āhur ya eva samānapakṣe puṇyāhanī syātāṃ tayor eva kāryaṃ samṛdhyai
apaśavyo dvirātra ity āhur dve hy ete chandasī gāyatraṃ ca traiṣṭubhaṃ ca jagatīm antaryantīti na tena jagatī kṛtā yat tṛtīyasavane kriyate
yadā vā eṣāhīnasyāhar bhajate sāhvasya vā savanam athaiva jagatī kṛtā traiśokam uttarasyāhno brahmasāma bhavati vaikhānasam acchāvākasāma yac chukriye savane kriyete tenaiva jagatī kṛtā tena paśavyaḥ
vyuṣṭir vā eṣa dvirātro vy evāsmai vāsayati
athaiṣa rāṭ
yo rājya āśaṃsamāno rājyaṃ na prāpnuyāt sa etena yajeta rājaivainaṃ rājānaṃ karoti taṃ tu vairājeti vadeyur yaṃ rājā rājānaṃ kuryād rājaivainaṃ rājānaṃ karoti
chando 'nye yajñāḥ saṃpadyante stomam eṣa vīryaṃ vai stomo vīrya evādhy abhiṣicyate
aṣṭāv ekaviṃśāḥ saṃstuto bhavaty aṣṭau vai vīrā rāṣṭraṃ samudyacchanti rājabhrātā ca rājaputraś ca purohitaś ca mahiṣī ca sūtaś ca grāmaṇī ca kṣattā ca saṃgrahītā caite vai vīrā rāṣṭraṃ samudyacchanty eteṣv evādhy abhiṣicyate
kṣatraṃ vā ekaviṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhā kṣatrasyevāsya prakāśo bhavati pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
athaiṣa virāḍ annādyakāmo yajeta
parokṣam anye yajñā virājaṃ saṃpadyante pratyakṣam eṣa virājaṃ saṃpannaḥ
pratyakṣam etenānnādyam avarundhe 'nnādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
sarvo daśadaśī bhavati daśākṣarā virāḍ vairājam annam annādyasyāvarudhyai
tā u pañca pañca bhavanti pāṅkto yajñaḥ pāṅktā paśavo yajña eva paśuṣu pratitiṣṭhati
etenaiva pratiṣṭhākāmo yajeta daśabhir vā idaṃ puruṣaḥ pratiṣṭhito 'syām eva pratitiṣṭhati
athaiṣa aupaśadaḥ
gandharvāpsarasāṃ stomaḥ prajākāmo yajeta gandharvāpsaraso vai manuṣyasya prajāyā vāprajastāyā veśate teṣām atra somapīthas tān svena bhāgadheyena prīṇāti te 'smai tṛptāḥ prītāḥ prajāṃ prayacchanti
ekaikā stotrīyopajāyate prajām evāsmā upajanayati
kakubhaṃ prācīm udūhati puruṣo vai kakub garbha eva sa madhyato dhīyate
atha yad eṣā dvipadā kakubho loke kriyate garbha eva tad dhi taṃ prajanayati
cyāvanaṃ bhavati prajātir vai cyāvanam
prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda
vasiṣṭhasya janitre bhavato vasiṣṭho vā ete putrahataḥ sāmanī apaśyat sa prajayā paśubhiḥ prājāyata yad ete sāmanī bhavataḥ prajātyai
dve saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyete dve striyā ūne prajananāya prajananam eva tat kriyate prajātyai
athaiṣa punaḥstomaḥ
yo bahu pratigṛhya garagīr iva manyeta sa etena yajeta
yaikādaśī yad eva pūrvavayase bahu pratigṛhṇāti yad garaṃ girati yad anannam atti prātaḥsavanāya tan niharati
atha yā dvādaśī yad evottaravayase bahu pratigṛhṇati yad garaṃ girati yad anannam atti tṛtīyasavanāya tan niharati
vairājo vai puruṣaḥ sa madhyato 'śuddho madhyata evainaṃ pāpmano muñcati
śuddhāśuddhīye bhavataḥ
indro yatīn sālāvṛkeyebhyaḥ prāyacchat tam aślīlā vāg abhyavadat so 'śuddho 'manyata sa ete śuddhāśuddhīye apaśyat tābhyām aśudhyat
yad eva bahu pratigṛhṇāti yad garaṃ girati yad anannam atti yad aśuddho manyate tad etābhyāṃ śudhyati
gauṣūktaṃ cāśvasūktaṃ ca bhavataḥ
gauṣūktiś cāśvasūktiś ca bahu pratigṛhya garagirāv amanyetāṃ tāv ete sāmanī apaśyatāṃ tābhyāṃ garaṃ niraghnātām
yad eva bahu pratigṛhṇāti yad garaṃ girati yad anannam atti tad etābhyāṃ nirhate
pañcadaśa stotrāṇi bhavanty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśaḥ pāpmana evainaṃ muktvaujasā vīryeṇa samardhayati
athaiṣa catuṣṭomaḥ
paśukāmo yajeta
yac catasṛbhir bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati catuṣpādāḥ paśavaḥ paśūn evāvarundhe
yad aṣṭābhir ājyāny aṣṭāśaphāḥ paśavaḥ śaphaśas tat paśūn āpnoti
yat dvādaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāno dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nu prajāyante tān evāvarundhe
yat ṣoḍaśāni pṛṣṭhāni ṣoḍaśa kalāḥ paśavaḥ kalāśas tat paśūn āpnoti
yad viṃśa ārbhavaḥ pāṅktatvam eṣāṃ tad āpnoti
yac caturviṃśo 'gniṣṭomaś caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe
prāṇo gāyatrī prajananaṃ prāṇād eva gāyatryāḥ prajāyate
ekaṃ sāma bahūni chandāṃsi tasmād eko bahūn poṣān puṣyati
ātmā vā agniṣṭomaḥ paśavaś chandāṃsy ātmany eva tat paśūn pratiṣṭhāpayati noktho nāgniṣṭomo na hi grāmyāḥ paśavo nāraṇyāḥ
atha yasya catvāri stotrāṇi catasṛbhiś catvāry aṣṭābhiś catvāri dvādaśabhiś catvāri ṣoḍaśabhiḥ sa gāṃ nātivadati
ṣoḍaśakalāḥ paśavaḥ kalāśas tat paśūn [KSS & BI: praśūn] āpnoti
ukthyaḥ ṣoḍaśimān bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni vajraḥ ṣoḍaśī vajreṇaivāsmai paśūn parigṛhṇāty anapakrāmukā asmāt paśavo bhavanti noktho nātirātro na hi grāmyāḥ paśavo nāraṇyāḥ
asurāṇāṃ vai balas tamasā prāvṛto 'śmāpidhānaś cāsīt tasmin gavyaṃ vasv antar āsīt taṃ devā nāśaknuvan bhettuṃ te bṛhaspatim abruvann imān na utsṛjeti sa udbhidaiva balaṃ vyacyāvayad balabhidābhinat tān utsedhenaivodasṛjan niṣedhena paryagṛhṇāt
paśukāmo yajeta
yad udbhidā yajeta balam evasmai vicyāvayati yad balabhidā balam evāsmai bhinatti
utsedhaniṣedhau brahmasāmanī bhavata utsedhenaivāsmai paśūn utsidhya niṣedhena parigṛhṇāti
''yajña indram avardhayad'' iti brahmaṇa ājyaṃ rūpeṇa samṛddham
saptisaptadaśau bhavato yat saptabhiḥ stuvanti sapta grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ paśūn evāvarūndhe saptapadā śakvarī paśavaḥ śakvarī paśūn evāvarūndhe 'tha yat saptadaśabhiḥ prajāpatir vai saptadaśaḥ prajāpatim evāpnoti
gāyatrīṃ saṃpadyate tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe prāṇo gāyatrī prajananaṃ prāṇād eva gāyatryāḥ prajāyate
athaiṣo 'pacitir apacitikāmo yajetāpacityaivāsmā apacitiṃ vindati
tasya caturviṃśau pavamānau caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī tejasaivāsmai brahmavarcasenāpacitiṃ vindati
ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavata ubhābhyām evāsmai bṛhadrathantarābhyām apacitiṃ vindati
bhargayaśasī bhavato bhargeṇaivāsmai bhargo dadhāti yaśasā yaśaḥ
ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś cobhayair evāsmai stomair apacitiṃ vindati
tad āhur vilomāna stomā īśvarā yajamānaṃ vikṣetor vi hy atiyantīti
ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo 'ntata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati
athaiṣa sarvastomo 'pacitir apacitikāmo yajeta sarvair evāsmai stomair apacitiṃ vindati
virājaṃ saṃpadyata eṣa vā apacito yo 'nnādo 'nnaṃ virāḍ annādyam evāsmin dadhāti
ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavato bhargayaśasī bhavata ubhaye stomāś chandomāś ca pṛṣṭhyāś cobhayair evāsmai stomair apacitiṃ vindati
tasya chandomāḥ pṛṣṭhāni paśavo vai chandomā annaṃ pṛṣṭhāny abhipūrvam evāsminn annādyaṃ paśūn dadhāti yac chandomavāṃs tena dvādaśāhayājinam āpnoti
tad āhur nānālokāḥ stomāś chandomāś ca pṛṣṭhyāś ca yad ekasmin yajñakratau samavarudhyanta īśvaro [corr. Caland; BI & KSS īśvarā] yajamāno 'pratiṣṭhātor iti
ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomo bhavati pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhām eva tad abhyāyanti
pakṣī vā eṣa stomaḥ
pakṣy eṣa nidhīyate
na vā apakṣaḥ pakṣiṇam āpnoty atha yad eṣa pakṣy apakṣiṇi nidhīyate tasmāt pakṣiṇaḥ pakṣaiḥ patanti
pakṣī jyotiṣmān puṇyān lokān saṃcarati ya evaṃ veda
trivṛtāv abhito bhavatas tejo brahmavarcasaṃ trivṛt teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe
atha pañcadaśau vīryaṃ vai pañcadaśo vīryam evāvarundhe
atha saptadaśau paśavo vai saptadaśaḥ paśūn evāvarundhe
athaikaviṃśau pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo madhyata eva yajñasya pratitiṣṭhati
atha triṇavāv ime vai lokās triṇava eṣv eva lokeṣu pratitiṣṭhati
atha trayastriṃśo varṣma vai trayastriṃśaḥ
varṣma svānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
eṣa vāva bradhnasya viṣṭapo yad etau trayastriṃśau madhyataḥ saṃdhīyete tena bradhnasya viṣṭapam ārohati
madhyato vā agnir variṣṭhas tasmād ete stomā madhyato variṣṭhāḥ kriyante
trivṛtā praiti trivṛtodeti prāṇo vai trivṛt prāṇenaiva praiti prāṇam abhyudeti
athaiṣa jyotiḥ
tasya trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni caturviṃśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni
prāṇo vai trivṛd ātmā pañcadaśaḥ
mukhaṃ gāyatry annaṃ vai saptadaśo mukhata eva tad annaṃ dhatte
annam atty annādo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
mādhyandinena vai pavamānena devāḥ svargaṃ lokam āyan yad eṣa caturviṃśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāno bhavati svargasya lokasyākrāntyai caturviṃśatyakṣarā gāyatrī tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatrī teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe prāṇo gāyatrī prajananaṃ prāṇād eva gāyatryāḥ prajāyate
ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate
pakṣi vā etac chandaḥ pakṣī jyotiṣmān puṇyān lokān saṃcarati ya evaṃ veda
madhyato vā agnir variṣṭhas tasmād ete stomā madhyato variṣṭhāḥ kriyante
ekā saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyata ekākinam evainam annādyasyādhyakṣaṃ karoti
jyotir vā eṣo 'gniṣṭomo jyotiṣmantaṃ puṇyaṃ lokaṃ jayati ya evaṃ vidvān etena yajate
athaiṣa ṛṣabhaḥ
ṛṣabho vā eṣa stomānām ṛṣabhatāṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
rājanyaṃ yājayed ṛṣabho vai paśūnām adhipatī rājanyo manuṣyāṇām
yo vā asti so 'dhipatiḥ
adhipatiḥ samānānāṃ bhavati ya evaṃ veda
tasya sadoviśīyaṃ mādhyandine pavamāne bhavati viśam evāsmai savanābhyāṃ parigṛhṇāty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati
samantaṃ bhavati samantām evāsmai viśaṃ karoty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati
ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavata iyaṃ vai rathantaraṃ dyaur bṛhadevāsmāl lokād gāyatry evāmuṣmād ubhayor anayor lokayoḥ pratitiṣṭhati
anuṣṭubhi bṛhad bhavaty anto vā anuṣṭup chandasām anto bṛhat sāmnām anto rājanyo manuṣyāṇām anta eva tad antaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati tasmād yo rājanyānāṃ hīyate na sa punaragraṃ paryeti
yo vai vājapeyaḥ sa rājasūyo yo rājasūyaḥ sa varūṇasavo 'thaiṣa gosavaḥ svārājyo vā eṣa yajñaḥ
svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
prajāpatir hi svārājyaṃ parameṣṭhī svārājyam
parameṣṭhitāṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
ubhe bṛhadrathantare bhavatas tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
ayutaṃ dakṣiṇās tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
pratiduhābhiṣicyate tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
bṛhataḥ stotra pratyabhiṣicyate tad dhi svārājyaṃ svārājyaṃ gacchati ya evaṃ veda
anuddhate dakṣiṇata āhavanīyasyābhiṣicyate 'syām evānantarhite 'dhy abhiṣicyate
sarvaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśastena gosavaḥ
athaiṣa marutstoma etena vai maruto 'parimitāṃ puṣṭim apuṣyann aparimitāṃ puṣṭiṃ puṣyati ya evaṃ veda
yad gaṇaśaḥ stomās tena marutstomo gaṇaśo hi marutaḥ
etenaiva trīn yājayet
yat trīṇi trivṛnti stotrāṇi bhavanti nānā brahmavarcase pratitiṣṭhanti
yat trīṇi pañcadaśāni nānā vīrye
yat trīṇi saptadaśāni nānā paśuṣu
yat trīṇy ekaviṃśāni nānā pratitiṣṭhanti
pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
athaiṣa indrāgnyoḥ kulāyaḥ prajākāmo vā paśukāmo vā yajeta prajā vai kulāyaṃ paśavaḥ kulāyaṃ gṛhāḥ kulāyaṃ kulāyam eva bhavati
etenaiva dvau yājayet
yat ṣaṭ trivṛnti stotrāṇi bhavanti nānā brahmavarcase pratitiṣṭhato yat dve pañcadaśe nānā vīrye yat dve saptadaśe nānā paśuṣu yat dve ekaviṃśe nānā pratitiṣṭhataḥ pratitiṣṭhati ya evaṃ veda
athaiṣa pañcadaśa indrastoma ukthyaḥ
etena vā indro 'ty anyā devatā abhavad aty anyāḥ prajā bhavati ya evaṃ veda
rājanyaṃ yājayet
sarvaḥ pañcadaśo bhavaty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśa ojasaivainaṃ vīryeṇa samardhayati
aindrīṣu bhavantīndriyeṇaivainaṃ vīryeṇa samardhayati
ukthyo bhavati paśavo vā ukthāni viḍ ukthāni viśam evāsmai paśūn anuniyunakty anapakrāmukāsmād viḍ bhavati
pañcadaśa stotrāṇi pañcadaśāni bhavanty ojo vīryaṃ pañcadaśo 'bhipūrvam evāsminn ojo vīryaṃ dadhāti
athaiṣa indrāgnyoḥ stoma etena vā indrāgnī aty anyā devatā abhavatām aty anyāḥ prajā bhavati ya evaṃ veda
trivṛt pañcadaśo bhavati
brahma vai trivṛt kṣatraṃ pañcadaśo brahmaṇa iva cāsya kṣatrasyeva ca prakāśo bhavati ya evaṃ veda
rājā ca purohitaś ca yajeyātām
gāyatrīṃ ca jagatīṃ ca saṃpadyate
tejo brahmavarcasaṃ gāyatryā brāhmaṇo 'varundhe viśaṃ rājā jagatyā praviśati
purodhākāmo yajeta
bṛhaspatir akāmayata devānāṃ purodhāṃ gaccheyam iti sa etenāyajata sa devānāṃ purodhām agacchad gacchati purodhāṃ ya evaṃ veda
athaiṣa vighanaḥ
indro 'kāmayata pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ vihanyām iti sa etaṃ vighanam apaśyat tena pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ vyahan vi pāpmānaṃ bhrātṛvyaṃ hate ya evaṃ veda
yat trivṛd bhavati prāṇāṃs tenāvarundhe yat dvādaśaḥ saṃvatsaraṃ tena yat pañcadaśo vīryaṃ tena yat saptadaśo 'nnādyaṃ tena yad ekaviṃśaḥ pratiṣṭhā tena yan navadaśaḥ prajananaṃ tena yac caturviṃśo brahmavarcasaṃ tena yat triṇavo vajraṃ bhrātṛvyāya praharati
paśukāmo yajeta bṛhatīṃ saṃpadyate paśavo vai bṛhatī paśūn evāvarundhe
ṣaḍ etā bṛhatyo bhavanti ṣaḍ ṛtavaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ saṃvatsaraṃ paśavo 'nu prajāyante tān evāptvāvarundhe
indram adevyo māyā ayacanta sa prajāpatim upādhāvavat tasmā etaṃ vighanaṃ prāyacchat tena sarvā mṛdho vyahata yad vyahata tad vighanasya vighanatvam
sarvā mṛdho vihate ya evaṃ vidvān vighanena yajate yam evaṃ vidvān vighanena yājayati
paśukāmo yajeta paśavo vai bṛhatī paśuṣv eva pratitiṣṭhati
trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni pañcadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni saptadaśa ārbhava ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ sokthyaḥ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
jyotiṣṭomenātirātreṇarddhikāmo yajetābhikramo vā eṣa stomānām abhikrāntyā abhikrāntena hi yajñasyardhnoti
eṣo 'gniṣṭoma eṣa ukthya eṣo 'tirātro 'gniṣṭomena vai devā imaṃ lokam abhyajayann ukthyair antarikṣaṃ rātryāmuṃ lokam ajayann ahorātrābhyām abhyavartanta
parācyo vā anyā vyucchanti pratīcyo 'nyā eṣā vāva pratīcī vyucchati yāśvinena vyucchati pratīcīr evāsmā uṣaso vivāsayati
dve saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyete eṣā vai stanavatī virāṭ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etāṃ dugdhe
trivṛtā praiti trivṛtodeti prāṇo vai trivṛt prāṇenaiva praiti prāṇam abhyudeti
trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭhāni triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
sarvastomenātirātreṇa bubhūṣan yajeta sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati
yat trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavati tat trivṛtaṃ stomam āpnoti gāyatrīṃ chando yat pañcadaśāny ājyāni tat pañcadaśaṃ stomam āpnoti triṣṭubhaṃ chando yat saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānas tat saptadaśaṃ stomam āpnoti jagatīṃ chando yad ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭāni tad ekaviṃśaṃ stomam āpnoty anuṣṭubhaṃ chando yat triṇava ārbhavas tat triṇavaṃ stomam āpnoti paṅktiṃ chando yat trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomas tat trayastriṃśaṃ stomam āpnoti virājaṃ chando yad uṣṇikkakubhau kriyete tad uṣṇikkakubhāv āpnoti yad āśvinaṃ śasyate tat sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati
prāñcaṃ vai trayastriṃśo yajñaṃ prabhujati tam adhvaryur ekādaśinyā purastāt pratyudyacchaty ekādaśa raśanā ekādaśa paśava ekādaśa yūpā bhavanti tat trayastriṃśe trayastriṃśaṃ pratiṣṭhāpayati
tayā samudyatayā rātryā yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate taṃ tam abhyaśnute yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate taṃ tam abhyaśnute ya evaṃ veda
trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ chandomā itarāṇi triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamam athaikaviṃśam atha saptadaśam ekaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśī pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhis trivṛt prathamam atiriktastotram atha pañcadaśam atha saptadaśam athaikaviṃśam
prajāpatiḥ paśūn asṛjata te 'smāt sṛṣṭā apākrāmaṃs tān agniṣṭomena nāpnot tān ukthair nāpnot tān ṣoḍaśinā nāpnot tān rātryā nāpnot tān sandhinā nāpnot tān āśvinena nāpnot tān agnim abravīd imān ma īpseti tān agnis trivṛtā stomena jarābodhīyena sāmnā nāpnot tān indram abravīd imān ma īpseti tān indraḥ pañcadaśena stomena sattrāsāhīyena sāmnā nāpnot tān viśvān devān abravīd imān ma ipsateti tān viśve devāḥ saptadaśena stomena mārgīṃyaveṇa sāmnā nāpnuvaṃs tān viṣṇum abravīd imān ma īpseti tān viṣṇur ekaviṃśena stomenāpnod vāravantīyenāvārayatedaṃ viṣṇur vicakrama iti vyakramata
yasmāt pra preva paśavo bhraṃśeran sa etena yajeta
etena vai devā jaitvāni jitvā yaṃ yaṃ kāmam akāmayanta taṃ tam āpnuvan yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etenāpnoti
tad aptoryāmno 'ptoryāmatvam
trivṛd bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ navasaptadaśāni stotrāṇy ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ sokthaḥ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
navasaptadaśenātirātreṇa prajākāmo yajeta nava vai prāṇāḥ prajāpatiḥ saptadaśaḥ prāṇebhya eva tad adhi prajāpateḥ prajāḥ prajāyante
kakubhaṃ prācīm udūhati puruṣo vai kakup garbho vā eṣa madhyato dhīyate
tasyāṃ sākamaśvam
prajāpatiḥ prajā asṛjata tā na prājāyanta sa etat sāmāpaśyat tā aśvo bhūtvābhyajighrat tāḥ prājāyanta prajananaṃ vā etat sāma
prajāyate bahur bhavati ya evaṃ veda
dvipadāṃ kakubho loke karoti garbham eva taddhitaṃ madhyataḥ prajanayati
atirātro bhavaty ahorātre vā anu prajāḥ prajāyante 'horātre evānu prajayā paśubhiḥ prajāyate
trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni pañcadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ saptadaśāni pṛṣṭhāni saptadaśa ārbhava ekaviṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ saptadaśāny ukthāni pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
viṣuvatātirātreṇa jyeṣṭhaṃ jyaiṣṭhineyaṃ yājayed viṣuvān vā eṣa stomānāṃ viṣuvān eva bhavati yad eka ekaviṃśo bhavaty ekaviṃśo vā ito 'sāv āditya dvādaśa māsāḥ pañcartavas traya ime lokā
asāv āditya ekaviṃśa ādityasyaivainaṃ mātrāṃ gamayati
eṣa vā udeti na vā enam anyat jyotiṣāṃ jyotiḥ pratyudeti
nainam anyaḥ sveṣu pratyudeti ya evaṃ veda
pañcadaśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ trivṛnty ājyāni saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ sokthaṃ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir goṣṭomenātirātreṇa bhrātṛvyavān yajeta gavā vai devā asurān ebhyo lokebhyo 'nudanta rātryānapajayyam ajayann ebhyo lokebhyo bhrātṛvyaṃ praṇudya rātryānapajayyaṃ jayati
trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ sokthaṃ pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir āyuṣṭomenātirātreṇa svargakāmo yajetordhvāḥ stomā yanty anapabhraṃśāya yad atirātro bhavaty ahorātrābhyām eva svargaṃ lokam eti
trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ saptadaśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya pañcadaśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ saptadaśam acchāvākasyaikaviṃśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamānaḥ saptadaśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭham ekaviṃśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya triṇavaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsina ekaviṃśam acchāvakasya triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhir abhijitātirātreṇa bhrātṛvyavān yajetābhijitā vai devā asurān imān lokān abhyajayat rātryānapajayyam ajayann abhijitaiva bhrātṛvyam imān lokān abhijitya rātryānapajayyaṃ jayati
trivṛt bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañcadaśaṃ hotur ājyaṃ saptadaśaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyaikaviṃśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ pañcadaśam acchāvākasya saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśaṃ hotuḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ triṇavaṃ maitrāvaruṇasya
saptadaśaṃ brāhmaṇācchaṃsina ekaviṃśam acchāvākasya triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamaṃ dve ekaviṃśe saṣoḍaśike pañcadaśī rātriḥ trivṛt sandhir viśvajitātirātreṇa paśukāmo yajeta
reto hi nābhānediṣṭhīyaṃ paśavo vālakhilyā yan nābhānediṣṭhīyaṃ pūrvaṃ śasyata uttarā vālakhilyā retasas tat paśavaḥ prajāyante rūpāṇi vikaroti yad vārṣākapam ṛtuṣu pratitiṣṭhati yad evayāmarut
trivṛt ātirātreṇa brahmavarcasakāmo yajeta tejo vai trivṛt brahmavarcasaṃ teja eva brahmavarcasam avarundhe tejasi brahmavarcase pratitiṣṭhati pañcadaśenātirātreṇa vīryakāmo yajetaujo vīryaṃ pañcadaśa oja eva vīryam avarundha ojasi vīrye pratitiṣṭhati saptadaśenātirācreṇānnādyakāmo yajetānnaṃ vai saptadaśo 'nnādyam evāvarundha ekaviṃśenātirātreṇa pratiṣṭhākāmo yajeta pratiṣṭhā vā ekaviṃśo yad atirātro bhavaty ahorātrayor eva pratitiṣṭhati
jyotiṣṭomo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahaḥ sarvastomo 'tirātra uttaram
tasya caturviṃśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ pañadaśāny ājyāni saptadaśo mādhyandinaḥ pavamāna ekaviṃśāni pṛṣṭhāni triṇava ārbhavas trayastriṃśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pratyavarohīṇy ukthāni triṇavaṃ prathamam athaikaviṃśam atha saptadaśam ekaviṃśaḥ ṣoḍaśī pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
aṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs teṣāṃ haviṣmāṃś ca haviṣkṛc cāṅgirasāv ahīyetā tāv āgacchetāṃ yato 'ṅgirasaḥ svargaṃ lokam āyaṃs tāv atapyetāṃ tāv ete sāmanī apaśyatāṃ tābhyāṃ dvirātram atanvātāṃ tena svargaṃ lokam aitām
yaḥ pauṇyo hīna iva syāt sa etena yajetāpnoti pūrveṣāṃ prahām āpnutāṃ hi tāv aṅgirasaḥ
prajākāmo yajeta dvitīyaṃ hy etad yat prajāḥ
svargakāmo yajeta dvitīyād dhi lokāt paro loko 'bhiprakramyo durādho dvirātra ity āhur yad agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavaty ukthyam antaryanti yady ukthyo 'gniṣṭomam
yaj jyotir ukthyaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavati nāgniṣṭomam antaryanti nokthāni
tad āhur eṣā vāva yajñasya mātrā yad agniṣṭomo yad agniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavati yajñasya mātrāṃ nātikrāmaty athottarasyāhna ukthebhyo 'dhi rātrim upayanti tenokthāny anantaritāni
caturviṃśaṃ bahiṣpavamānaṃ bhavaty uttarasyāhnaś caturviṃśaty akṣarā gāyatrī prajananaṃ gāyatrī prajātyai
ubhaye stomā yugmantaś cāyujaś ca tan mithunaṃ tasmān mithunāt prajāyate
sarvastomo 'tirātro bhavati sarvasyāptyai sarvasya jityai sarvam evaitenāpnoti sarvaṃ jayati
atha yasya jyotir ukthyaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavaty āyur atirātra uttaram
tisraḥ pūrvasyāhno virājam atiricyante dvābhyām uttaram ahar virāja ūnam ūnātiriktaṃ vā anuprajāḥ prajāyante
pra prajayā pra paśubhir jāyate ya evaṃ veda
ekā saṃstutānāṃ virājam atiricyate ekākinam evainam annādyasyādhyakṣaṃ karoti
etena vai citrarathaṃ kāpeyā ayājayaṃs tam ekākinam annādyasyādhyakṣam akurvaṃs tasmāc caitrarathīnām ekaḥ kṣatrapatir jāyate 'nulamba iva dvitīyaḥ
atha yasya trivṛt pañcadaśo 'gniṣṭomaḥ pūrvam ahar bhavaty āyur atirātra uttaram
mithunābhyāṃ stomābhyām uttaram ahaḥ prajanayanti tat prajātaṃ śva ārabhante cakre vā ete sākaṃvṛtī yat trivṛt pañcadaśau stomau yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate tam etenābhyaśnute yatra yatra hi cakrīvatā kāmayate tat tad abhyaśnute
atha yad āyur atirātro bhavati pratiṣṭhityai
etena vai kapivano bhauvāyana iṣṭvārūkṣatām agacchat
arūkṣo bhavati ya evaṃ vidvān etena yajate
trivṛt prātaḥsavanaṃ pañcadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ saptadaśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ pañcadaśaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ saptadaśaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanaṃ soktham ekaviṃśaṃ prātaḥsavanaṃ triṇavaṃ mādhyandinaṃ savanaṃ trayastriṃśa ārbhavaś catustriṃśo 'gniṣṭoma ekaviṃśāny ukthāni saṣoḍaśikāni ṣoḍaśaṃ prathamaṃ rātriṣāma pañcadaśī rātris trivṛt sandhiḥ
prajāpatir vā idam eka āsīt tasya vāg eva svam āsīd vāg dvitīyā sa aikṣatemām eva vācaṃ visṛjā iyaṃ vā idaṃ sarvaṃ vibhavanty eṣyatīti sa vācaṃ vyasṛjata sedaṃ sarvaṃ vibhavanty ait sordhvodātanod yathāpāṃ dhārā santataivaṃ tasyā eti tṛtīyam acchinat tad bhūmir abhavad abhūd iva vā idam iti tad bhūmer bhūmitvaṃ keti tṛtīyam acchinat tad antarikṣam abhavad antar eva vā idam iti tad antarikṣasyāntarikṣatvaṃ ho iti tṛtīyam ūrdhvam udāsyat tat dyaur abhavad adyutad iva vā iti tad divo divatvam
eṣā vāva pratyakṣaṃ vāg yaj jihvāgreṇaitad vāco vadati yad eti madhyenaitad vāco vadati yat keti sarvayaitad vāco raso 'dhyūrdhva udvad ati yaddho iti
yad etāni rūpāṇy anvahaṃ vyajyante mukhata eva tad vācaṃ visṛjante mukhato yajñiyaṃ karma
prajāpatir vā idam ekākṣarāṃ vācaṃ satīṃ tredhā vyakarot ta ime lokā abhavan rūkṣā anupajīvanāḥ sa aikṣata katham ime lokā loma gṛhṇīyuḥ katham upajīvanīyāḥ syur iti sa etaṃ trirātram apaśyat tam āharat tenemān lokān anvātanot tato vā ime lokā lomāgṛhṇaṃs tata upajīvanīyā abhavaṃs trirātrasya vā idaṃ puṣṭaṃ trirātrasyodaraṇaṃ yad idam eṣu lokeṣv adhi
gacchati paśūnāṃ bhūmānaṃ dvipadāṃ catuṣpadāṃ ya evaṃ veda
prajāpatir yad vācaṃ vyasṛjata sākṣarad eveti prathamaṃ kṣeti dvitīyaṃ reti tṛtīyaṃ yena yena vai rūpeṇa prajāpatir vācaṃ vyasṛjata tena tena rūpeṇājyāni cārabhyante 'hāni cāpyante
tad āhur brahmavādino 'kṣarestho vai trirātra ity ekākṣarā vai vāk tryakṣaram akṣaraṃ tryakṣaraḥ puruṣaḥ sa vā enaṃ vedety āhur ya enaṃ puruṣasammitaṃ vedeti
etena vai devā eṣu lokeṣv ārdhnuvann etena svargaṃ lokamāyan
vāg vai trirātro vāco rūpeṇājyāni cāhāni ca vibhajyanta ekākṣarā vai vāk tryakṣaram akṣaram akṣarasya rūpeṇa vibhajyante trayo gandharvās teṣām eṣā bhaktir agneḥ pṛthivī vāyor antarikṣam asāv ādityasya dyaus trayo gharmāsa uṣasaṃ sacante
agnir uṣasaṃ sacate vāyur uṣasaṃ sacate 'sāv āditya uṣasaṃ sacate
trīṇi mithunāni tāny eṣaḥ
mithunaṃ dve sambhavato mithunād yat prajāyate tat tṛtīyam
indro vṛtrāya vajram udayacchat so 'bravīn mā me praharṣīr asti vā idaṃ mayi vīryaṃ tat te pradāsyāmīti tad asmai prāyacchat tad viṣṇuḥ pratyagṛhṇāt sa dvitīyaṃ sa tṛtīyam udayacchat sa evābravīn mā me prahārṣīr asti vā idaṃ mayi vīryaṃ tat te pradāsyāmīti tad asmai prāyacchat tad viṣṇuḥ pratyagṛhṇād etad vāca tad abhyanūcyate
